	Ia5-Li7-Bi2 (24)
[1]	Pian7-nga2-bin2 toe7, A-na2-tut8 siaN5 e5 che3-si tiong, Hi-lek8-ka e5 kiaN2, Ia5-li7-bi2 e5 oe7 ki3 ti7 e7-toe2.  2). Tng Iu5-tai7 ong5 A-bun5 e5 kiaN2 Iok-se-a che7-ui7 e5 chap8-saN--ni5, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 i.  3). Koh ti7 Iu5-tai7 ong5 Iok-se-a e5 kiaN2 Iok-nga2-keng3 che7-ui7 e5 si5, tit8-kau3 Iu5-tai7 ong5 Iok-se-a e5 kiaN2 Se-ti2-ka chap8-it--ni5 e5 lou7-be2; gou7-geh8 kan, Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 lang5 siu7-liah8 e5 si5, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 i.
	4). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 goa2, kong2,  5). Goa2 be7 chhong3-cho7 li2 ti7 pak-tou2-lai7 e5 tai7-seng, Goa2 bat li2; li2 be7 chhut-thai e5 tai7-seng, Goa2 hun-piat li2 choe3-seng3; siat-lip8 li2 choe3 liat8-kok e5 sian-ti.  6). Goa2 chiu7 kong2, Hai7--ah! Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, li2 khoaN3, goa2 boe7 hiau2 kong2, in-ui7 goa2 si7 gin2-na2.  7). Chong2-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 goa2 kong2, Li2 m7-thang kong2, Goa2 si7 gin2-na2; in-ui7 Goa2 kiN3-u7 chhe li2, li2 tioh8 khi3; Goa2 kiN3-u7 hoan-hu3 li2, li2 tioh8 kong2.  8). Li2 boh8-tit kiaN--in, in-ui7 Goa2 kap li2 ti7-teh, beh kiu3 li2; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2 e5.  9). Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 chhun I e5 chhiu2 bong goa2 e5 chhui3.  Ia5-ho5-hoa ka7 goa2 kong2, Li2 khoaN3, Goa2 u7 chiong Goa2 e5 oe7, he7 ti7 li2 e5 chhui3.  10). KhoaN3 ah, kin-a2-jit8 Goa2 siat-lip8 li2 ti7 liat8-pang liat8-kok e5 teng2-bin7; si7 ui7-tioh8 beh puih8-chhut, beh thiah-hui2, beh pai7-hoai7, beh chhia-to2, beh kian3-lip8, beh chai-poe5.
	11). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 koh lim5-kau3 goa2, kong2, Ia5-li7-bi2 ah, li2 khoaN3-kiN3 sim2-mih8? Goa2 kong2, Goa2 khoaN3-kiN3 heng7-chhiu7 e5 chit8-ki.  12). Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 tui3 goa2 kong2, Li2 sou2 khoaN3 si7 tioh8; Goa2 teh koan-kou3 Goa2 e5 oe7 lai5 chiaN5--i.  13). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 te7-ji7 pai2 lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2, Li2 khoaN3-kiN3 sim2-mih8? Goa2 kong2, Goa2 khoaN3-kiN3 chit8 e5 tiaN2 teh kun2, i e5 bin7 tui3 pak--si3 ng3 ke3--lai5.  14). Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 tui3 goa2 kong2, Beh u7 chai-e7 tui3 pak-hng hoat-chhut, lim5-kau3 chit sou2-chai7 it-chhe3 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3.  15). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh tiau3 pak-hng liat8-kok e5 cheng3-chok8; in beh lai5, tak8-e5 an cho7-ui7 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 chiah e5 siaN5-mng5-khau2; chiu-ui5 kong-kek siaN5-chhiuN5, iah8 beh kong-kek Iu5-tai7 it-chhe3 e5 siaN5.  16). Lun7-kau3 chit e5 peh-siN3 it-chhe3 e5 phaiN2, chiu7-si7 li7-khui Goa2, ng3 pat8 e5 siong7-te3 sio-hiuN; kui7-pai3 in e5 chhiu2 sou2 choe3--e5; Goa2 beh kong2-khi2 Goa2 e5 phoaN3-toan3 lai5 kong-kek in.  17). Sou2-i2 li2 tioh8 ha5-io, khi2--lai5, chiong Goa2 sou2 hoan-hu3 li2 it-chhe3 e5 oe7 ka7 in kong2; boh8-tit in-ui7 in lai5 kiaN-hiaN5, kiaN-liau2 Goa2 hou7 li2 ti7 in e5 bin7-cheng5 lai5 kiaN-hiaN5.  18). KhoaN3 ah, in-ui7 Goa2 kin-a2-jit8 hou7 li2 chiaN5-choe3 kian-kou3 e5 siaN5, choe3 thih-thiau7, choe3 tang5-chhiuN5, lai5 ti2-tng choan5-toe7, i2-kip8 Iu5-tai7 e5 liat8-ong5, kui3-chok8, che3-si, kap chit sou2-chai7 e5 cheng3 peh-siN3.  19). In beh kong-kek li2, chong2-si7 boe7-oe7 iaN5 li2; in-ui7 Goa2 kap li2 ti7-teh, beh chin2-kiu3 li2; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.

[2]	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 koh lim5-kau3 goa2, kong2,  2). Li2 khi3 ng3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 lang5 e5 hi7-khang kio3 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Li2 siau3-lian5 e5 un-ai3, hun-in e5 ai3-cheng5, li2 chaiN2-a2-iuN7 ti7 khong3-ia2, ti7 be7-bat cheng3-choh e5 toe7, kun-te3 Goa2; Goa2 long2 ka7 li2 ki3-tit.  3). Hit-si5 I2-sek-liat8 choe3-seng3 kui Ia5-ho5-hoa; choe3 I khi2-khau5 sek8 e5 thou2-san2; kiN3-na7 thun-chiah8 i--e5, beh sng3 choe3 u7 choe7; chai-e7 beh lim5-kau3 in; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	4). Nga2-kok e5 ke ah, I2-sek-liat8 ke e5 tak8 pang5-thau5 ah, lin2 tioh8 thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7.  5). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Lin2 e5 liat8-chou2 khoaN3 Goa2 u7 sim2-mih8 put-gi7, keng2-jian5 li7-khui Goa2 hng7-hng7, khi3 than3 hiah e5 hu-ke2--e5, lai5 choe3 hu-ke2--e5 ah?  6). In iah8 bo5 kong2, Hit e5 chhoa7 lan2 chhut Ai-kip8 toe7 e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 toh-loh8? I si7 chhoa7 lan2 keng-ke3 khong3-ia2, soa-bou5, kap chhim-khiN e5 sou2-chai7, khong3-han7 si2-im3 e5 toe7; bo5 lang5 keng-ke3, bo5 lang5 khia7-khi2 e5 keng2-kai3.  7). Goa2 chhoa7 lin2 jip8 pui5 e5 toe7, hou7 lin2 chiah8 hit tiong-kan e5 ke2-chi2 kap ho2-mih8; chong2-si7 lin2 jip8-lai5-liau2, chiu7 phah la5-sam5 Goa2 e5 toe7; hou7 Goa2 e5 san2-giap8 chiaN5-choe3 kho2-ouN3--e5.  8). Che3-si long2 bo5 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 toh-loh8 leh? kang2-kai2 lut8-hoat--e5 m7-bat Goa2, koaN-tiuN2 poe7-biu7 Goa2, sian-ti kho3 Pa-lek8 lai5 chham3-gu2, koh than3 bo5 li7-ek e5 su7.
	9). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 in-ui7 an2-ni beh kap lin2 cheng-pian7; iah8 beh kap lin2 e5 kiaN2-kiaN2 sun-sun cheng-pian7.  10). Lin2 tioh8 ke3-khi3 Ki-the5 chiah e5 hai2-su7 lai5 koan-khoaN3, chhe lang5 khi3 Ki-tat8 liu5-sim cha-kho2; khoaN3 bat u7 chit-ho7 su7 a2-bo5.  11). Kiam2 u7 chit8-kok koe2-oaN7 in e5 siong7-te3 mah? ki5-sit8 hiah-e5 m7-si7 Siong7-te3; chong2-si7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 chiong in e5 eng5-kng lai5 oaN7 hit-e5 bo5 li7-ek--e5.  12). Chiah e5 thiN ah, tioh8 in-ui7 chit-e5 lai5 gong5-ngiah8, kek8-ki5 kiaN-hiaN5, chin7-chai7 leng2-cheng7; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  13). In-ui7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 choe3 nng7-hang7 phaiN2-tai7, chiu7-si7 Goa2 choe3 oah8-chui2 e5 goan5-thau5, in li7-khui Goa2; koh ui7 ka-ki7 khui ti5, si7 phoa3-lih8 boe7 toe2 chui2 e5 ti5.
	14). I2-sek-liat8 si7 lou5-pok8 mah? Si7 ke-tiong siN e5 lou5-pok8 mah? Ui7-ho5 chiaN5-choe3 siu7 chhiuN2 e5 mih8 ah?  15). Iong2 e5 sai ng3 i hm7-hm7-hau2, chhut toa7-siaN, hou7 i e5 toe7 pha-hng; siaN5 iah8 long2 sio-hui2, bo5 lang5 khia7-khi2.  16). Lo5-hut lang5 kap Tap-pi2-lek8 lang5 iah8 phah-chhui3 li2 e5 thau5-khak-teng2.  17). Chit e5 su7 kiam2-m7-si7 li2 ka-ki7 chhu2--e5 mah? in-ui7 li2 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhoa7 li2 kiaN5-lou7 e5 si5, li2 u7 khi3-sak I.  18). TaN li2 siaN2-su7 ti7 Ai-kip8 e5 lou7, si7 beh lim Se-hat e5 chui2 mah? li2 siaN2-su7 ti7 A-sut8 e5 lou7, si7 beh lim Toa7-ho5 e5 chui2 mah?  19). Li2 ka-ki7 e5 phaiN2 beh keng2-kai3 li2; li2 poe7-gek8 e5 su7 beh chek-pi7 li2; tui3 an2-ni thang chai, thang khoaN3-chhut li2 khi3-sak li2 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa, bo5 chun5 keng3-ui3 Goa2 e5 sim, chiu7-si7 phaiN2 koh kan-khou2 e5 su7; che si7 Chu2 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	20). Goa2 ti7 kou2-cha2 e5 si5, at-chih8 li2 e5 taN, thau2-khui li2 e5 soh; li2 kong2, Goa2 m7 sun7-hok8; in-ui7 li2 ti7 tak8 e5 koaiN5-soaN-teng2, tak8 chang5 chhiN-chhui3 e5 chhiu7-kha, khut-loh8 sin-khu kiaN5-im5.  21). Na7-si7 Goa2 bat chai-cheng3 li2, si7 siong7-teng2 e5 phu5-to5-chhiu7, choan5-jian5 si7 chin e5 cheng2-chi2; li2 tui3-ti7 Goa2 chaiN2-iuN7 piN3-choe3 pat8-khoan2 phu5-to5-chhiu7 e5 phaiN2-ki ah?  22). Li2 sui-bong2 eng7 kiN, eng7 choe7-choe7 soat-bun5 lai5 soe2, li2 e5 choe7-ok e5 hun5-jiah iu5-goan5 hian2-chhut ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  23). Li2 thai2-tho2 oe7 kong2, Goa2 bo5 bak--tioh8 la5-sam5, bo5 te3 chiah e5 Pa-lek8 ah? li2 khoaN3, li2 soaN-kok-tiong e5 lou7, chiu7 chai li2 sou2 kiaN5--e5 chaiN2-iuN7; li2 si7 toaN-nia7 gau5 chau2 e5 lok8-to5, chau2-lai5 chau2-khi3.  24). Li2 si7 ia2-lu5, koaiN3-si3 ti7 khong3-ia2; iok8-sim hoat-tong7, chiu7 khip-hong; siau2 e5 si5, chi7-chui7 oe7 chou2-chi2 i ah? kiN3-na7 chhe7 i e5, m7-bian2 tioh8-boa5; ti7 i hit-geh8, tek-khak oe7 chhe7--tioh8.  25). Li2 tioh8 kim3-chi2 li2 e5 kha, bian2-ti3 bo5 oe5; kim3-chi2 li2 e5 na5-au5, bian2-ti3 chhui3-ta; chong2-si7 li2 kong2, Che si7 bo5 chhai2-kang, m7--ah; goa2 i2-keng loan5-bou7 pat8-e5; goa2 beh te3 in.  26). Chhat8 hou7 lang5 liah8--tioh8, chaiN2-iuN7 kian3-siau3, I2-sek-liat8 ke kap in e5 kun-ong5, kui3-chok8, che3-si, sian-ti, iah8 long2 an2-ni kian3-siau3.  27). In tui3 chha5-thau5 kong2, Li2 si7 goa2 e5 pe7; tui3 chioh8-thau5 kong2, Li2 si7 siN-goa2-e5.  In eng7 ka-chiah ng3 Goa2, bo5 eng7 bin7 ng3 Goa2; kau3 tu2-tioh8 hoan7-lan7 e5 si5, chiah kong2, Khi2--lai5, lai5 kiu3 goan2.  28). Li2 ui7 ka-ki7 sou2 cho7 e5 siong7-te3 ti7 toh-loh8? i na7 oe7 kiu3 li2, ti7 li2 tu2-tioh8 hoan7-lan7 e5 si5, chiu7 tioh8 khi2-lai5 kiu3 li2; Iu5-tai7 ah, li2 e5 siong7-te3 e5 siau3-giah8 kap li2 e5 siaN5 e5 siau3-giah8 piN5-piN5 choe7.
	29). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Lin2 siaN2-su7 kap Goa2 cheng-pian7? lin2 long2 poe7-gek8 Goa2.  30). Goa2 tok-chek lin2 e5 kiaN2-ji5, si7 khang-khang; in bo5 siu7 keng2-kai3.  Lin2 e5 to, chhin-chhiuN7 beng2 sai, thun-ka7 lin2 e5 sian-ti.  31). Chit se3-tai7 ah, lin2 tioh8 beng5 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7; Goa2 tui3-ti7 I2-sek-liat8 kiam2 bat choe3 chhin-chhiuN7 khong3-ia2, a2-si7 bat choe3 chhin-chhiuN7 ou-am3 e5 toe7 ah? Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 siaN2-su7 kong2, Goan2 thoat-li7 iok-sok, m7 koh kui-ng3 Li2 lah?  32). Chai7-sek-lu2 kiam2 oe7 boe7-ki3-tit i e5 chng-thaN7 mah? sin-niu5 kiam2 oe7 boe7-ki3-tit i e5 sui2-saN? chong2-si7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 boe7-ki3-tit Goa2 boe7 sng3-tit jit8.  33). Li2 chaiN2-iuN7 siu-cheng2 li2 e5 lou7, iau-kiu5 thiong2-ai3; lian5 phaiN2 hu7-jin5-lang5, li2 iah8 eng7 li2 e5 lou7 ka3-si7 in.  34). Koh li2 e5 saN-a2-ku u7 bo5-choe7 e5 song3-hiong lang5 e5 huih; m7-si7 ti7 iah chhu3-khang e5 sou2-chai7 tu2-tioh8, si7 ti7 tak8 sou2-chai7 long2 u7.  35). Li2 iau2-ku2 kong2, Goa2 bo5 choe7; Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 siu7-khi3 tek-khak oat8-tng2 li7-khui goa2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh sim2-mng7 li2, in-ui7 li2 ka-ki7 kong2, Goa2 bo5 hoan7-choe7.  36). Li2 siaN2-su7 chau2-tang chau2-sai, beh koe2-oaN7 li2 e5 lou7 ah? li2 beh in-ui7 Ai-kip8 lai5 kian3-siau3, chhin-chhiuN7 cheng5 in-ui7 A-sut8 lai5 kian3-siau3 chit8-iuN7.  37). Li2 iah8 beh siang-chhiu2 pho7 thau5-khak, tui3 hia chhut--lai5; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa i2-keng khi3-choat8 li2 sou2 oa2-kho3--e5; li2 iah8 boe7 tui3 in tit-tioh8 heng-thong.

[3]	U7 teh kong2, Lang5 na7 li5-chhut i e5 bou2, bou2 chiu7 li7-khui i, ke3 pat8-lang5; chiu7 i cheng5 e5 tiong7-hu kiam2 thang koh chhin-kun7 i mah? na7 an2-ni, hit e5 toe7-hng kiam2 bo5 bak-tioh8 la5-sam5 mah? tok8-tok8 li2 kap choe7-choe7 chhin-ai3--e5 kiaN5-im5, iau2-ku2 thang kui ti7 Goa2; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  2). Li2 tioh8 kiah8-bak8 khoaN3 chiah e5 kng-kho7-kho7 koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7; ti7 toh-loh8 bo5 u7 im5-heng7 ah? li2 che7 ti7 lou7-piN theng3-hau7, chhin-chhiuN7 A-lah8-pek lang5 ti7 khong3-ia2 chit8-iuN7; koh eng7 li2 e5 im5-heng7 sia5-ok phah la5-sam5 choan5-toe7.  3). In-ui7 an2-ni, ho2 e5 hou7-chui2 theng5-chi2, chhun-thiN e5 hou7 bo5 loh8; li2 iau2 u7 chhiong-ki e5 bin7, m7-chai kian3-siau3.  4). Li2 kiam2 m7 tui3 chit-si5 kio3 Goa2 kong2, Goa2 e5 pe7 ah, Li2 si7 goa2 siau3-lian5 e5 si5, in2-chhoa7 goa2--e5?  5). I kiam2 eng2-eng2 khng3 siu7-khi3, lau5 kau3 lou7-be2 mah? khoaN3 ah, li2 u7 an2-ni kong2, iau2-ku2 chin7 li2 sou2 oe7--e5 kiaN5-phaiN2.
	6). Tng Iok-se-a ong5 che7-ui7 e5 si5, Ia5-ho5-hoa koh tui3 goa2 kong2, Poe7-gek8 e5 I2-sek-liat8 sou2 choe3--e5, li2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 bo5? I chiuN7 chiah e5 koaiN5-soaN, ti7 long2-chong2 chhiN-chhui3 e5 chhiu7-kha kiaN5 im5-loan7. 7). I kiaN5 chiah e5 tai7-chi3 i2-au7, Goa2 kong2, I beh kui-oa2 Goa2, chong2-si7 i bo5, i kan-cha3 e5 sio2-be7 Iu5-tai7 iah8 u7 khoaN3-kiN3.  8). Poe7-gek8 e5 I2-sek-liat8 kiaN5 im5-loan7, Goa2 ui7-tioh8 chit e5 ian5-kou3 hou7 i li5-su, li5-chhut i; Goa2 khoaN3-kiN3 i kan-cha3 e5 sio2-be7 Iu5-tai7, iu5-goan5 bo5 kiaN, iah8 si7 khi3 kiaN5-im5.  9). I sui5-pian7 kiaN5 i e5 im5-loan7, chiu7 phah la5-sam5 chit e5 toe7-hng; chiu7 kap chioh8-thau5 chha5-thau5 kiaN5-im5.  10). Sui-jian5 u7 chiah-e5 it-chhe3 e5 su7, i kan-cha3 e5 sio2-be7 Iu5-tai7 iu5-goan5 bo5 choan-sim kui-ng3 Goa2, put-ko3 si7 ke2-i3 na7-tiaN7; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	11). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 goa2 kong2, Poe7-gek8 e5 I2-sek-liat8, pi2 kan-cha3 e5 Iu5-tai7, iau2 khah u7 gi7.  12). Li2 tioh8 khi3 ng3 pak-hng thoan5 chiah e5 oe7, kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Poe7-gek8 e5 I2-sek-liat8 ah, tioh8 to3--lai5; Goa2 bo5 beh eng7 siu7-khi3 e5 bak8-chiu khoaN3 lin2; in-ui7 Goa2 si7 chu5-ai3--e5, Goa2 bo5 beh eng2-oan2 khng3 siu7-khi3; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  13). Tok8-tok8 tioh8 jin7 li2 e5 choe7, chiu7-si7 li2 ui5-poe7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3; ti7 long2-chong2 chhiN-chhui3 e5 chhiu7-kha, chau2-tang chau2-sai, chhe7 pat8-e5; bo5 thiaN-than3 Goa2 e5 oe7; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  14). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Poe7-gek8 e5 kiaN2-ji5 ah, tioh8 to3--lai5; in-ui7 Goa2 choe3 lin2 e5 tiong7-hu; koh Goa2 beh chiong lin2 tui3 chit8 e5 siaN5 chhu2 chit8 lang5, tui3 chit8-chok8 chhu2 nng7 lang5, toa3 kau3 Sek-an.  15). Goa2 beh chiong hap8 Goa2 e5 sim e5 bok8-chia2 siuN2-su3 lin2; in beh eng7 chai-bat kap ti3-hui7 iuN2-chhi7 lin2.  16). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Lin2 ti7 kok-lai7 siN-thoaN3 choe7-choe7; tng hiah e5 jit8-chi2, lang5 bo5 beh koh kong2-khi2, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 iok-kui7; iah8 bo5 beh ki3 ti7 sim--nih; long2 boe7-ki3--tit, long2 bo5 khi3 chhe7, iah8 bo5 koh choe3--i.  17). Hit-si5 lang5 beh chheng Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 choe3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 po2-cho7; ban7-kok beh chu7-chip8 kau3 hia; chiu7-si7 in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5, lai5 kau3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2; in bo5 koh chiau3 ka-ki7 phaiN2-sim e5 kong-ngi7 kiaN5 tai7-chi3.  18). Tng hiah e5 jit8-chi2, Iu5-tai7 ke beh kap I2-sek-liat8 ke tang5-kiaN5; tui3 pak-hng e5 toe7 saN-kap lai5, kau3 Goa2 siuN2-su3 lin2 e5 liat8-chou2 choe3-giap8 e5 toe7.
	19). Chong2-si7 Goa2 kong2, Goa2 chaiN2-iuN7 oe7 thang pai5-liat8 lin2 ti7 chiah e5 kiaN2 e5 tiong-kan, chiong ho2 e5 toe7 siuN2-su3 li2, chiu7-si7 liat8-kok-tiong siong7-ho2 e5 giap8? Goa2 koh kong2, Lin2 tioh8 chheng Goa2 kong2, Goa2 e5 pe7 ah; iah8 bo5 koh to3-tng2 khi3, m7-te3 Goa2.  20). I2-sek-liat8 ke ah, lin2 tui3 Goa2 kiaN5 kan-cha3, chin-chiaN3 chhin-chhiuN7 hu7-jin5 kiaN5 kan-cha3 li7-khui i e5 tiong7-hu; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  21). Ti7 kng-kho7-kho7 koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7 thiaN-kiN3 siaN, chiu7-si7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 thi5-khau3 khun2-kiu5 e5 siaN; chiu7-si7 in-ui7 in kiaN5 sia5-phiah e5 lou7, boe7-ki3-tit in e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  22). Lin2 chiah e5 poe7-gek8 e5 kiaN2-ji5 ah, tioh8 to3--lai5; Goa2 beh i-ho2 lin2 e5 poe7-gek8.  KhoaN3 ah, goan2 lai5 kau3 Li2 chia; in-ui7 Li2 si7 goan2 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  23). Tui3 sio2-soaN a2-si7 toa7-soaN e5 lau7-jiat8, ng3-bang7 tit-tioh8 pang-chan7, sit8-chai7 si7 khang-khang; I2-sek-liat8 e5 tit-tioh8 kiu3, chin-chiaN3 chai7-ti7 goan2 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  24). Tui3 goan2 siau3-lian5 i2-lai5, hit e5 thang kian3-siau3 e5 su7, chiong goan2 e5 liat8-chou2 sou2 tioh8-boa5 lai5 tit-tioh8--e5, chiu7-si7 in e5 iuN5-kun5, gu5-kun5, kap in e5 kiaN2, cha-bou2-kiaN2, long2 thun-chiah8--khi3.  25). Goan2 to2 ti7 goan2 e5 kian3-siau3-tiong, goan2 e5 leng5-jiok8 jia-kham3 goan2; in-ui7 tui3 siau3-lian5 kau3 taN, goan2 kap goan2 e5 liat8-chou2 siong5-siong5 tek-choe7 goan2 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa; bo5 thiaN-than3 goan2 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 siaN.

[4]	Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, I2-sek-liat8 ah, Li2 na7 kheng2 to3--lai5, chiu7 to3--lai5 Goa2 chia; na7 tui3 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tu5--khi3 li2 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7, iah8 bo5 chhin3-chhai2 kiaN5;  2). iah8 chiau3 seng5-sit8, kong-peng5, kong-gi7, ki2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 eng2-oah8 lai5 chiu3-choa7; chiu7 liat8-kok beh tui3 I lai5 ka-ki7 kiu5 hok-khi3; iah8 beh in-ui7 I lai5 khoa-khau2.
	3). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Iu5-tai7 lang5 kap Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 an2-ni kong2, Tioh8 khai-khun2 lin2 e5 thou2-toe7, boh8-tit ia7-cheng2 ti7 chhi3-phe3-lai7.  4). Iu5-tai7 lang5 kap Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 ah, lin2 tioh8 ka7 pun2-sin kiaN5 kat-le2, kui ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa; tu5--khi3 sim-lai7 e5 su-iok8; kiaN-liau2 Goa2 e5 siu7-khi3, in-ui7 lin2 sou2-kiaN5 e5 phaiN2, lai5 hoat-choh; chhin-chhiuN7 he2 toh8--khi2-lai5, sim7-chi3 bo5 lang5 oe7 phah-hoa.
	5). Lin2 tioh8 thoan5 ti7 Iu5-tai7, po3 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, kong2, Lin2 tioh8 ti7 kok-lai7 pun5 sau3-kak, toa7-siaN kio3 kong2, Lin2 tioh8 chu7-chip8, lan2 thang chin3-jip8 kian-kou3 e5 siaN5.  6). Eng-kai ng3 Sek-an khia7 toa7-ki5; tioh8 to5-chau2, m7-thang theng5-kha; in-ui7 Goa2 beh hou7 chai-e7 kap toa7 e5 hui2-hoai7 tui3 pak-hng lai5.  7). U7 sai tui3 am7 e5 chhiu7-na5-tiong chiuN7--lai5, hui2-hoai7 liat8-kok--e5, i i2-keng khi2-sin, chhut i e5 pun2 sou2-chai7; beh hou7 li2 e5 toe7 pha-hng, hou7 li2 e5 siaN5 hong-hoe3, bo5 lang5 khia7-khi2.  8). Ui7-tioh8 an2-ni, lin2 e5 io tioh8 ha5 moa5-pou3, toa7-siaN thi5-khau5; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 toa7 siu7-khi3 bo5 tui3 lan2 oat8-to3-tng2.  9). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, kau3 hit-jit8 kun-ong5 e5 sim, kui3-chok8 e5 sim, long2 beh siau-biat8; che3-si long2 beh chhiN-kiaN, sian-ti long2 beh gong5-ngiah8.  10). Goa2 kong2, Ai--ah, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 chin-chiaN3 si7 toa7-toa7 khi-phian3 chit e5 peh-siN3 kap Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2; ka7 in kong2, Lin2 beh tit-tioh8 peng5-an, ki5-sit8 to-kiam3 hai7-tioh8 in e5 siN3-mia7.  11). Hit-si5 beh u7 oe7 tui3 chit e5 peh-siN3 kap Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 kong2, Beh u7 jiat8-jiat8 e5 hong, tui3 khong3-ia2 kng-kho7-kho7 koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7, ng3 Goa2 e5 cheng3 peh-siN3 chhe--lai5; m7-si7 beh poa3--i, iah8 m7-si7 beh hou7 i chheng-khi3.  12). Beh u7 koh-khah toa7 e5 hong, ui7-tioh8 Goa2 chhe--lai5; taN Goa2 koh beh hoat-chhut phoaN3-su5 lai5 kong-kek in.  13). KhoaN3 ah, i beh chhin-chhiuN7 hun5 khi2-lai5; i e5 chian3-chhia chhin-chhiuN7 kng2-le5-hong, i e5 be2 pi2 eng-chiau2 khah kin2; u7 chai-e7 ah, in-ui7 lan2 pai7-bo5 lah.  14). Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 ah, li2 tioh8 soe2-chheng li2 e5 sim, lai5 tu5--khi3 phaiN2, hou7 li2 thang tit-tioh8 kiu3; phaiN2 liam7-thau5 chun5 ti7 li2 e5 sim-lai7, beh kau3 ti7-si5 ah?  15). U7 siaN tui3 Tan3 thoan5-po3, tui3 I2-hoat-lian5 soaN po3 chai-e7.  16). Lin2 tioh8 thoan5 hou7 liat8-kok, po3-ko3 kong-kek Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 tai7-chi3, kong2, U7 ui5-khun3 siaN5--e5, tui3 hng7-hng7 e5 sou2-chai7 lai5; chhut in e5 siaN, kong-kek Iu5-tai7 chiah e5 siaN5.  17). In chiu-ui5 kong-kek i chhin-chhiuN7 kou3-hng5 e5 lang5; in-ui7 i poe7-poan7 Goa2; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  18). Li2 e5 sou2-kiaN5, li2 e5 sou2-choe3, ti3-kau3 li2 u7 chiah e5 su7; che si7 li2 e5 choe7-ok, sit8-chai7 si7 khou2, si7 hai7 kau3 li2 e5 sim.
	19). goa2 e5 chong7-hu2 ah, goa2 e5 chong7-hu2 ah, goa2 e5 sim thang3-thiaN3, goa2 e5 sim ti7 goa2 e5 lai7-bin7 peh-pak, goa2 boe7-oe7 cheng7-cheng7 bo5 kong2-oe7; in-ui7 goa2 i2-keng thiaN-kiN3 sau3-kak e5 siaN, kau-chian3 e5 hoah-hiam3.  20). Lang5 teh po3 hui2-hoai7, koh hui2-hoai7; in-ui7 choan5-toe7 pai7-hoai7, goa2 e5 pou3-piN5 hut-jian5 pai7-hoai7, goa2 e5 tiuN3-ui5 tiap-a2-ku2 phoa3-lih8.  21). Goa2 khoaN3-kiN3 toa7-ki5, thiaN-kiN3 sau3-kak e5 siaN; beh kau3 joa7-ku2 ah?  22). Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 gu5-gong7, m7-bat Goa2; in si7 gu5-gong7 bo5 chhang-mia5 e5 kiaN2; kiaN5-phaiN2 chiu7 gau5, kiaN2-ho2 chiu7 ham-ban7.
	23). Sian-ti kong2, Goa2 khoaN3 toe7, khoaN3 ah, toe7 si7 khang-khang hun7-tun7; goa2 khoaN3 thiN, thiN iah8 bo5 kng.  24). Goa2 khoaN3 hiah e5 toa7-soaN, khoaN3 ah, in long2 tin2-tang7; sio2-soaN iah8 long2 io5-lai5 io5-khi3.  25). Goa2 koh khoaN3, khoaN3 ah, long2 bo5 lang5; khong-tiong e5 pe-chiau2, iah8 long2 pe-chau2.  26). Goa2 koh khoaN3--i, khoaN3 ah, pui5 e5 chhan5 piN3-choe3 pha-hng e5 toe7; it-chhe3 e5 siaN5 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5, in-ui7 I e5 toa7 siu7-khi3, long2-chong2 to2-hoai7.  27). In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Choan5-toe7 tek-khak pha-hng; chong2-si7 Goa2 bo5 beh hui2-biat8 kau3-chin7.  28). In-ui7 an2-ni toe7 beh iu-bun7, thiN-teng2 ia7 beh ou-am3; Goa2 i2-keng kong2--i, i2-keng tiaN7-tioh8--i, tek-khak bo5 the3-hoe2, ia7 bo5 oat8-tng2 i3-su3, m7 choe3--i.  29). Tak8 e5 siaN5 e5 lang5 in-ui7 be2-peng kap sia7-chiN3 e5 lang5 e5 hoa7-hoa7-hau2, chiu7 long2 to5-chau2, chin3-jip8 chhiu7-na5, pe5-chiuN7 chioh8-poaN5-teng2; tak8 e5 siaN5 tu2-tioh8 khi3-sak, bo5 lang5 khia7-khi2.  30). Li2 soe-pai7 e5 si5 beh chaiN2-iuN7 choe3? Sui-jian5 chheng7 chu-ang5 e5 saN, eng7 kim-khi3 chng-thaN7, eng7 sek-liau7 ui7 li2 e5 bak8-chiu, an2-ni tian2 ho2-khoaN3, si7 khang-khang; loan5-ai3 li2--e5 khoaN3-khin li2, soa3 siau3-siuN7 li2 e5 siN3-mia7.  31). In-ui7 goa2 thiaN-kiN3 siaN chhin-chhiuN7 siN-kiaN2 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, chhin-chhiuN7 siN thau5-chiuN7-kiaN2 e5 kan-khou2, chiu7-si7 Sek-an cha-bou2-kiaN2 e5 siaN, i chhoan2 toa7-khui3, thi2-khui chhiu2, kong2, Goa2 u7 chai-e7 ah, in-ui7 goa2 e5 sin5-hun5 ui7-tioh8 thai5-lang5-e5 lai5 hun7-khi3.

[5]	Lin2 tioh8 chau2-lai5 chau2-khi3 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 koe-lou7 lai5 khoaN3 lai5 tham3-thiaN, ti7 i e5 khoan-khoah e5 sou2-chai7 lai5 chhe7, khoaN3 oe7 tu2-tioh8 chit8-lang5, a2-si7 u7 lang5 kiaN5 kong-gi7, kiu5 seng5-sit8; Goa2 chiu7 beh sia3-bian2 chit e5 siaN5.  2). In sui-jian5 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 oah8--e5, in sou2 chiu3 e5 choa7 sit8-chai7 si7 ke2.  3). Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 e5 bak8-chiu kiam2-m7-si7 ng3 seng5-sit8 mah? Li2 phah in, in ia7 bo5 iu-siong; Li2 hui2-biat8 in, in m7-kheng2 siu7 kau3-tok; in hou7 in e5 bin7 pi2 chioh8 khah-teng7, m7-kheng2 hoe5-thau5.  4). Goa2 chiu7 kong2, Chiah e5 lang5 sit8-chai7 si7 song3-hiong, si7 gu5-gong7, in-ui7 m7-bat Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 lou7, kap in e5 Siong7-te3 e5 hoat-tou7;  5). goa2 beh khi3 kiN3 in e5 se3-ka, kap in kong2-oe7; in-ui7 in bat Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 lou7, kap in e5 Siong7-te3 e5 hoat-tou7.  Na7-si7 in tang5-sim at-chih8 taN, phah-tng7 pak8 i e5 soh.  6). Sou2-i2 chhiu7-na5 e5 sai beh chhut-lai5 ka7-si2 in; e5-hng-si5 e5 chhai5-long5 beh thun-chiah8 in, pa3 beh ti7 chiah e5 siaN5-goa7 tng-tan2 in, kiN3-na7 chhut-siaN5-e5 tek-khak hou7 in thiah-chhui3, in-ui7 in e5 choe7-koa3 chin-choe7, poe7-gek8 na2 siong-tiong7.  7). Che Goa2 thai2 oe7 sia3-bian2 li2 ah? li2 e5 kiaN2-ji5 li7-khui Goa2, koh ki2 chiah e5 m7-si7 Siong7-te3--e5 lai5 chiu3-choa7; Goa2 hou7 in pa2-chiok, in chiu7 kiaN5 kan-im5, kui-tin7 chu7-chip8 ti7 chhiong-ki e5 chhu3.  8). In chhin-chhiuN7 chhi7-pa2 e5 be2 si3-koe3 phau2; tak8-e5 ng3 i chhu3-piN e5 bou2 chhin-chhiuN7 be2 ki-ki-hau2.  9). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 kiam2 bo5 in-ui7 chiah e5 su7 lai5 pan7 in mah? Goa2 e5 sim kiam2 bo5 beh tui3 chit ho7 e5 kok-bin5 lai5 po3-siu5 mah?
	10). Lin2 tioh8 chiuN7 i e5 phu5-to5-hng5 e5 chhiuN5 lai5 hui2-hoai7 i, chong2-si7 m7-thang hui2 kau3-liau2; tioh8 tu5--khi3 i e5 ki, in-ui7 in bo5 siok8 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  11). In-ui7 I2-sek-liat8 ke kap Iu5-tai7 ke toa7-toa7 kiaN5 khui2-cha3, kong-kek Goa2; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2 e5.  12). In m7-jin7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, chiu7 kong2, Che peng7 m7-si7 I; chai-e7 bo5 beh lim5-kau3 goan2; to-kiam3 kap ki-hng goan2 ia7 boe7-oe7 tu2-tioh8.  13). Sian-ti e5 oe7 beh chiaN5-choe3 hong, Chu2 e5 oe7 bo5 ti7 in e5 sim; beh chiau3 an2-ni hou7 in tu2-tioh8.  14). Sou2-i2 ban7-kun e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, In-ui7 lin2 kong2 chit e5 oe7; khoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh hou7 Goa2 e5 oe7 ti7 li2 e5 chhui3 choe3 he2, hou7 chit e5 peh-siN3 choe3 chha5, chit e5 he2 beh sio-biat8 in.  15). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, I2-sek-liat8 e5 ke ah, li2 khoaN3, Goa2 beh hou7 chit8-kok tui3 hng7-hng7 lai5 kong-kek lin2, chiu7-si7 kiong5 e5 kok, tui3 kou2-cha2 chiu7 u7 e5 kok, i e5 gian5-gu2 li2 boe7 hiau2-tit, ia7 boe7 beng5-pek8 i sou2 kong2--e5.  16). In e5 chiN3-te7 si7 khui-khui e5 bong7; in long2 si7 iong2-su7.  17). In beh chiah8-liau2 li2 e5 gou7-kak kap li2 e5 bi2-niu5, chiu7-si7 li2 e5 kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2 sou2 tioh8 chiah8 e5; ia7 beh chiah8-liau2 li2 e5 iuN5-kun5, gu5-kun5; chiah8-liau2 li2 e5 phu5-to5 kap bu5-hoa-ko2; koh beh eng7 to hui2-hoai7 li2 sou2 oa2-kho3 kian-kou3 e5 siaN5.  18). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Chiu7-na7 kau3 hit-si5 Goa2 ia7 bo5 beh it-chin7 chau5-biat8 lin2.  19). Hit-si5 lin2 na7 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa goan2 e5 Siong7-te3 ui7-tioh8 siaN2-su7 tui3 goan2 kiaN5 che it-chhe3 e5 su7 ah? li2 tioh8 in3 i kong2, Chhin-chhiuN7 lin2 i2-keng pang3-sak Goa2, hok8-sai7 pat8-ho7 e5 siong7-te3 ti7 lin2 e5 toe7-hng, an2-ni lin2 ia7 beh hok8-sai7 goa7-pang lang5 ti7 bo5 siok8 lin2 e5 toe7-hng.
	20). Lin2 tioh8 thoan5 ti7 Nga2-kok ke, po3 ti7 Iu5-tai7, kong2,  21). Gong7-gong7 bu5-ti e5 peh-siN3 ah, lin2 u7 bak8-chiu boe7 khoaN3, u7 hi7-khang boe7 thiaN, taN tioh8 thiaN chit e5 oe7;  22). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Lin2 m7 kiaN Goa2 mah? bo5 ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5 mah? Goa2 siat eng2-oan2 e5 le7, eng7 soa choe3 hai2 e5 kai3-han7, i boe7 poaN5-ke3; i e5 eng2 sui-jian5 gia5 koaiN5, ia7 boe7-oe7 iaN5; sui-jian5 hoa7-hoa7-hau2, ia7 boe7-oe7 poaN5-ke3.  23). Tok8-tok8 chit e5 peh-siN3 u7 hoan2-poan7 poe7-gek8 e5 sim; in poe7-gek8 Goa2 choe3 in khi3.  24). In sim-lai7 ia7 bo5 kong2, TaN lan2 tioh8 keng3-ui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lan2 e5 Siong7-te3, I chiau3-si5 siuN2-su3 hou7-chui2, chiu7-si7 cheng5 e5 hou7; au7 e5 hou7; I ia7 u7 teng7 chiah e5 siu-seng5 e5 si5-ki5, lau5-teh hou7 lan2.  25). Lin2 e5 choe7-giat8 hou7 chiah e5 su7 hoan2-tng2 li7-khui lin2; lin2 e5 choe7-ok hou7 lin2 boe7-oe7 tit-tioh8 hok-khi3.  26). In-ui7 ti7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3-tiong u7 chhe7-tioh8 phaiN2-lang5; in bih--teh, chhin-chhiuN7 siat oah8-tauh e5 lang5 teh tng-tan2; in tiuN lo5-bang7 lai5 liah8 lang5.  27). In e5 chhu3 u7 khui2-cha3 moa2-moa2, si7 chhin-chhiuN7 chiau2-lang5-lai7 u7 chiau2 moa2-moa2; sou2-i2 in chiaN5-choe3 toa7 koh ho2-giah8.  28). In pui5 koh kng-siN, choe3 phaiN2 ke3-thau5; bo5 ui7-tioh8 lang5 sin-oan, chiu7-si7 bo5 ui7-tioh8 bo5-pe7 e5 kiaN2 sin-oan, hou7 i heng-thong; iah8 bo5 in-ui7 song3-hiong lang5 phoaN3-toan3.  29). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 kiam2 bo5 in-ui7 chiah e5 su7 lai5 pan7 in mah? Goa2 e5 sim kiam2 bo5 beh tui3 chit-ho7 e5 kok-bin5 lai5 po3-siu5 mah?
	30). Chit e5 thou2-toe7 u7 ki5-iN7 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7;  31). sian-ti thoan5 hu-ke2, che3-si oa2-kho3 in lai5 pa3-koan5; Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 iah8 ai3 i an2-ni; kau3 kiat-kiok8, lin2 beh chaiN2-iuN7 choe3?

[6]	Pian7-nga2-bin2 lang5 ah, lin2 tioh8 chau2-chhut Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2; ti7 The5-ko-a pun5 sau3-kak; ti7 Pek-hap-ki-lim5 pang3 ian-tun; in-ui7 u7 chai-e7 kap toa7 e5 hui2-biat8 tui3 pak-hng loh8--lai5.  2). Goa2 beh chau5-biat8 Sek-an e5 cha-bou2-gin2-na2, chiu7-si7 hit e5 sui2 koh iu3-siu3--e5.  3). Bok8-chia2 kap i e5 iuN5-kun5 beh kau3 i hia, ti7 i e5 chiu-ui5 tah pou3-piN5; tak8-e5 ti7 i sou2 chiam3 e5 toe7, hou7 iuN5 chiah8-chhau2.  4). Lin2 tioh8 pi7-pan7 kau-chian3 kong-kek i; khi2-lai5 ah, lan2 tioh8 than3 tiong-tau3 e5 si5 chiuN7-khi3; chham2--ah, jit8 i2-keng chhia5-sai, beh am3 e5 iaN2 i2-keng thoa-tng5.  5). Khi2-lai5 ah, lan2 tioh8 thau3-mi5 chiuN7-khi3, hui2-hoai7 i e5 kiong-tian7.  6). In-ui7 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Lin2 tioh8 chho3 chhiu7-bak8, khi2 thou5-tui, kong-kek Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2; che si7 hit-e5 eng-kai siu7 heng5-hoat8 e5 siaN5; in tiong-kan it-chin7 si7 po7-giok8.  7). ChiN2 chaiN2-iuN7 chheng3-chhut chui2, chit e5 siaN5 iah8 an2-ni chheng3-chhut phaiN2; ti7 in tiong-kan siong5-siong5 thiaN-kiN3 u7 kiong5-po7 hui2-biat8 e5 su7; piN7-thiaN3 sun2-siong iah8 siong5-siong5 ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5.  8). Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 ah, li2 tioh8 siu7 ka3-si7; bian2-tit Goa2 e5 sim kap li2 chhiN-sou; bian2-tit Goa2 hou7 li2 pha-hng, chiaN5-choe3 bo5 lang5 khia7-khi2 e5 toe7.
	9). Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, In beh it-chin7 liah8 I2-sek-liat8 chhun e5 peh-siN3, chhin-chhiuN7 tiah phu5-to5 chit8-iuN7; li2 tioh8 chhin-chhiuN7 tiah phu5-to5-e5, chhiu2 koh tng2-jip8 chhiu7-ki.  10). TaN goa2 beh tui3 chi7-chui7 kong2-oe7 choe3 kan-cheng3, hou7 in thiaN ah? khoaN3 ah, in e5 hi7-a2 be7 siu7 kat-le2, boe7-oe7 thiaN; khoaN3 ah, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7, in liah8-choe3 kian3-siau3, bo5 hoaN-hi2--i.  11). In-ui7 an2-ni, goa2 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 siu7-khi3 chhiong-moa2, lun2-boe7-tiau5; goa2 beh choe3-chit8-e7 piaN3 ti7 koe-lou7 e5 gin2-na2, kap chu7-hoe7 e5 siau3-lian5 lang5; lian5 tiong7-hu kap i e5 bou2, lau7-lang5 kap jit8-chi2 moa2-chiok--e5, long2 beh siu7-liah8.  12). In e5 chhu3-theh8, chhan5-hng5, kap bou2, long2 beh pian3-choe3 pat8-lang5-e5; in-ui7 Goa2 beh chhun-chhiu2 kong-kek chit sou2-chai7 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  13). In-ui7 in tui3 te7-it soe3 kau3 te7-it toa7--e5, long2 it-bi7 tham-sim; tui3 sian-ti kau3 che3-si, long2 kiaN5 kan-cha3.  14). In chhin3-chhin3 chhai2-chhai2 i-ti7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 e5 siong, kong2, Peng5-an lah, peng5-an lah; ki5-sit8 bo5 peng5-an.  15). In kiaN5 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7, chai kian3-siau3 mah? bo5, in long2 bo5 kian3-siau3, iah8 boe7 ang5-bin7; in-ui7 an2-ni, in beh poah8-to2 ti7 poah8-to2 e5 lang5 e5 tiong-kan; Goa2 pan7 in e5 si5, in beh tian-to2; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2 e5.
	16). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Lin2 tioh8 khia7 ti7 lou7--nih khoaN3; chha5-mng7 ku7 e5 lou7, hit tiau5 ho2-lou7 ti7 toh-loh8, chiu7 tioh8 kiaN5--i; an2-ni lin2 e5 sim beh tit-tioh8 an-hioh; chong2-si7 in kong2, Goan2 m7 kiaN5--i.  17). Goa2 ka7 lin2 siat siu2-bang7--e5, kong2, Tioh8 thiaN sau3-kak e5 siaN; chong2-si7 in kong2, Goan2 m7 thiaN.  18). Liat8-kok ah, in-ui7 an2-ni lin2 tioh8 thiaN; hoe7-chiong3 ah, lin2 tioh8 chai in tiong-kan u7 sim2-mih8 su7.  19). Toe7 ah, tioh8 thiaN; khoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh hou7 chai-e7 kau3 chit e5 peh-siN3, chiu7-si7 in e5 tou5-bou5 e5 kiat-ko2; in-ui7 in m7 thiaN-than3 Goa2 e5 oe7; Goa2 e5 lut8-hoat, in iah8 khi3-choat8.  20). Tui3 Si7-pa chhut e5 ju2-hiuN, tui3 hng7-hng7 e5 sou2-chai7 chhut e5 chhiong-pou5, toa3 lai5 hou7 Goa2, beh siaN2-tai7? lin2 e5 sio-che3 bo5 tit-tioh8 chiap-lap8; lin2 e5 le2-mih8, Goa2 iah8 bo5 hoaN-hi2.  21). Sou2-i2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh he7 that-gai7 e5 chioh8 ti7 chit e5 peh-siN3 e5 bin7-cheng5; pe7 kap kiaN2 beh choe3-chit8-e7 poah8 ti7 hit teng2-bin7; chhu3-piN kap peng5-iu2 iah8 long2 beh biat8-bo5.
	22). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, u7 chit8 chiong2 e5 peh-siN3 tui3 pak-hng lai5; iah8 u7 chit8 e5 toa7-kok heng-khi2, tui3 toe7-kek8 lai5.  23). In kiah8 keng kap chhiuN; in chan5-jim2 bo5 lin5-bin2; in e5 siaN chhin-chhiuN7 hai2 hoa7-hoa7-hau2; Sek-an e5 cha-bou2-gin2-na2 ah, in long2 khia5-be2 liat8-tin7, chhin-chhiuN7 chian3-su7 beh kong-kek li2.  24). Goan2 thiaN-kiN3 in e5 hong-siaN, chhiu2 chiu7 nng2--loh8-khi3; thong3-khou2 khiN5-tioh8 goan2, thang3-thiaN3 chhin-chhiuN7 siN-kiaN2 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 chit8-iuN7.  25). Lin2 m7-thang chhut-khi3 chhan5--nih, iah8 m7-thang kiaN5 ti7 lou7-nih; in-ui7 ti7-hia u7 tui3-tek8 e5 to-kiam3, si3-ui5 u7 kiaN-hiaN5.  26). Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 ah, tioh8 ha5 moa5-pou3, ko7 ti7 he2-hu-tiong; tioh8 pi-siong, chhin-chhiuN7 song3-sit tok8-siN kiaN2, thong3-sim thi5-khau3; in-ui7 chan5-hai7--e5 beh hut-jian5 kau3 ti7 lan2.  27). Goa2 siat-lip8 li2 ti7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3-tiong, choe3 chhi3-giam7--e5 kap oe7-sou2; hou7 li2 chai lai5 chhi3-giam7 in e5 kiaN5-choe3.  28). In long2 si7 toa7 poe7-gek8 e5 lang5; si3-koe3 kiaN5 hui2-pong3; in si7 tang5, si7 thih; long2 si7 kiaN5 hui2-hoai7--e5.  29). Hong-kui7 sio--tioh8, ian5 i2-keng iuN5 ti7 he2-lai7; in tit8-tit8 thoan3-lian7, kau3-be2 si7 khang-khang; in-ui7 phaiN2--e5 iau2-be7 tu5-khi3.  30). Lang5 beh chheng in choe3 siu7 khi3-sak e5 gun5, in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa i2-keng khi3-sak in.

[7]	U7 oe7 tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa kau3 Ia5-li7-bi2, kong2,  2). Li2 tioh8 khia7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3 e5 mng5, ti7-hia soan-thoan5 chit e5 oe7, kong2, Hoan7-na7 siok8 Iu5-tai7 jip8 chiah e5 mng5, keng3-pai3 Ia5-ho5-hoa--e5, tioh8 thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7.  3). Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3, an2-ni kong2, Lin2 tioh8 koe2-chiaN3 sou2-kiaN5 sou2-choe3, Goa2 chiu7 hou7 lin2 khia7-khi2 ti7 chit e5 toe7-hng.  4). Lin2 m7-thang oa2-kho3 peh8-chhat8 e5 oe7, kong2, Chiah-e5 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 tian7, si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 tian7, si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 tian7.  5). Lin2 na7 it-chin7 koe2-chiaN3 sou2-kiaN5 sou2-choe3; ti7 lang5 kap chhu3-piN e5 tiong-kan, chin-chiaN3 u7 kiaN5 kong-peng5;  6). bo5 phaiN2 khoan2-thai7 chhut-goa7 lang5, i2-kip8 kou-ji5 koaN2-hu7; ti7 chit e5 toe7-hng bo5 lau5 bo5-choe7 e5 lang5 e5 huih, iah8 bo5 than3 pat8-ho7 e5 siong7-te3 lai5 ham7-hai7 ka-ki7;  7). Goa2 chiu7 hou7 lin2 khia7-khi2 ti7 chit e5 sou2-chai7, chiu7-si7 Goa2 sou2 siuN2-su3 lin2 e5 liat8-chou2 e5 toe7, tui3 eng2-oan2 kau3 eng2-oan2.  8). KhoaN3 ah, lin2 oa2-kho3 peh8-chhat8 bo5 li7-ek e5 oe7.  9). Lin2 thau-theh8, thai5-lang5, kan-im5, lam7-sam2 chiu3-choa7, ng3 Pa-lek8 sio-hiuN, iah8 than3 lin2 peng5-sou3 sou2 m7-bat pat8-ho7 e5 siong7-te3,  10). koh lai5 khia7 ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5, ti7 chit-keng eng7 Goa2 e5 mia5 lai5 chheng-hou e5 chhu3, kong2, Goan2 tit-tioh8 kiu3 lah; an2-ni, si7 beh hou7 lin2 khi3 kiaN5 chiah e5 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7 mah?  11). Chit-keng eng7 Goa2 e5 mia5 lai5 chheng-hou e5 chhu3, lin2 khoaN3-choe3 chhat8-siu7 mah? Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2, Goa2 i2-keng khoaN3-kiN3 lah.  12). Lin2 taN tioh8 khi3 Goa2 ti7 Si7-lo5 e5 sou2-chai7, chiu7-si7 Goa2 khi2-thau5 siat-choe3 kiu5-kio3 Goa2 e5 mia5 e5 ui7, khoaN3 Goa2 in-ui7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 choe7-ok, chaiN2-iuN7 khoan2-thai7 hit sou2-chai7.  13). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, TaN in-ui7 lin2 kiaN5 chiah e5 it-chhe3 e5 su7, Goa2 u7 tui3 lin2 kong2, iah8 si7 cha2-cha2 khi2--lai5 kong2, na7-si7 lin2 m7 thiaN; Goa2 koh kio3 lin2, na7-si7 lin2 m7 in3;  14). sou2-i2 Goa2 beh khoan2-thai7 lin2 sou2 oa2-kho3 chit-keng eng7 Goa2 e5 mia5 chheng-hou e5 chhu3, i2-kip8 Goa2 sou2 siuN2-su3 lin2 kap lin2 e5 liat8-chou2 e5 toe7, chhin-chhiuN7 Goa2 cha2 khoan2-thai7 Si7-lo5 chit8-iuN7.  15). Goa2 ia7 beh koaN2 lin2 li7-khui Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5, chhin-chhiuN7 Goa2 bat koaN2 lin2 e5 cheng3 hiaN-ti7, I2-hoat-lian5 it-chhe3 e5 hou7-e3.
	16). Sou2-i2 li2 boh8-tit ui7-tioh8 chit e5 peh-siN3 ki5-to2, boh8-tit ui7-tioh8 in chhut-siaN ki5-kiu5, iah8 boh8-tit thoe3 in kiu5 Goa2; in-ui7 Goa2 bo5 beh thiaN li2.  17). In ti7 Iu5-tai7 chiah e5 siaN5-tiong, kap Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 koe-lou7 sou2 kiaN5--e5, li2 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 mah?  18). KiaN2-ji5 khioh chha5, lau7-pe7 hiaN5-he2, hu7-jin5-lang5 chhiau-mi7 choe3-piaN2, hian3 hou7 Thian-hou7; koh tui3 pat8-ho7 e5 siong7-te3 koan3-tian7; beh kek Goa2 siu7-khi3.  19). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, In kiam2-si7 kek Goa2 siu7-khi3? kiam2 m7-si7 kek in ka-ki7, ti3-kau3 in e5 bin7 kian3-siau3 mah?  20). Sou2-i2 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh chiong Goa2 e5 siu7-khi3, Goa2 e5 thong3-hun7, piaN3 ti7 chit sou2-chai7; chiu7-si7 piaN3 ti7 lang5, kap cheng-siN, i2-kip8 chhan5-ia2 e5 chhiu7-bak8, kap thou2-toe7 e5 chhut-san2; chhin-chhiuN7 he2 toh8 boe7 hoa.
	21). Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 an2-ni kong2, Tioh8 chiong lin2 e5 sio-che3 chham-ka ti7 lin2 chiah e5 che3, lai5 chiah8 bah.  22). In-ui7 Goa2 chhoa7 lin2 e5 liat8-chou2 chhut Ai-kip8 e5 jit8, lun7-kau3 sio-che3 kap chiah e5 che3, Goa2 be7-bat tui3 in kong2-khi2 lai5 beng7-leng7 in.  23). Goa2 tok8-tok8 hoan-hu3 in chi2 chit8-hang7, kong2, Lin2 tioh8 thiaN-than3 Goa2 e5 siaN, Goa2 chiu7 beh choe3 lin2 e5 Siong7-te3, lin2 iah8 beh choe3 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3; koh kiaN5 Goa2 long2-chong2 beng7-leng7 lin2 e5 lou7, chiu7 thang tit-tioh8 hok-khi3.  24). Chong2-si7 in m7 thiaN-than3, iah8 m7 aN3 hi7-khang; keng2-jian5 chiau3 in e5 ke3-bou5, kap kong-ngi7 e5 phaiN2-sim, the3-au7 bo5 chin3-cheng5.  25). Tui3 lin2 e5 liat8-chou2 chhut Ai-kip8 e5 jit8 kau3 kin-a2-jit8, Goa2 chhe Goa2 e5 cheng3 lou5-pok8 sian-ti kau3 lin2 hia; koh tak8-jit8 cha2-cha2 khi2--lai5 chhe in.  26). In iau2-ku2 m7 thiaN Goa2, iah8 m7 aN3 hi7-khang; hoan2-tng2 ngi7 in e5 am7-kun2; in kiaN5 phaiN2 pi2 in e5 liat8-chou2 khah siong-tiong7.  27). Li2 tioh8 chiong chiah-e5 it-chhe3 e5 oe7 ka7 in kong2; chong2-si7 in bo5 beh thiaN li2; li2 kio3--in, in iah8 bo5 beh in3--li2.  28). Li2 tioh8 tui3 in kong2, Che chiu7-si7 m7 thiaN-than3 Ia5-ho5-hoa in e5 Siong7-te3 e5 siaN, bo5 siu7 kau3-tok e5 kok-bin5; seng5-sit8 bo5-khi3, tui3 in e5 chhui3 choat8-tng7.
	29). Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 ah, tioh8 thi3 li2 e5 thau5-mng5 hiat-kak8; ti7 kng-kho7-kho7 koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7 chhiuN3 ai-siong e5 koa; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa khi3-sak li7-khui I sou2 siu7-khi3 e5 se3-tai7.  30). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Iu5-tai7 e5 peh-siN3 kiaN5 Goa2 sou2 khoaN3-choe3 phaiN2 e5 su7; chiong kho2-ouN3 e5 mih8 chhai7 ti7 eng7 Goa2 e5 mia5 chheng-hou e5 chhu3, phah la5-sam5--i.  31). In ti7 Pian7-him-lun3 e5 soaN-kok, khi2 To5-hui-tek8 soaN-thau5 e5 toaN5; thang ti7 he2-tiong sio in e5 kiaN2, cha-bou2-kiaN2; che m7-si7 Goa2 sou2 hoan-hu3--e5, iah8 m7-si7 Goa2 e5 sim sou2 siuN7--e5.  32). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, In-ui7 jit8-chi2 beh kau3, chit e5 toe7-hng bo5 koh chheng-choe3 To5-hui-tek8, kap Pian7-him-lun3 e5 soaN-kok; si7 beh chheng-choe3 Thai5-lang5 e5 soaN-kok; in-ui7 beh ti7 To5-hui-tek8 bai5-chong3 si2-lang5, kau3 bo5 chhun sou2-chai7.  33). Koh chit e5 peh-siN3 e5 sin-si, beh hou7 khong-tiong e5 pe-chiau2, kap toe7-chiuN7 e5 ia2-siu3, choe3 chiah8-mih8; bo5 lang5 koaN2--i.  34). Hit-si5, ti7 Iu5-tai7 chiah e5 siaN5 kap Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 koe-chhi7, Goa2 beh hou7 hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN, khoai3-lok8 e5 siaN, sin-kiaN2-sai3 e5 siaN, sin-niu5 e5 siaN, long2-chong2 soah; in-ui7 chit e5 toe7 long2 beh piN3-choe3 pha-hng.

[8]	Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Tng hit-si5 lang5 beh chiong Iu5-tai7 liat8-ong5 e5 kut-hai5, kui3-chok8 e5 kut-hai5, che3-si e5 kut-hai5, sian-ti e5 kut-hai5, Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 e5 kut-hai5, long2 tui3 bong7-tiong theh8--chhut-lai5,  2). pai5 ti7 jit8, geh8, kap thiN-siong7 e5 e7-bin7; chiu7-si7 in peng5-sou3 sou2 i3-ai3, sou2 hok8-sai7, sou2 sun7-than3, sou2 chhe7-kiu5, sou2 kui7-pai3--e5; chiah e5 kut-hai5 bo5 koh siu-sip8, bo5 koh bai5-chong3; beh ti7 toe7-bin7-chiuN7 chiaN5-choe3 pun3-so3.  3). Koh chit e5 phaiN2-chok8 sou2 chhun--e5, chiu7-si7 ti7 Goa2 koaN2 in kau3 hia sou2 chhun--e5, in long2 beh keng2 si2, m7 keng2 oah8; che si7 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	4). Li2 tioh8 tui3 in kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Lang5 poah8-to2, bo5 koh peh--khi2-lai5 mah? lang5 oat--khi3, bo5 koh oat--lai5 mah?  5). Goa2 liu5-sim thiaN, chong2-si7 in bo5 kong2 cheng3-tit8 e5 oe7, bo5 lang5 hoan2-hoe2 in phaiN2 e5 sou2-kiaN5, kong2, Goa2 choe3--e5 si7 sim2-mih8? in tak8-lang5 choan2-tng2 kiaN5 ka-ki7 e5 lou7, chhin-chhiuN7 be2 phau2-jip8 chian3-tiuN5.  7). Khong-tiong e5 hoh8 chai i tiaN7-tioh8 e5 ki5; ka-chui iN3-a2 kap hai2-gan7, long2 siu2 in lai5 e5 si5; tok8-tok8 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 m7-chai Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 hoat-lut8.  8). Ti3-hui7 e5 lang5 kian3-siau3, kiaN-hiaN5, siu7-liah8; khoaN3 ah, in pang3-sak Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7, in e5 sim-lai7 iau2 u7 sim2-mih8 ti3-hui7 ah?  10). In chhin3-chhin3 chhai2-chhai2 i-ti7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 e5 siong, kong2, Peng5-an lah, peng5-an lah; ki5-sit8 bo5 peng5-an.  12). In kiaN5 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7, chai kian3-siau3 mah? bo5, in long2 bo5 kian3-siau3, iah8 boe7 ang5-bin7; in-ui7 an2-ni, in beh poah8-to2 ti7 poah8-to2 e5 lang5 e5 tiong-kan; in siu7 pan7 e5 si5 beh tian-to2; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  13). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 beh it-chin7 biat8--in; phu5-to5-chhiu7 beh bo5 phu5-to5; bu5-hoa-ko2 chhiu7 beh bo5 bu5-hoa-ko2; hioh8 iah8 beh kou-ta5; Goa2 sou2 hou7 in--e5, long2 beh bo5--khi3.
	14). Lan2 siaN2-su7 cheng7-cheng7 che7 ah? lin2 tioh8 chu7-chip8, chiu7 lan2 thang jip8 chiah e5 kian-kou3 e5 siaN5; ti7-hia tiam7-tiam7; in-ui7 lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa hou7 lan2 tiam7-tiam7; koh chiong khou2 e5 chui2 hou7 lan2 lim; long2 si7 in-ui7 lan2 tek-choe7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  15). ThiaN-kiN3 tui3 Tan3 hia tui3-tek8 e5 be2 phng7-phng7-hau2; in e5 iong2 e5 be2 ki-ki-hau2, choan5-toe7 chiu7 long2 tin2-tang7; in-ui7 in lai5 thun-biat8 chit e5 toe7, i2-kip8 hit lai7-bin7 sou2-u7--e5; thun-biat8 chit e5 siaN5, kap ki5-tiong khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3.  17). 	18). Goa2 u7 iu-bun7, cheng5-goan7 oe7-tit an-ui3; goa2 e5 sim hun7--khi3.  19). KhoaN3 ah, goa2 e5 peh-siN3 ai-siong e5 siaN, tui3 hng7-hng7 e5 sou2-chai7 lai5, kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa bo5 ti7 Sek-an mah? i e5 ong5 bo5 ti7 hi2 lai7-bin7 mah? Siu-seng5 e5 si5 i2-keng ke3, he7-thiN e5 jit8 i2-keng chin7; goan2 iau2 bo5 tit-tioh8 kiu3.  21). In-ui7 goa2 e5 peh-siN3 e5 hui2-siong, goa2 iah8 siu7 hui2-siong; goa2 chin7-chai7 ai-siong, kiaN-hiaN5 khiN5-tiau5 goa2.  22). Ti7 Ki-liat8 kiam2 bo5 ju2-hiuN? ti7-hia kiam2 bo5 i-seng? goa2 e5 peh-siN3 chaiN2-iuN7 boe7 tit-tioh8 i-ho2?

[9]	Goan7 goa2 e5 thau5-khak choe3 chui2-choaN5, goa2 e5 bak8-chiu choe3 bak8-sai2 e5 goan5-thau5; goa2 thang ui7 goa2 e5 peh-siN3-tiong siu7-thai5 e5 lang5, jit8-mi5 thi5-khau3.
	2). Goan7 goa2 ti7 khong3-ia2 u7 chhut-goa7 lang5 hioh-mi5 e5 sou2-chai7, goa2 chiu7 thang khi3-sak goa2 e5 peh-siN3 lai5 li7-khui in; in-ui7 in long2 si7 kiaN5 kan-im5--e5, si7 kiaN5 khui2-cha3 e5 tong2-lui7.  3). In kng2-oan in e5 chih8 chhin-chhiuN7 keng lai5 kong2 peh8-chhat8; in ti7 kok-lai7 ke-thiN se3-lek8, m7-si7 ui7-tioh8 chin-sit8; chiu7-si7 phaiN2-liau2 koh phaiN2, ia7 m7-bat Goa2; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  4). Lin2 tak8-lang5 tioh8 ti5-hong5 i e5 chhu3-piN, long2 m7-thang sin3-kho3 hiaN-ti7; in-ui7 hiaN-ti7 it-chin7 saN moa5-phian3; chhu3-piN long2 si3-koe3 kiaN5, hui2-pong3 lang5.  5). In tak8-lang5 khi-phian3 chhu3-piN; m7-goan7 kong2 chin-sit8; in ka3-si7 in e5 chih8 kong2 peh8-chhat8; tioh8-boa5 choe3-phaiN2.  6). Li2 khia7-khi2 ti7 khui2-cha3-tiong; in in-ui7 khui2-cha3 m7-kheng2 jin7-bat Goa2; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	7). Sou2-i2 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh chiong in iuN5-hoa3 lai5 thoan3-lian7 in; na7 bo5, Goa2 in-ui7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 beh chaiN2-iuN7 choe3 ah?  8). In e5 chih8 si7 hai7-si2 lang5 e5 chiN3; si7 kong2 khui2-cha3; lang5-lang5 tui3 i e5 chhu3-piN chhui3 kong2 peng5-an, sim-lai7 teh siau3-siuN7 i.  9). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 kiam2 bo5 in-ui7 chiah e5 su7 lai5 pan7 in mah? Goa2 e5 sim kiam2 bo5 beh tui3 chit ho7 e5 kok-bin5 lai5 po3-siu5 mah?
	10). Goa2 beh ui7-tioh8 soaN-nia2 thi5-khau3 pi-ai, ui7-tioh8 khong3-ia2 e5 chhau2-tiuN5 chhut-siaN ai-hau2; in-ui7 in i2-keng sio-lio--khi3, sim7-chi3 bo5 lang5 keng-ke3; lang5 ia7 bo5 thiaN-kiN3 cheng-siN e5 siaN; khong-tiong e5 pe-chiau2 kap toe7-chiuN7 e5 ia2-siu3 long2 chau2-lau2-khi3.  11). Goa2 beh hou7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 pian3-choe3 thou5-tui, choe3 ia2-kau2 khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7; ia7 beh hou7 Iu5-tai7 chiah e5 siaN5 pha-hng, bo5 lang5 khia7-khi2.  12). Chi7-chui7 si7 ti3-hui7 e5 lang5 thang beng5-pek8 chit-e5 ah? Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhui3 tui3 chi7-chui7 kong2, hou7 i thang thoan5-po3 ah? chit e5 toe7 siaN2-su7 biat8-bo5, sio-hui2 chhin-chhiuN khong3-ia2, sim7-chi3 bo5 lang5 keng-ke3 ah?
	13). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, In-ui7 in u7 khi3-sak Goa2 sou2 siat ti7 in e5 bin7-cheng5 e5 lut8-hoat, bo5 thiaN Goa2 e5 siaN, ia7 bo5 kiaN5 i;  14). tok8-tok8 chiau3 in e5 sim e5 kong-ngi7 lai5 kiaN5, koh than3 chiah e5 Pa-lek8, chiu7-si7 in e5 liat8-chou2 sou2 ka3-si7 e5;  15). sou2-i2 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3, an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh chiong in-tin5 hou7 chit e5 peh-siN3 chiah8, koh chiong khou2 e5 chui2 hou7 in lim.  16). Goa2 ia7 beh si3-soaN3 in ti7 liat8-pang-tiong, chiu7-si7 in kap in e5 liat8-chou2 m7-bat e5 pang-kok; ia7 beh hou7 to-kiam3 tui-jip in, kau3 Goa2 it-chin7 chau5-biat8 in.
	17). Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Tioh8 ti3-i3 siuN7, kio3 hiah e5 thoe3 lang5 khau3 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 lai5, ia7 chhe lang5 khi3 chhe7 hiah e5 gau5 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, hou7 in lai5;  18). in tioh8 kin2-kin2 lai5, ui7 lan2 chhut-siaN hau2, hou7 lan2 bak8-sai2 tit8-tit8 lau5, hou7 lan2 e5 bak8-chiu-phe5 chheng3-chhut chui2.  19). In-ui7 thiaN-kiN3 ai-siong e5 siaN tui3 Sek-an chhut, kong2, Lan2 chaiN2-iuN7 soe-pai7! toa7-toa7 kian3-siau3, in-ui7 lan2 li7-khui thou2-toe7, in-ui7 lang5 u7 thiah-hui2 lan2 e5 chhu3-theh8.  20). Lin2 chiah e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 ah, tioh8 thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7, hi7-khang tioh8 thiaN-siu7 I e5 chhui3 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, tioh8 ka3-si7 lin2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 thi5-khau3, tak8-e5 tioh8 ka3-si7 in e5 chhu3-piN chhiuN3 ai-ko.  21). In-ui7 si2-bo5 chiuN7-lai5 lan2 e5 thang-a2-mng5, jip8 lan2 e5 kiong-tian7; tui3 goa7-bin7 chau5-biat8 hiah e5 gin2-na2, tui3 koe-lou7 chau5-biat8 hiah e5 siau3-lian5 lang5.  22). Li2 tioh8 ka7 in kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Lang5 e5 sin-si beh chhin-chhiuN7 pun3-so3, hiat ti7 kau-ia2; koh chhin-chhiuN7 siu-koah e5 lang5 ka-chiah-au7 sou2 ka-lauh8 chit8-pe2-a2 e5 tiu7-a2, bo5 lang5 khioh--i.
	23). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Ti3-hui7 e5 lang5, boh8-tit in-ui7 i e5 ti3-hui7 lai5 khoa-khau2; iong2-beng2 e5 lang5, boh8-tit in-ui7 i e5 iong2-beng2 lai5 khoa-khau2; ho2-giah8 e5 lang5, boh8-tit in-ui7 i e5 ho2-giah8 lai5 khoa-khau2.  24). KiN3-na7 ai3 khoa-khau2--e5, tioh8 in-ui7 chit-e5 lai5 khoa-khau2, chiu7-si7 i bat Goa2, chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, kiaN5 chu5-ai3, kong-peng5, kong-gi7 ti7 toe7--nih-e5; in-ui7 Goa2 liah8 chiah-e5 choe3 hoaN-hi2; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  25). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, KhoaN3 ah, jit8-chi2 beh kau3, Goa2 beh heng5-hoat8 it-chhe3 siu7 kat-le2--e5, bo5 siu7 kat-le2--e5;  26). chiu7-si7 Ai-kip8, Iu5-tai7, I2-tong, A-bun5-chok8, Mou5-ap lang5; kap it-chhe3 khia7-khi2 khong3-ia2 thi3 pin3-piN--e5; in-ui7 liat8-kok long2 bo5 siu7 kat-le2; I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 sim iah8 bo5 siu7 kat-le2.

[10]	I2-sek-liat8 ke ah, tioh8 thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 lin2 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7.  2). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Lin2 m7-thang oh8 liat8-kok e5 sou2-kiaN5; iah8 m7-thang ui7-tioh8 thiN e5 tiau7-thau5 lai5 kiaN-hiaN5; in-ui7 liat8-kok ui7-tioh8 che lai5 kiaN-hiaN5.  3). Cheng3 peh-siN3 e5 hong-siok8 si7 khang-hu; in ti7 chhiu7-na5-lai7 chho3 chit8 chang5 chhiu7, sai-hu7 e5 chhiu2 eng7 pou2-thau5 cho7-chiaN5--e5.  4). In eng7 kim eng7 gun5 siuN--i, eng7 teng kap thui5-a2 teng3-tiau5, hou7 i bo5 io5-tang7.  5). I chhin-chhiuN7 chhia-iN5 e5 thiau7, boe7 kong2-oe7; tioh8 lang5 kng, in-ui7 i boe7 kiaN5; lin2 boh8-tit kiaN--i; in-ui7 in boe7 kang3 chai-e7, iah8 bo5 koan5 thang kang3 hok-khi3.  6). Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, bo5 sim2-mih8 oe7 pi2-pheng7-tit Li2; tok8-tok8 Li2 choe3 toa7; Li2 e5 mia5 toa7 koh u7 leng5-lek8.  7). Ban7 peh-siN3 e5 Ong5 ah, chi7-chui7 m7-tioh8 kiaN-ui3 Li2, che si7 hap8 ti7 Li2; in-ui7 ti7 liat8-kok ti3-hui7 e5 lang5 e5 tiong-kan, sui-jian5 u7 koan5-ui7--e5, iah8 boe7 pi2-tit Li2.  8). In long2 si7 gu5-chhun2 bu5-ti; ngou2-siong7 e5 ka3-si7, put-ko3 si7 chha5 na7-tiaN7.  9). U7 gun5 phah kui phiN3, tui3 Tha-si toa3-lai5-e5; iah8 u7 tui3 OU-hoat lai5 e5 kim; long2 si7 sai-hu7 kap gun5-chhiuN7 e5 chhiu2 choe3--e5; koh u7 lam5-sek chi2-sek e5 liau7 choe3-saN, long2 si7 ki5-khiau2 e5 sai-hu7 choe3--e5.  10). Tok8-tok8 Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 chin e5 Siong7-te3, I si7 oah8 e5 Siong7-te3, si7 eng2-oan2 e5 Ong5; I chit8-e7 siu7-khi3, toe7 chiu7 tin2-tang7; I chit8-e7 thong3-hun7, liat8-kok long2 tong3-boe7-tiau5.
	11). Lin2 tioh8 ka7 in an2-ni kong2, Hiah-e5 m7-si7 chhong3-cho7 thiN-toe7 e5 siong7-te3 long2 beh tui3 toe7-chiuN7 kap thiN-e7 biat8-bo5--khi3.
	12). Ia5-ho5-hoa eng7 leng5-lek8 chhong3-cho7 toe7; eng7 ti3-hui7 kian3-lip8 se3-kai3; eng7 chhang-mia5 tian2-khui chiah e5 thiN.  13). I chit8-e7 chhut siaN, khong-tiong chiu7 u7 choe7-choe7 chui2 kek-tong7; I hou7 hun5-bu7 tui3 toe7-kek8 chheng3--khi2-lai5; I ui7-tioh8 hou7 chhong3-cho7 sih-na3; I hou7 hong tui3 I e5 hu2-khou3 chhut--lai5.  14). Tak8-lang5 long2 gu5-chhun2 bo5 ti3-sek; tak8 e5 gun5-chhiuN7 long2 ui7-tioh8 i tiau-khek e5 ngou2-siong7 lai5 kian3-siau3; in-ui7 i sou2 chu3 e5 ngou2-siong7 si7 ke2--e5, iah8 bo5 oah8-khi3 ti7 i e5 lai7-bin7.  15). Long2 si7 khang-khang--e5; si7 be5-hek8 lang5 e5 sou2 choe3; kau3 pan7-li2 in e5 si5, tek-khak siu7 tu5-biat8.  16). Nga2-kok e5 hun7-giah8 bo5 chhin-chhiuN7 chiah-e5; in-ui7 I si7 chhong3-cho7 ban7-mih8 e5 Chu2; I2-sek-liat8 iah8 si7 I san2-giap8 e5 chi-phai3; ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 I e5 mia5.
	17). Li2 khia7-khi2 siu7-ui5 e5 siaN5--e5, tioh8 tui3 toe7--nih siu-sip8 li2 e5 mih8-kiaN7.  18). In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 chit-si5 beh chiong chit sou2-chai7 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 hiN3--chhut-khi3; koh beh khun3-khou2 in, hou7 in hiau2-ngou7.  19). Goa2 u7 chai-e7 ah, in-ui7 goa2 siu7 hui2-siong, goa2 e5 siong chin siong-tiong7; chong2-si7 goa2 kong2, Che si7 goa2 e5 thong3-khou2, tek-khak tioh8 jim2-siu7.  20). Goa2 e5 pou3-piN5 hui2-hoai7, goa2 e5 soh long2 tng7; goa2 e5 kiaN2-ji5 li7-khui goa2 chhut-khi3, taN long2 bo5--lah; bo5 lang5 koh tah goa2 e5 pou3-piN5, koa3 goa2 e5 tiuN3-pak.  21). In-ui7 bok8-chia2 long2 gu5-chhun2, bo5 chhe7-kiu5 Ia5-ho5-hoa; sou2-i2 boe7 tit-tioh8 heng-thong, in e5 iuN5-kun5 iah8 long2 si3-soaN3.  22). U7 hong-siaN, khoaN3 ah, lai5--lah; u7 toa7 jiau2-loan7 tui3 pak-hng chhut-lai5, beh hou7 Iu5-tai7 chiah e5 siaN5 pha-hng, choe3 ia2-kau2 khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7.  23). Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 chai lang5 e5 lou7, m7-si7 tui3 ka-ki7; kiaN5-lou7 e5 lang5 iah8 boe7 chu2-i3 ka-ki7 e5 kha-pou7.  24). Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 chek-pi7 goa2, tioh8 chiong5-khoan; m7-thang ti7 Li2 e5 siu7-khi3-tiong chek-pi7 goa2; kiaN-liau2 hou7 goa2 kui ti7 bo5--khi3.  25). Goan7 Li2 piaN3-chhut Li2 e5 siu7-khi3 ti7 m7-bat Li2 e5 liat8-kok e5 teng2-bin7, i2-kip8 bo5 kiu5-kio3 Li2 e5 mia5 e5 tak8-chok8; in-ui7 in thun-chiah8 Nga2-kok, thun--i, biat8--i, hou7 i khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7 pha-hng.

[11]	U7 oe7 tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lim5-kau3 Ia5-li7-bi2, kong2,  2). Lin2 tioh8 thiaN chit e5 iok e5 oe7, ka7 Iu5-tai7 lang5 kap Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 kong2.  3). Li2 tui3 in kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 an2-ni kong2, Bo5 thiaN-than3 chit e5 iok e5 oe7 e5 lang5, tioh8 siu7 chiu3-chou2.  4). Chit e5 iok si7 Goa2 chhoa7 lin2 e5 liat8-chou2 chhut Ai-kip8 toe7, thoat-li7 chu3-thih e5 lou5, hit-jit8 sou2 hoan-hu3 in--e5, kong2, Lin2 tioh8 thiaN-than3 Goa2 e5 oe7, chiau3 Goa2 it-chhe3 sou2 hoan-hu3--e5 khi3 kiaN5; an2-ni lin2 chiu7 choe3 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3, Goa2 iah8 choe3 lin2 e5 Siong7-te3.  5). Hou7 Goa2 thang kian-kou3 tui3 lin2 e5 liat8-chou2 sou2 chiu3 e5 choa7; siuN2-su3 in lau5 ni kap bit8 e5 toe7; tu2-tu2 chhin-chhiuN7 kin-a2-jit8 chit8-iuN7; goa2 chiu7 in3 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, A-beng7.
	6). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 goa2 kong2, Li2 tioh8 thoan5 chiah e5 oe7 ti7 Iu5-tai7 chiah e5 siaN5, kap Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 koe-chhi7, kong2, Lin2 tioh8 thiaN chit e5 iok e5 oe7, lai5 kiaN5--i.  7). In-ui7 tui3 Goa2 chhoa7 lin2 liat8-chou2 chhut Ai-kip8 hit chit8 jit8, kau3 kin-a2-jit8, Goa2 chhiat-chhiat keng2-kai3 in, chiu7-si7 cha2-cha2 khi2-lai5 keng2-kai3 in, kong2, Lin2 tioh8 thiaN-than3 Goa2 e5 oe7.  8). Chong2-si7 in m7 thiaN-than3, m7 aN3 hi7-khang; keng2-jian5 tak8-e5 chiau3 ka-ki7 phaiN2-sim e5 kong-ngi7 khi3 kiaN5; sou2-i2 Goa2 hou7 chit e5 iok it-chhe3 chiu3-chou2 e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 in e5 sin-chiuN7; chit e5 iok si7 Goa2 hoan-hu3 in tioh8 kiaN5--e5, chong2-si7 in bo5 kiaN5.
	9). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 goa2 kong2, Ti7 Iu5-tai7 lang5 kap Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 lang5 e5 tiong-kan u7 bou5-poan7 e5 su7.  10). In oat8-tng2 kiaN5 in e5 liat8-chou2 e5 phaiN2, in e5 liat8-chou2 m7-kheng2 thiaN Goa2 e5 oe7; in chiu7 than3 pat8-ho7 e5 siong7-te3 lai5 hok8-sai7 i; I2-sek-liat8 ke kap Iu5-tai7 ke ui5-poe7 Goa2 kap in e5 liat8-chou2 sou2 lip8 e5 iok.  11). Sou2-i2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh hou7 chai-e7 lim5-kau3 in, chiu7-si7 in sou2 boe7 to5-thoat--e5; in beh tui3 Goa2 ai-kiu5, Goa2 m7 thiaN in.  12). Hit-si5 Iu5-tai7 chiah e5 siaN5 e5 lang5, kap Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3, beh khi3 ai-kiu5 in sou2 sio-hiuN lai5 hok8-sai7 hiah e5 siong7-te3; chong2-si7 tu2-tioh8 hoan7-lan7 e5 si5, chiah e5 siong7-te3 long2 boe7-oe7 chin2-kiu3 in.  13). Iu5-tai7 ah, li2 e5 siong7-te3 e5 siau3-giah8, kap li2 e5 siaN5 e5 siau3-giah8 piN5-piN5; li2 ia7 ui7-tioh8 thang kian3-siau3 e5 mih8 lai5 khi2 toaN5, chiau3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 chiah e5 koe-lou7 e5 siau3-giah8; hiah e5 toaN5 chiu7-si7 sio-hiuN ti7 Pa-lek8--e5.  14). Sou2-i2 li2 boh8-tit ui7-tioh8 chit e5 peh-siN3 ki5-to2, boh8-tit ui7-tioh8 in chhut-siaN ki5-kiu5, in-ui7 in tu2-tioh8 hoan7-lan7 ai-kiu5 Goa2 e5 si5, Goa2 bo5 beh thiaN in.
	15). Goa2 sou2 thiaN3--e5, li2 i2-keng kiaN5 phaiN2, li2 ti7 Goa2 e5 chhu3 beh siaN2-su7? he7 goan7, hian3 bah, kiam2 oe7 tu5-khi3 li2 e5 choe7-ok, hou7 li2 hoaN-hi2?  16). Ia5-ho5-hoa bat chheng li2 e5 mia5 choe3 chhiN-chhui3 e5 kaN-na2-chhiu7, ho2-khoaN3, iah8 kiat ho2 ke2-chi2; taN I eng7 hoa7-hoa7-jiong2 e5 siaN, khi2 he2 ti7 i e5 teng2-bin7, ki-oaiN7 iah8 siu7 at-chih8.  17). Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, cha2 chai-poe5 li2--e5, taN beng7-leng7 chai-e7 kong-kek li2; si7 in-ui7 I2-sek-liat8 kap Iu5-tai7 ke kiaN5-phaiN2, ng3 Pa-lek8 sio-hiuN, jia2 Goa2 e5 siu7-khi3; ka-ki7 choe3, ka-ki7 siu7.
	18). Ia5-ho5-hoa chi2-tiam2 goa2, goa2 chiah chai; hit-si5 Li2 chiong in sou2 kiaN5--e5 po3 goa2 khoaN3.  19). Chong2-si7 goa2 chhin-chhiuN7 sun5-liong5 e5 iuN5-a2, khan kau3 siu7 thai5 e5 toe7; goa2 peng7 m7-chai in siat ke3-bou5 beh hai7 goa2, kong2, Lan2 chiong chhiu7 kap ke2-chi2 long2 ka7 i biat8--khi3, chiong i tui3 oah8-lang5 e5 toe7 chian2-tu5--khi3; hou7 i e5 mia5 bo5 koh hou7 lang5 ki3-liam7.  20). Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 si7 chiau3 kong-gi7 phoaN3-toan3, kam3-chhat lang5 e5 sim-pak sin7-tng5--e5; kiu5 Li2 hou7 goa2 khoaN3 Li2 tui3 in po3-siu5, in-ui7 goa2 chiong goa2 e5 an3-kiaN7 pin2-beng5 ti7 Li2.  21). Sou2-i2 Ia5-ho5-hoa lun7-kau3 siau3-siuN7 li2 e5 siN3-mia7 e5 A-na2-tut8 lang5 an2-ni kong2, In kong2, Li2 boh8-tit hong7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5 lai5 chham3-gu2; bian2-tit li2 si2 ti7 goan2 e5 chhiu2-thau5.  22). Sou2-i2 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh heng5-hoat8 in; siau3-lian5 lang5 beh hou7 to thai5-si2; in e5 kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2 beh in-ui7 ki-hng lai5 si2; hou7 in bo5 chhun chit8-e5;  23). in-ui7 pan7-li2 in e5 ni5, Goa2 beh kang3 chai-e7 ti7 A-na2-tut8 lang5.

[12]	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 kap Li2 pian7-lun7 e5 si5, Li2 si7 kong-gi7; chong2-si7 goa2 iau2 ai3 kap Li2 li2-lun7; phaiN2-lang5 e5 lou7 ui7-ho5 heng-thong? toa7 kiaN5 khui2-cha3--e5 ui7-ho5 tit-tioh8 peng5-an?  2). Li2 chai-poe5 in, in iah8 teng3 kun, toa7-chang5 koh kiat ke2-chi2; chiau3 in e5 chhui3 kong2, Li2 si7 kun7; chiau3 in e5 sim siuN7, Li2 si7 hng7.  3). Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 chai goa2, Li2 khoaN3-kiN3 goa2, chhi3-giam7 goa2 ng3 Li2 e5 sim; kiu5 Li2 chiong in thoa--chhut-lai5, chhin-chhiuN7 beh thai5 e5 iuN5; hun-piat--i lai5 theng3-hau7 thai5 e5 jit8.  4). Chit e5 toe7 pi-ai, thong-kok e5 chhau2-chhai3 kou-ta5, beh kau3 ti7-si5 ah? ui7-tioh8 khia7-khi2 hia e5 peh-siN3 e5 phaiN2, cheng-siN pe-chiau2 long2 biat8-bo5; in-ui7 in kong2, I bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 goan2 e5 kiat-kiok8.  5). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Li2 kap pou7-kiaN5 e5 lang5 saN-kap chau2, siong7-chhiaN2 ia3-sian7; thai2-oe7 kap be2 tau3-phau2 ah? li2 ti7 peng5-an e5 toe7, sui-jian5 an-un2, ti7 Iok-tan3 ho5-piN e5 chhiu7-na5 beh an3-chaiN2-iuN7?  6). In-ui7 lian5 li2 e5 hiaN-ti7, lian5 li2 e5 lau7-pe7 e5 ke, long2 eng7 kan-cha3 khoan2-thai7 li2; in iah8 ti7 li2 e5 au7-bin7 toa7-siaN kio3; sui-jian5 tui3 li2 kong2 ho2-oe7, li2 iah8 boh8-tit sin3--in.
	7). Goa2 li7-khui Goa2 e5 chhu3, pang3-sak Goa2 e5 san2-giap8; chiong Goa2 e5 sim sou2 thiaN3--e5, kau ti7 i e5 tui3-tek8 e5 chhiu2.  8). Goa2 e5 san2-giap8 tui3 Goa2 chhin-chhiuN7 chhiu7-na5-lai7 e5 sai; i chhut-siaN kong-kek Goa2, in-ui7 an2-ni Goa2 oan3-hun7 i.  9). Goa2 e5 san2-giap8 tui3 Goa2 kiam2 chhin-chhiuN7 pan-tiam2 e5 eng-chiau2 mah? hiah e5 eng-chiau2 kiam2 ti7 i e5 si3-ui5 kong-kek i mah? lin2 tioh8 khi3 chu7-chip8 chhan5-ia2 e5 pah siu3, hou7 i lai5 thun-chiah8--i.  10). Choe7-choe7 bok8-chia2 hui2-hoai7 Goa2 e5 phu5-to5-hng5, thun2-tah8 Goa2 e5 hun7-giah8; hou7 Goa2 ho2-ho2 e5 hun7-giah8 piN3-choe3 pha-hng e5 khong3-ia2.  11). In hou7 toe7 pha-hng, toe7 i2-keng pha-hng, chiu7 tui3 Goa2 pi-ai; choan5-toe7 pha-hng, in-ui7 bo5 lang5 khoa3-i3.  12). Chan5-hai7--e5 kau3 khong3-ia2-tiong it-chhe3 kng-kho7-kho7 koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7; Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 to, tui3 toe7 e5 chit-peng5 kau3 toe7 e5 hit-peng5, it-chin7 chau5-biat8; kiN3-u7 hiat-khi3--e5, long2 bo5 peng5-an.  13). In cheng3 beh8, siu-seng5 chhi3-phe3; lo5-khou2 iah8 long2 bo5 li7-ek; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 toa7 siu7-khi3, in beh ui7-tioh8 in e5 thou2-san2 lai5 kian3-siau3.
	14). Lun7-kau3 it-chhe3 phaiN2 chhu3-piN, chiu7-si7 hai7-tioh8 Goa2 sou2 hou7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 I2-sek-liat8 seng5-chiap e5 san2-giap8--e5, Ia5-ho5-hoa u7 an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh chiong in puih8-chhut in e5 toe7; koh beh chiong Iu5-tai7 ke tui3 in tiong-kan puih8-chhut--lai5.  15). Goa2 puih8-chhut in i2-au7, Goa2 beh to3-tng2 lai5 lin5-bin2 in; chhoa7 in to3--lai5, tak8-lang5 kui i e5 pun2-giap8, tak8-lang5 kui i e5 pun2 sou2-chai7.  16). In na7 kheng2 un-khun5 hak8-sip8 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 e5 to7-lou7, ki2 Goa2 e5 mia5 chiu3-choa7, kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 oah8--e5, chhin-chhiuN7 in cheng5 ka3-si7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 ki2 Pa-lek8 lai5 chiu3-choa7 chit8-iuN7, in chiu7 beh tit-tioh8 kian3-lip8 ti7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 e5 tiong-kan.  17). In na7 m7 thiaN, chiu7 Goa2 beh puih8-chhut chit-kok, puih8-chhut lai5 biat8--i; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.

[13]	Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 goa2 an2-ni kong2, Li2 tioh8 khi3 boe2 chit8-tiau5 moa5-pou3 e5 toa3 lai5 ha5-io; m7-thang he7 ti7 chui2--nih.  2). Goa2 chiu7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7, boe2 chit8 tiau5 toa3 ha5-io.  3). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 te7-ji7 pai2 lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  4). Tioh8 theh8 li2 sou2 boe2 e5 toa3, chiu7-si7 li2 io--nih e5 toa3, khi2--lai5 khi3 Pek-lah8, ti7-hia khng3--i ti7 chioh8-poaN5 khang.  5). Goa2 chiu7 khi3, khng3 i ti7 Pek-lah8, chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3 goa2--e5.  6). Ke3 choe7-choe7 jit8, Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 goa2 kong2, Li2 khi2--lai5, khi3 Pek-lah8, chiong Goa2 hoan-hu3 li2 khng3 ti7-hia e5 io-toa3 theh8--lai5.  7). Goa2 chiu7 khi3 Pek-lah8 lai5 kut8, tui3 goa2 sou2 khng3 e5 sou2-chai7 theh8 hit tiau5 toa3; khoaN3 ah, hit tiau5 toa3 i2-keng phaiN2--khi3, long2 bo5 lou7-eng7.  8). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  9). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 beh chiau3 an2-ni pai7-hoai7 Iu5-tai7 e5 kiau-ngou7, kap Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 toa7 kiau-ngou7.  10). Chit-e5 phaiN2 e5 peh-siN3 m7-kheng2 thiaN Goa2 e5 oe7, chiau3 in e5 sim e5 kong-ngi7 khi3 kiaN5; koh than3 pat8-ho7 e5 siong7-te3, hok8-sai7 i, kui7-pai3 i; in beh chhin-chhiuN7 chit-tiau5 bo5 lou7-eng7 e5 toa3.  11). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Io-toa3 chaiN2-iuN7 lian5 ti7 lang5 e5 io, Goa2 u7 hou7 I2-sek-liat8 choan5-ke, kap Iu5-tai7 choan5-ke, lian5 ti7 Goa2, iah8 si7 an2-ni; beh hou7 in choe3 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3, choe3 Goa2 e5 mia5-siaN, choe3 Goa2 e5 o-lo2, choe3 Goa2 e5 eng5-kng; chong2-si7 in m7-kheng2 thiaN.
	12). Li2 tioh8 koh tui3 in kong2 chit e5 oe7, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Tak8 e5 ang3 beh toe2 chiu2 moa2-moa2; in beh tui3 li2 kong2, Goan2 kiam2 m7-chai tak8 e5 ang3 beh toe2 chiu2 moa2-moa2 mah?  13). Li2 chiu7 tioh8 tui3 in kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh hou7 chit sou2-chai7 it-chhe3 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3, chiu7-si7 che7 Tai7-pit8 po2-cho7 e5 liat8-ong5, kap che3-si, sian-ti, i2-kip8 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 it-chhe3 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3, long2 toa7-toa7 chiu2-chui3.  14). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 beh hou7 in tai7-ke saN-khap8; chiu7-si7 pe7 kap kiaN2 saN-khap8; Goa2 bo5 beh kho2-lin5, bo5 beh thiaN3-sioh, bo5 beh lin5-bin2, lai5 m7-biat8--i.
	15). Lin2 tioh8 thiaN, tioh8 aN3 hi7-khang; boh8-tit kiau-ngou7, in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa i2-keng kong2--i.  16). OU-am3 be7 kau3, lin2 e5 kha be7 tioh8-tak ti7 ou-am3 e5 soaN, sou2 ng3-bang7 e5 kng iau2-be7 pian3-choe3 si2-bo5 e5 im3-ng2, ou-ou am3-am3 e5 tai7-seng, lin2 tioh8 kui eng5-kng lin2 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  17). Lin2 na7 m7 thiaN chit e5 oe7, chiu7 goa2 e5 sim beh in-ui7 lin2 e5 kiau-ngou7, ti7 un2-bat8 e5 sou2-chai7 thi5-khau3; goa2 e5 bak8-chiu beh bak8-sai2 chhe7-chhe7-to3; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 iuN5-kun5 siu7-liah8.  18). Li2 tioh8 tui3 kun-ong5 kap thai3-hou7 kong2, Lin2 tioh8 khiam-pi, che7 ti7 e7-bin7; in-ui7 lin2 eng5-kng e5 bian2-liu5 tui3 lin2 e5 thau5-khak lak--loh8-khi3.  19). Lam5-hng chiah e5 siaN5 long2 koaiN, bo5 lang5 khui; Iu5-tai7 choan5-chok8 siu7-liah8; koh liah8 kau3 liau2-liau2.
	20). Lin2 tioh8 kiah8-bak8 khoaN3, tui3 pak-hng lai5 e5 lang5; cheng5 sou2 hou7 li2 e5 iuN5-kun5, chiu7-si7 li2 sui2 e5 iuN5-kun5, taN ti7 toh-loh8 ah?  21). Li2 peng5-sou3 sou2 chhin-bit8 e5 peng5-iu2, siat-su2 I siat-lip8 in choe3-thau5 lai5 koan2-hat li2, li2 iau2 u7 sim2-mih8 oe7 thang kong2? thong3-khou2 kiam2 bo5 khiN5-tiau5 li2, chhin-chhiuN7 siN-kiaN2 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5?  22). Li2 na7 sim-lai7 kong2, Che it-chhe3 e5 su7 ui7-ho5 kau3 ti7 goa2 leh? si7 in-ui7 li2 e5 choe7-koa3 chin-tang7, sou2-i2 li2 lou7-the2 chhiah-kha.  23). Kou2-sit8 e5 lang5 oe7 pian3-oaN7 phe5-hu, pa3 oe7 pian3-oaN7 pan-tiam2 mah? Na7 oe7, chiu7 lin2 chiah-e5 koan3-lian7 kiaN5 phaiN2--e5, oe7 kiaN5 ho2.  24). Sou2-i2 Goa2 beh phah-soaN3 in, chhin-chhiuN7 chhau2-iu3 hou7 khong3-ia2 e5 hong chhe--khi3 chit8-iuN7.  25). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Che si7 li2 sou2 eng-kai tu2-tioh8--e5; si7 Goa2 niu5 hou7 li2 e5 hun7-giah8; in-ui7 li2 boe7-ki3-tit Goa2, khi3 oa2-kho3 hu-ke2.  26). Sou2-i2 Goa2 beh hian-khi2 li2 e5 kun5, ta3 ti7 li2 e5 bin7; li2 e5 kian3-siau3 chiu7 lou7-chhut.  27). Li2 hiah-e5 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7, chiu7-si7 ti7 soaN--nih chhan5--nih kiaN5 kan-im5, chhut ki-ki-hau2 e5 siaN, chhiong-ki khoan2 e5 im5-loan7, Goa2 long2 khoaN3-kiN3 lah.  Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 ah, li2 u7 chai-e7; li2 m7-kheng2 chheng-khi3, beh kau3 ti7-si5 ah?

[14]	Lun7-kau3 khong3-han7 e5 su7, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 Ia5-li7-bi2.
	2). Iu5-tai7 pi-ai, siaN5-mng5 soe-pai7, lang5 chheng7 ou-saN che7 ti7 thou5-kha; Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 pi-ai e5 siaN thau3 kau3 teng2-bin7.  3). In e5 se3-ka chhe gin2-na2-kang khi3 chhiuN7-chui2; in kau3 chiN2--nih, chhe7 bo5 chui2; chiu7 toa3 khang e5 khi3-ku7 to3--lai5; kian3-siau3, lau3-khui3, ta3 thau5-khak.  4). Choh-chhan5 lang5 kian3-siau3, ta3 thau5-khak; si7 in-ui7 bo5 loh8 hou7, thou5-toe7 pit-lih8.  5). Chhan5-ia2 e5 lok8-bu2 siN-kiaN2, chiu7 pang3 hiat-kak8; in-ui7 bo5 chhau2.  6). Ia2-lu5 khia7 ti7 kng-kho7-kho7 koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7, chhoan2-khui3 chhin-chhiuN7 ia2-kau2; in-ui7 bo5 chhau2, bak8-chiu sit-beng5.
	7). Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goan2 e5 choe7-koa3 sui-jian5 choe3 kan-cheng3 ko3 goan2; iau2-ku2 kiu5 Li2 ui7-tioh8 Li2 e5 mia5 lai5 choe3 tai7-chi3; goan2 tauh8-tauh8 poe7-gek8, tek-choe7 Li2.  8). I2-sek-liat8 sou2 ng3-bang7--e5, ti7 hoan7-lan7-tiong choe3 Kiu3-chu2--e5 ah, Li2 siaN2-su7 ti7 chit sou2-chai7 chhin-chhiuN7 kia3-kha--e5, koh chhin-chhiuN7 ke3-lou7 lang5 oat8--lai5 hioh ke3-mi5 ah?  9). Li2 siaN2-su7 chhin-chhiuN7 gong5-ngiah8 e5 lang5, chhin-chhiuN7 boe7-oe7 kiu3 lang5 e5 iong2-su7 ah? Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 iu5-goan5 ti7 goan2 tiong-kan; goan2 iah8 chheng-choe3 siok8 Li2 e5 mia5 e5 lang5; m7-thang pang3-sak goan2.
	10). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 chit e5 peh-siN3 an2-ni kong2, In ai3 hong3-tong7, bo5 iok-sok in e5 kha; sou2-i2 Ia5-ho5-hoa m7 chiap-lap8 in, taN beh ki3-tit in e5 choe7-koa3, pan7 in e5 choe7-ok.  11). Ia5-ho5-hoa koh tui3 goa2 kong2, Boh8-tit ui7-tioh8 chit e5 peh-siN3 ki5-to2, kiu5 hok-khi3.  12). In kim3-chiah8 e5 si5, Goa2 m7-thiaN in e5 kiu5-kio3; in hian3 sio-che3 kap le2-mih8, Goa2 iah8 m7 chiap-lap8.  Goa2 hoan2-tng2 beh eng7 to-kiam3, eng7 ki-hng, eng7 un-ek8 lai5 biat8 in.  13). Goa2 chiu7 kong2, Hai7--ah, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, khoaN3 ah, hiah e5 sian-ti tui3 in kong2, Lin2 boe7 khoaN3-kiN3 to-kiam3, iah8 boe7 tu2-tioh8 ki-hng; Ia5-ho5-hoa beh ti7 chit e5 toe7-hng siuN2-su3 lin2 ku2-tng5 e5 peng5-an.  14). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 goa2 kong2, Hiah e5 sian-ti thok Goa2 e5 mia5 thoan5 peh8-chhat8; Goa2 bo5 chhe in, bo5 hoan-hu3 in, iah8 bo5 tui3 in kong2; in thoan5 hou7 lin2--e5, si7 hu-ke2 e5 khe2-si7, kap chiam-pok, kap bo5-iaN2 e5 su7, i2-kip8 in e5 sim e5 khui2-cha3.  15). Sou2-i2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Lun7-kau3 thok Goa2 e5 mia5 lai5 thoan5-pou3 e5 hiah e5 sian-ti, Goa2 peng7-bo5 chhe in, in iau2-ku2 kong2, Chit e5 toe7 boe7-oe7 tu2-tioh8 to-kiam3, ki-hng; ki5-sit8 hiah e5 sian-ti beh tui3 to-kiam3 ki-hng lai5 biat8-bo5.  16). Koh thiaN in thoan5-pou3 e5 peh-siN3, beh in-ui7 ki-hng to-kiam3 siu7 hiat-kak8 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 koe-lou7; in kap bou2 kap kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2, long2 bo5 lang5 bai5-chong3; Goa2 beh chiong in e5 phaiN2 piaN3 ti7 in e5 sin-chiuN7.  17). Li2 tioh8 chiong chit e5 oe7 ka7 in kong2, Goan7 goa2 e5 bak8-sai2 jit8-mi5 lau5 bo5 soah; in-ui7 goa2 e5 peh-siN3 tu2-tioh8 toa7 hui2-siong, phah kau3 chin-thiam2.  18). Goa2 na7 chhut-khi3 chhan5--nih, chiu7 khoaN3-kiN3 u7 hou7 to thai5--e5; goa2 na7 jip8 siaN5, chiu7 khoaN3-kiN3 u7 tui3 ki-hng lai5 phoa3-piN7--e5; sian-ti kap che3-si ti7 kok-lai7 si3-koe3 kiaN5, iah8 long2 boe7 hiau2-tit.
	19). Li2 it-chin7 khi3-sak Iu5-tai7 mah? Li2 e5 sim iam3-ouN3 Sek-an mah? siaN2-su7 phah goan2, iah8 bo5 thang tit-tioh8 i-ho2? Goan2 ng3-bang7 peng5-an, iah8 bo5 u7 hok-khi3; ng3-bang7 i-ti7 e5 ki-hoe7, bo5 phah-sng3 tu2-tioh8 kiaN-hiaN5.  20). Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goan2 jin7 ka-ki7 e5 choe7-ok, kap goan2 e5 liat8-chou2 e5 choe7-koa3; in-ui7 goan2 tek-choe7 Li2.  21). Kiu5 Li2 in-ui7 Li2 e5 mia5 e5 ian5-kou3, boh8-tit iam3-ouN3 goan2; boh8-tit leng5-jiok8 Li2 eng5-kng e5 po2-cho7; kiu5 Li2 tui-liam7, boh8-tit poe7 Li2 kap goan2 sou2 lip8 e5 iok.  22). Goa7-pang bo5-iaN2-chiah e5 sin5-beng5, u7 chit8-e5 oe7 loh8-hou7 mah? thiN oe7 ka-ki7 loh8 toa7-hou7 mah? Ia5-ho5-hoa goan2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, oe7 an2-ni--e5, kiam2 m7-si7 Li2 mah? sou2-i2 goan2 iu5-goan5 beh theng3-hau7 Li2; in-ui7 che long2 si7 Li2 sou2 choe3--e5.

[15]	Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 goa2 kong2, Sui-jian5 u7 Mou5-se kap Sat-bou2-jiN2 khia7 ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5, thoe3 in kiu5, Goa2 e5 sim iah8 bo5 koan3-kou3 chit e5 peh-siN3; tioh8 koaN2 in li7-khui Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5, hou7 in chhut--khi3.  2). In na7 tui3 li2 kong2, Goan2 tioh8 chhut-khi3 toh-loh8? li2 tioh8 ka7 in kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Kai si2--e5 tioh8 si2; kai hou7 to thai5--e5, tioh8 hou7 to thai5; kai tu2-tioh8 ki-hng--e5, tioh8 tu2-tioh8 ki-hng; kai hou7 lang5 liah8--e5, tioh8 hou7 lang5 liah8.  3). Ia5-ho5-hoa koh kong2, Goa2 tiau-chhoan5 si3-hang7 lai5 pan7--in; chiu7-si7 to lai5 thai5--in, kau2 lai5 thoa--in, khong-tiong e5 chiau2, toe7-chiuN7 e5 ia2-siu3, chiah8 lai5 biat8 in.  4). Koh beh hou7 in liu5-loh8 ti7 thiN-e7 ban7-kok tiong; long2 si7 in-ui7 Iu5-tai7 ong5 Hi-se-ka e5 kiaN2 Ma2-na2-se ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 sou2 kiaN5 e5 su7.
	5). Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 ah, chi7-chui7 kho2-lin5 li2 ah? chi7-chui7 ui7 li2 pi-siong ah? chi7-chui7 oat8-tng2-sin mng7 li2 peng5-an--bo5?  6). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Li2 khi3-choat8 Goa2, oat8-tng2-sin the3-au7; in-ui7 an2-ni, Goa2 chhun-chhiu2 kong-kek li2, hui2-hoai7 li2; Goa2 lin5-bin2 li2 kau3 ia3.  7). Goa2 ti7 keng2-lai7 tak8 e5 siaN5 mng5-khau2, eng7 poa3-ki poa3--in; Goa2 choat8 in e5 hou7-su5, Goa2 biat8 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3, in iu5-goan5 bo5 oat8-tng2 li7-khui in e5 lou7.  8). In e5 koaN2-hu7 ke-thiN ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5, pi2 hai2-soa khah-choe7; Goa2 hou7 chan5-hai7--e5 tiong-tau3 lai5, kong-kek siau3-lian5 lang5 e5 lau7-bu2; hou7 thong3-khou2 kiaN-hiaN5 hut-jian5 kau3 i e5 sin-chiuN7.  9). SiN chhit e5 kiaN2 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, soe-lam2 khui3-tng7; tng-thau5 peh8-jit8, i e5 jit8-thau5 hut-jian5 loh8, i lau3-khui3 kian3-siau3; sou2 chhun e5 peh-siN3, Goa2 beh ti7 in e5 tui3-tek8 e5 bin7-cheng5, kau hou7 to-kiam3; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	10). goa2 e5 lau7-bu2 ah, goa2 u7 chai-e7; in-ui7 li2 siN goa2 choe3 chit8-e5 kap choan5-toe7 saN cheng-pian7 ke3-kau3 e5 lang5; goa2 peng5-sou3 bo5 eng7 gun5 chioh lang5, lai5 theh8 li7-sek; lang5 iah8 bo5 eng7 gun5 chioh goa2, lai5 theh8 li7-sek; chong2-si7 lang5 long2 chiu3-chou2 goa2.  11). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 chin-chiaN3 beh kian-kou3 li2, hou7 li2 tit-tioh8 hok-khi3; chai-e7 khou2-lan7 lim5-kau3 e5 si5, Goa2 chin-chiaN3 beh hou7 tui3-tek8 kiu5 li2.
	12). Thih, chiu7-si7 pak-hng e5 thih, kap tang5, lang5 kiam2 oe7 at-chih8--i mah?  13). In-ui7 li2 e5 choe7-ok, Goa2 beh ti7 li2 e5 si3-keng2-lai7 hou7 li2 e5 he3-chai5 po2-mih8 peh8-peh8 hou7 lang5 chhiuN2--khi3.  14). Goa2 iah8 beh hou7 tui3-tek8 toa3 in kau3 li2 sou2 m7-bat e5 toe7; in-ui7 Goa2 ti7 siu7-khi3-tiong u7 hoat-chhut he2, beh ka7 lin2 sio-lio--khi3.
	15). Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 chai, kiu5 Li2 ki3-liam7 goa2, koan3-kou3 goa2, ka7 goa2 po3 oan-siu5 ti7 hiah e5 khun2-pek goa2 e5; Li2 khoan-iong5 e5 si5, m7-thang liah8 goa2 khi3; tioh8 chai goa2 ui7-tioh8 Li2 e5 ian5-kou3 siu7 leng5-jiok8.  16). Ban7-kun e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 tit-tioh8 Li2 e5 oe7 chiu7 chiah8--i; Li2 e5 oe7 ti7 goa2 si7 choe3 goa2 sim-lai7 e5 hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8; in-ui7 goa2 si7 chheng-choe3 siok8 Li2 e5 mia5--e5.  17). Goa2 bo5 che7-ti7 ian3-lok8 e5 lang5 e5 hoe7-tiong, lai5 khoai3-lok8; goa2 in-ui7 Li2 e5 kam2-tong7, ka-ki7 cheng7-cheng7 che7; in-ui7 Li2 eng7 siu7-khi3 chhiong-moa2 goa2.  18). Goa2 e5 thong3-khou2 chaiN2-iuN7 ku2-tng5 bo5 soah? goa2 e5 siong chaiN2-iuN7 boe7-i--tit, i-boe7-ho2 ah? Li2 khoan2-thai7 goa2 kiam2 beh chhin-chhiuN7 khi-phian3 e5 khoe, kho3-boe7-chu7 e5 chui2 ah?
	19). Sou2-i2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Li2 na7 to3-tng2--lai5, Goa2 chiu7 beh hou7 li2 to3-tng2--lai5 khia7 ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5; li2 na7 tui3 ha7-chian7 e5 tiong-kan keng2 po2-kui3--e5 chhut-lai5, li2 chiu7 beh choe3 chhin-chhiuN7 Goa2 e5 chhui3; in tek-khak beh kui-ng3 li2, chong2-si7 li2 m7-thang kui-ng3 in.  20). Goa2 beh hou7 li2 tui3 ti7 chit e5 peh-siN3 chiaN5-choe3 kian-kou3 e5 tang5 chhiuN5; in beh kong-kek li2, chong2-si7 boe7 iaN5 li2, in-ui7 Goa2 kap li2 ti7-teh, beh chin2-kiu3 li2, khan-kiu3 li2; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  21). Goa2 beh khan-kiu3 li2 thoat-li7 phaiN2-lang5 e5 chhiu2, kiu3-siok8 li2 thoat-li7 kiong5-po7 e5 lang5 e5 chhiu2-thau5.

[16]	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 koh lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  2). Li2 ti7 chit sou2-chai7 m7-thang chhoa7-bou2, siN kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2.  3). In-ui7 lun7-kau3 chit sou2-chai7 sou2 siN e5 kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2, koh lun7-kau3 chit e5 kok-lai7 siN--in e5 pe7-bu2, Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2:  4). In beh tu2-tioh8 tang7-piN7 lai5 si2; bo5 lang5 thi5-khau3; boe7 tit-tioh8 bai5-chong3; beh ti7 toe7-chiuN7 chhin-chhiuN7 pun3-so3; koh beh tui3 to-kiam3, tui3 ki-hng lai5 biat8-bo5; in e5 sin-si beh hou7 khong-tiong e5 pe-chiau2, kap toe7-chiuN7 e5 ia2-siu3 choe3 chiah8-mih8.  5). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Boh8-tit jip8 song-su7 e5 ke, boh8-tit khi3 ka7 i thi5-khau3, iah8 boh8-tit ui7 in pi-siong; in-ui7 Goa2 chiong Goa2 e5 peng5-an, chiu7-si7 un-tian2 kap lin5-bin2, tui3 chit e5 peh-siN3 chhiuN2--khi3; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  6). Tui3 toa7 kau3 soe3, beh si2 ti7 chit e5 toe7-hng; boe7 tit-tioh8 bai5-chong3; bo5 lang5 ui7 in thi5-khau3, iah8 bo5 lang5 ui7 in koah-bah, thi3 kng thau5.  7). In tu2-tioh8 song-su7, bo5 lang5 ui7 in peh-piaN2, in-ui7 si2-lang5 lai5 an-ui3 in; in si2-pe7 si2-bu2, iah8 bo5 lang5 eng7 an-ui3 e5 poe hou7 in lim.  8). Li2 iah8 m7-thang jip8 ian3-lok8 e5 ke, kap in che7-teh lim-chiah8.  9). In-ui7 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3, an2-ni kong2, Lin2 iau2 oah8-teh e5 jit8, ti7 lin2 e5 bak8-cheng5, Goa2 beh hou7 hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN, khoai3-lok8 e5 siaN, sin-kiaN2-sai3 e5 siaN, sin-niu5 e5 siaN ti7 chit sou2-chai7 long2 soah.  10). Li2 chiong chiah e5 it-chhe3 e5 oe7 chi2-si7 chit e5 peh-siN3; in tui3 li2 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa siaN2-su7 kong2, Beh kang3-loh8 chit e5 toa7 chai-e7 kong-kek goan2 ah? goan2 u7 sim2-mih8 choe7-koa3? goan2 u7 sim2-mih8 choe7-koa3, tek-choe7 goan2 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah?  11). Li2 tioh8 ka7 in kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, In-ui7 lin2 e5 liat8-chou2 pang3-sak Goa2, khi3 than3 pat8-ho7 e5 siong7-te3, hok8-sai7 in, kui7-pai3 in;  12). koh pang3-sak Goa2, bo5 siu2 Goa2 e5 lut8-hoat; koh lin2 kiaN5-phaiN2, pi2 lin2 e5 liat8-chou2 khah-phaiN2; khoaN3 ah, lin2 tak8-lang5 than3 phaiN2-sim e5 kong-ngi7 khi3 kiaN5; sim7-chi3 bo5 thiaN-than3 Goa2.  13). Sou2-i2 Goa2 beh koaN2 lin2 chhut chit sou2-chai7, kau3 lin2 i2-kip8 lin2 e5 liat8-chou2 sou2 m7-bat e5 toe7; ti7-hia lin2 beh jit8-mi5 hok8-sai7 pat8-ho7 e5 siong7-te3; ti7-hia Goa2 bo5 beh si-un hou7 lin2.
	14). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, KhoaN3 ah, jit8-chi2 beh kau3, lang5 ki2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 eng2-oah8 lai5 chiu3-choa7, bo5 beh kong2, I si7 chhoa7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 hou7-e3 tui3 Ai-kip8 toe7 chiuN7--lai5-e5;  15). in ki2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 eng2-oah8 lai5 chiu3-choa7, si7 beh kong2, I chhoa7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 hou7-e3 tui3 pak-hng e5 toe7, iah8 tui3 kiN3-na7 I sou2 koaN2 in kau3 e5 toe7 chiuN7--lai5; koh Goa2 beh chhoa7 in to3-lai5 in e5 toe7, chiu7-si7 Goa2 cheng5 sou2 siuN2-su3 in e5 liat8-chou2--e5.  16). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh tiau3 choe7-choe7 liah8-hi5--e5 lai5 liah8 in; jian5-au7 Goa2 beh tiau3 choe7-choe7 phah-lah8--e5, tui3 chiah e5 soaN, chiah e5 soaN-thau5, chiah e5 chioh8-khang, lai5 phah in.  17). In-ui7 Goa2 e5 bak8-chiu teh khoaN3 in it-chhe3 e5 kiaN5-choe3; in bo5 jia-kham3 ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5; in e5 choe7-koa3 iah8 bo5 khng3-bat8 ti7 Goa2 e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5.  18). Goa2 beh tai7-seng ka-ki7 po3-eng3 in e5 choe7-koa3 kap choe7-ok; in-ui7 in eng7 thang iam3-chian7--e5 e5 sin-si phah la5-sam5 Goa2 e5 thou2-toe7; koh eng7 in kho2-ouN3 e5 mih8 chhiong-moa2 Goa2 e5 san2-giap8.  19). Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 si7 Goa2 e5 khui3-lat8, si7 Goa2 e5 oe7-sou2; ti7 khou2-lan7 e5 jit8, si7 goa2 to5-siam2 e5 sou2-chai7; liat8-kok e5 lang5 beh tui3 toe7-kek8 lai5 li2 chia, kong2, U7-iaN2 ah, goan2 e5 liat8-chou2 sou2 seng5-chiap-e5 put-ko3 si7 hu-ke2, ki5-tiong bo5 u7 li7-ek--e5.  20). Lang5 kiam2 thang ui7 ka-ki7 cho7 siong7-te3 mah? in sit8-chai7 m7-si7 Siong7-te3.  21). KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 chiong chi2-chit-pai2 hou7 in chai; Goa2 beh hou7 in chai Goa2 e5 chhiu2-toaN7 kap Goa2 e5 leng5-lek8; in chiu7 beh chai Goa2 e5 mia5 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.

[17]	Iu5-tai7 e5 choe7 si7 eng7 thih-pit, eng7 soan7-chioh8 pit-be2 ki3--e5; chiu7-si7 khek ti7 in e5 sim e5 pi, toaN5 e5 kak.  2). In e5 kiaN2 ki3-liam7 in koaiN5-soaN-teng2, chhiN-chhui3 chhiu7-piN e5 toaN5, kap ngou2-siong7.  3). Goa2 chhan5--nih e5 soaN ah, Goa2 beh in-ui7 li2 ti7 si3-keng2-lai7 sou2 hoan7 e5 choe7, chiong li2 e5 he3-mih8, chai5-po2 kap soaN-thau5 e5 toaN5, long2 hou7 lang5 chhiuN2-khi3.  4). Koh li2 ui7-tioh8 pun2-sin, beh chiong Goa2 sou2 siuN2-su3 e5 san2-giap8 pang3 he7-teh; Goa2 iah8 beh hou7 li2 ti7 sou2 m7-bat e5 toe7 hok8-sai7 li2 e5 tui3-tek8; in-ui7 lin2 kek Goa2 siu7-khi3 e5 he2, tit8-tit8 toh8 kau3 eng2-oan2.
	5). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KiN3-na7 oa2-kho3 lang5, eng7 jiok8-the2 choe3 i e5 chhiu2, i e5 sim li7-khui Ia5-ho5-hoa--e5, hit-ho7 lang5 siu7 chiu3-chou2.  6). In-ui7 i beh chhin-chhiuN7 khong3-ia2 e5 tou7-siong5; hok-khi3 kau3 e5 si5, i khoaN3-boe7-tioh8; beh tiam3 ti7 soa-bou5 ta-so3 e5 sou2-chai7, bo5 lang5 khia7-khi2 e5 kiam5-toe7.  7). Oa2-kho3 Ia5-ho5-hoa, liah8 Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3 i sou2 oa2-kho3--e5 hit-ho7 lang5 u7 hok-khi3.  8). I beh chhin-chhiuN7 chui2-piN sou2 chai e5 chhiu7, soan i e5 kun ti7 ho5-piN; iam7-jiat8 kau3 iah8 bo5 kiaN; hioh8 iu5-goan5 beh chhiN-chhui3; ti7 ta-so3 e5 ni5, long2 bo5 khoa3-lu7; koh kiat ke2-chi2 bo5 soah.  9). Lang5 e5 sim pi2 ban7-mih8 khah khui2-khiat, phaiN2 kau3 kek8-thau5; chi7-chui7 oe7 chai i ah?  10). Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 kam3-chhat lang5 e5 sim; chhi3-giam7 lang5 e5 chong7-hu2--e5; beh chiau3 tak8-lang5 sou2 kiaN5--e5, kap i choe3 tai7-chi3 e5 kiat-ko2, lai5 po3-eng3 i.  11). Lang5 bo5 chiau3 cheng3-to7 tit-tioh8 chiN5, chhin-chhiuN7 chia3-kou pu7 m7-si7 i siN e5 nng7; kau3 tiong-lian5, hit e5 chiN5 long2 beh li7-khui i, i e5 kiat-kiok8 chiaN5-choe3 gu5-gong7.
	12). Goan2 e5 seng3-sou2 si7 eng5-kng e5 po2-cho7; tui3 khi2-thau5 an-ti3 ti7 koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7.  13). I2-sek-liat8 sou2 ng3-bang7 e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiN3-na7 khi3-sak Li2--e5, long2 beh kian3-siau3; kiN3-na7 li7-khui Li2--e5, in e5 mia5 beh ki3 ti7 thou5--nih; in-ui7 in khi3-sak Ia5-ho5-hoa, oah8-chui2 e5 goan5-thau5.  14). Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 i-ti7 goa2, goa2 chiu7 tit-tioh8 i-ho2; chin2-kiu3 goa2, goa2 chiu7 tit-tioh8 kiu3; in-ui7 Li2 si7 goa2 sou2 o-lo2--e5.  15). KhoaN3 ah, lang5 tui3 goa2 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 ti7 toh-loh8? taN tioh8 hou7 i lai5.  16). Lun7-kau3 goa2, goa2 bo5 kin2-kin2 khi3-sak bok8-chia2 e5 chit, m7 te3--Li2; chai-e7 kau3 e5 jit8, m7-si7 goa2 sou2 ai3; che si7 Li2 sou2 chai, goa2 e5 chhui3 sou2 kong2--e5, long2 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5.  17). Boh8-tit choe3 hou7 goa2 kiaN-hiaN5-e5; tng hoan7-lan7 e5 jit8. Li2 choe3 goa2 to5-siam2 e5 sou2-chai7.  18). Hou7 hiah e5 khun2-pek goa2--e5 kian3-siau3, boh8-tit hou7 goa2 kian3-siau3; hou7 in kiaN-hiaN5, boh8-tit hou7 goa2 kiaN-hiaN5; hou7 chai-e7 e5 jit8 lim5-kau3 in, eng7 ka-pe7 e5 hui2-hoai7 lai5 hui2-hoai7 in.
	19). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 goa2 an2-ni kong2, Li2 khi3 khia7 ti7 cheng3 peh-siN3 e5 mng5, chiu7-si7 Iu5-tai7 liat8-ong5 tui3-hia jip8, tui3-hia chhut--e5; koh khia7 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 chiah e5 mng5.  20). Tui3 in kong2, Lin2 chiah e5 Iu5-tai7 ong5, kap Iu5-tai7 cheng3-lang5, kap Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 it-chhe3 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3, hoan7-na7 tui3 chiah e5 mng5 jip8--e5, long2 tioh8 thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7.  21). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Lin2 tioh8 ka-ki7 kin2-sin7, boh8-tit ti7 an-hioh-jit8 taN-taN3, ia7 boh8-tit un7 jip8 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 chiah e5 siaN5-mng5.  22). Iah8 boh8-tit ti7 an-hioh-jit8 tui3 ke-lai7 taN-taN3 chhut-khi3, bo5-lun7 sim2-mih8 kang long2 m7-thang choe3; tok8-tok8 tioh8 liah8 an-hioh-jit8 choe3 seng3-jit8, chiau3 Goa2 peng5-sou3 hoan-hu3 lin2 e5 liat8-chou2--e5.  23). Chong2-si7 in m7 thiaN-than3, m7 aN3 hi7-khang; chiu7-si7 ngi7 in e5 am7-kun2, ti3-kau3 boe7 thiaN, boe7 siu7 ka3-si7.  24). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Lin2 na7 liu5-sim thiaN-than3 Goa2, ti7 an-hioh-jit8 bo5 taN sim2-mih8 taN3 jip8 chit e5 siaN5 chiah e5 mng5; tok8-tok8 liah8 an-hioh-jit8 choe3 seng3-jit8, ti7 hit-jit8 long2 bo5 choe3 sim2-mih8 kang;  25). chiu7 u7 kun-ong5, ong5-chhin, che7 Tai7-pit8 e5 po2-cho7--e5, in kap in e5 ong5-chhin kap Iu5-tai7 lang5 kap Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3, hek8-si7 che7-chhia, hek8-si7 khia5-be2, jip8 chit e5 siaN5 chiah e5 mng5; koh chit e5 siaN5 beh lau5 kau3 eng2-oan2.  26). Iah8 beh u7 lang5 tui3 Iu5-tai7 chiah e5 siaN5, kap Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 si3-ui5 e5 sou2-chai7, tui3 Pian7-nga2-bin2 toe7, piN5-iuN5, soaN-toe7, kap lam5-hng e5 toe7 lai5; long2 toa3 sio-che3, tak8-iuN7 e5 che3, sou3-che3, kap ju2-hiuN, kap sia7-un che3, kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3.  27). Lin2 na7 m7 thiaN-than3 Goa2, m7 liah8 an-hioh-jit8 choe3 seng3-jit8; iu5-goan5 ti7 an-hioh-jit8 taN-taN3 jip8 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 tak8 e5 mng5; Goa2 beh ti7 tak8 e5 mng5 khi2 he2; chit e5 he2 iah8 beh sio-hui2 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 kiong-tian7, boe7-oe7 phah-hoa.

[18]	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 Ia5-li7-bi2 kong2,  2). Li2 khi2--lai5, loh8--khi3 sio-hui5 lang5 e5 chhu3; Goa2 ti7-hia beh hou7 li2 thiaN Goa2 e5 oe7.  3). Goa2 chiu7 loh8---khi3 sio-hui5 lang5 e5 chhu3; tu2-tng7 i eng7 lun5 teh tng2, choe3 i e5 kang.  4). Sio-hui5 lang5 eng7 thou5 choe3 e5 khi3-ku7, ti7 i e5 chhiu2 na7 phaiN2-khi3, i chiu7 eng7 hit te3 thou5 leng7-goa7 choe3 pat8-ho7 e5 khi3-ku7; chiau3 sio-hui5 lang5 sou2 khoaN3-choe3 ho2--e5 lai5 choe3--i.
	5). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 chiu7 lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  6). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, I2-sek-liat8 ke ah, Goa2 khoan2-thai7 lin2 kiam2 boe7-oe7 chhin-chhiuN7 chit e5 sio-hui5 lang5 e5 sou2-choe3 mah? I2-sek-liat8 ke ah, thou5 ti7 sio-hui5 lang5 e5 chhiu2-tiong chaiN2-iuN7, lin2 ti7 Goa2 e5 chhiu2-tiong iah8 si7 an2-ni.  7). Goa2 sim2-mih8 si5 lun7-kau3 chit8-chok8 a2-si7 chit8-kok kong2, Goa2 beh ka7 i puih8--khi2-lai5, ka7 i thiah-hui2, ka7 i hui2-hoai7;  8). Goa2 sou2 kong2 e5 hit-chit8-chok8, na7 hoan2-hoe2 li7-khui i e5 phaiN2, Goa2 chiu7 beh the3-hoe2 sou2 siuN7 beh kang3 hou7 in e5 chai-e7.  9). Goa2 sim2-mih8 si5 lun7-kau3 chit8-chok8 a2-si7 chit8-kok, kong2 beh kian3-lip8, beh chai-cheng3;  10). in na7 kiaN5 Goa2 khoaN3-choe3 phaiN2 e5 su7, m7 thiaN-than3 Goa2 e5 oe7, Goa2 chiu7 beh the3-hoe2 Goa2 sou2 kong2 beh hou7 in e5 hok-khi3.  11). TaN li2 tioh8 ka7 Iu5-tai7 lang5 kap khia7-khi2 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 peh-siN3 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 pi7-pan7 chai-e7 kong-kek lin2, iah8 siat ke3-bou5 kong-kek lin2; lin2 tak8-lang5 tioh8 oat8-thau5, li7-khui i e5 phaiN2-lou7, koe2-chiaN3 lin2 e5 sou2-kiaN5 lin2 e5 sou2-choe3.  12). Chong2-si7 in kong2, Bo5 ng3-bang7; goan2 beh chiau3 ka-ki7 e5 ke3-bou5 lai5 kiaN5, tak8-lang5 chiau3 i phaiN2-sim e5 kong-ngi7 lai5 choe3.
	13). Sou2-i2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Lin2 tioh8 khi3 tak8-kok chha5-mng7, khoaN3 chi7-chui7 thiaN-kiN3 chit-ho7 su7; I2-sek-liat8 e5 peh-siN3 u7 kiaN5 kek8 thang iam3-ouN3 e5 su7.  14). Li7-pa-lun3 e5 seh tui3 chhan5-ia2 e5 chioh8-poaN5 kiam2 oe7 choat8-tng7 mah? tui3 hng7-hng7 e5 sou2-chai7 lau5-loh8 e5 leng2-chui2 kiam2 oe7 ta--khi3 mah?  15). In-ui7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 boe7-ki3--tit Goa2, ng3 hu-ke2 e5 sin5 sio-hiuN; in hou7 in ti7 sou2 kiaN5 e5 lou7, ti7 ku7 e5 lou7 tak--tioh8, hou7 in kiaN5 phian-lou7, bo5 thun7-koaiN5-e5;  16). ti3-kau3 in e5 toe7 choe3 thang gong5-ngiah8, tng5-tng5 hou7 lang5 thi2-chhio3; kiN3-na7 tui3-hia ke3--e5 beh gong5-ngiah8 io5 thau5.  17).
