Goa2 beh chhin-chhiuN7 eng7 tang-hong ti7 tui3-tek8 e5 bin7-cheng5 koaN2-soaN3 in; in tu2-tioh8 hoan7-lan7 e5 jit8, Goa2 beh eng7 ka-chiah ng3 in, bo5 beh eng7 bin7.
	18). In chiu7 kong2, Lai5--ah, lan2 lai5 siat ke3-bou5 kong-kek Ia5-li7-bi2; in-ui7 che3-si u7 lut8-hoat, ti3-hui7 e5 lang5 u7 ke3-ek8, sian-ti u7 chham3-gu2 e5 oe7, long2 boe7 choat8-tng7.  Lai5--ah, lan2 tioh8 eng7 chih8 tu2-tak i, i e5 oe7 long2 m7-bian2 thiaN i.
	19). Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 ti3-i3 goa2, ia7 thiaN hiah e5 kap goa2 cheng-pian7 e5 lang5 e5 oe7.  20). Kiam2 thang eng7 phaiN2 po3 ho2 mah? in-ui7 in khui ham7-khiN beh hai7 goa2 e5 siN3-mia7.  Kiu5 Li2 ki3--tit goa2 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 thoe3 in kiu5 hok-khi3, hou7 Li2 e5 toa7 siu7-khi3 tui3 in oat8-to3-tng2.  21). Goan7 Li2 chiong in e5 kiaN2-ji5 kau hou7 ki-hng, chiong in kau hou7 to-kiam3; hou7 in e5 bou2 bo5 kiaN2, choe3 koaN2-hu7; hou7 in e5 ta-pou-lang5 hou7 si2-bo5 sou2 biat8, in e5 siau3-lian5 lang5 ti7 chian3-tin7 hou7 to thai5-si2.  22). Li2 hou7 kun-tui7 hut-jian5 lim5-kau3 in e5 si5, goan7 tui3 in e5 chhu3 thiaN-kiN3 thi5-khau3 e5 siaN; in-ui7 in kut8 ham7-khiN beh liah8 goa2, siat lo5-bang7 beh poaN3 goa2 e5 kha.  23). Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, in beh hai7 goa2 hiah e5 ke3-bou5, Li2 long2 chai; boh8-tit sia3-bian2 in e5 choe7-koa3; iah8 boh8-tit tui3 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 chhat-siau in e5 choe7-ok; tioh8 hou7 in ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 poah8-to2; Li2 siu7-khi3 e5 si5, tioh8 pan7--in.

[19]	Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Li2 khi3 boe2 sio-hui5 lang5 e5 hui5-pan5, koh chhoa7 peh-siN3 e5 lau7-toa7,  2). kap che3-si tiong e5 lau7-toa7, chhut-khi3 Pian7-him-lun3 e5 soaN-kok, Hap-jiN2-se e5 mng5-khau2 hia, soan-pou3 Goa2 sou2 hoan-hu3 li2 e5 oe7,  3). kong2, Iu5-tai7 e5 liat8-ong5 kap Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 ah, tioh8 thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7; ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3, an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh hou7 chai-e7 lim5-kau3 chit e5 toe7-hng, hoan7-na7 thiaN e5 lang5, in e5 hi7-khang tek-khak tio7.  4). In-ui7 in khi3-sak Goa2, khoaN3 chit e5 sou2-chai7 chhin-chhiuN7 goa7-pang; koh ti7-chia sio-hiuN hou7 pat8 e5 siong7-te3, chiu7-si7 in cheng5 sou2 m7-bat-e5; in e5 liat8-chou2, i2-kip8 Iu5-tai7 liat8-ong5, ia7 si7 an2-ni; koh hou7 bo5-choe7 e5 lang5 e5 huih pian3-moa2 chit e5 toe7-hng.  5). Koh ui7 Pa-lek8 khi2 soaN-thau5 e5 toaN5, thang ti7 he2-tiong sio in e5 kiaN2, choe3 sio-che3 lai5 hian3 hou7 Pa-lek8.  Che m7-si7 Goa2 sou2 beng7-leng7--e5, m7-si7 Goa2 sou2 the5-khi2--e5, iah8 m7-si7 Goa2 e5 sim sou2-siuN7--e5.  6). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, In-ui7 an2-ni, jit8-chi2 beh kau3, chit e5 toe7-hng bo5 koh chheng-choe3 To5-hui-tek8 kap Pian7-him-lun3 e5 soaN-kok; hoan2-tng2 chheng-choe3 Sat-liok8 e5 soaN-kok.  7). Goa2 beh ti7 chit e5 toe7-hng hou7 Iu5-tai7 kap Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 ke3-bou5 kui ti7 khang-khang; iah8 beh hou7 in ti7 tui3-tek8 e5 bin7-cheng5 to2 ti7 to-e7, kap siau3-siuN7 in e5 siN3-mia7 e5 lang5 e5 chhiu2-thau5; in e5 sin-si, Goa2 beh hou7 khong-tiong e5 pe-chiau2, kap toe7-chiuN7 e5 ia2-siu3 choe3 chiah8-mih8.  8). Goa2 beh hou7 chit e5 siaN5 choe3 thang gong5-ngiah8 thang thi2-chhio3--e5; hoan7-na7 keng-ke3 e5 lang5 beh in-ui7 chit e5 siaN5 sou2 tu2-tioh8 e5 chai-e7, lai5 gong5-ngiah8 thi2-chhio3.  9). Goa2 beh hou7 in ti7 ui5-khun3 khun2-pek e5 tiong-kan, chiu7-si7 tui3-tek8 kap siau3-siuN7 in e5 siN3-mia7 e5 lang5 khun2-pek in e5 si5, tak8-lang5 chiah8 in e5 kiaN2 e5 bah, cha-bou2-kiaN2 e5 bah, kap peng5-iu2 e5 bah.  10). Kong2 soah, li2 tioh8 siak-phoa3 hit e5 hui5-pan5, hou7 tang5-kiaN5 e5 lang5 chhin-bak8 khoaN3-kiN3,  11). soa3 ka7 in kong2, Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 beh an2-ni phah-phoa3 chit e5 siaN5, kap chit e5 peh-siN3, chhin-chhiuN7 lang5 siak-phoa3 sio-hui5-lang5 e5 hui5-khi3, boe7 koh pou2--tit.  Koh lang5 beh ti7 To5-hui-tek8 bai5-chong3 si2-lang5, kau3 bo5 chhun sou2-chai7.  12). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 beh an2-ni khoan2-thai7 chit e5 sou2-chai7, kap ki5-tiong khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3; hou7 chit e5 siaN5 chhin-chhiuN7 To5-hui-tek8 chit8-iuN7.  13). Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 chhu3, kap Iu5-tai7 liat8-ong5 e5 chhu3, i2-keng phah la5-sam5--e5, long2 beh chhin-chhiuN7 To5-hui-tek8, in-ui7 ti7 hiah e5 chhu3-teng2, lang5 ng3 thiN-teng2 e5 ban7-siong7 sio-hiuN, ng3 pat8-ho7 e5 siong7-te3 koan3-tian7.
	14). Ia5-li7-bi2 tui3 To5-hui-tek8, chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhe i khi3 thoan5 beng7-leng7 e5 toe7-hng, to3--lai5; khia7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3 e5 iN7-lai7, tui3 cheng3-lang5 kong2,  15). Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3, an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh hou7 Goa2 sou2 kong2 it-chhe3 heng5-hoat8 in e5 chai-e7 kau3 chit e5 siaN5, kap long2-chong2 siok8 i e5 siaN5; in-ui7 in ngi7 in e5 am7-kun2, m7-kheng2 thiaN Goa2 e5 oe7.

[20]	Che3-si Im-bek8 e5 kiaN2 Pa-si-hou7-jiN2, choe3 koan2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3 e5 thau5-lang5,  2). thiaN-kiN3 Ia5-li7-bi2 thoan5 chiah e5 oe7; Pa-si-hou7-jiN2 chiu7 phah sian-ti Ia5-li7-bi2, eng7 chha5-ke5 ka7 i ke5 ti7 Pian7-nga2-bin2 teng2 e5 mng5; chit e5 mng5 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 tian7-lai7.  3). Ke3-jit8 Pa-si-hou7-jiN2 khui chha5-ke5, thau2-pang3 Ia5-li7-bi2; Ia5-li7-bi2 chiu7 tui3 i kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa m7-si7 kio3 li2 e5 mia5 choe3 Pa-si-hou7-jiN2; chiu7-si7 kio3 li2 Ma2-ko-jiN2-bi2-sat-pit.  4). In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh hou7 li2 choe3 li2 pun2-sin, kap li2 cheng3 peng5-iu2, kiaN-hiaN5 e5 goan5-in; in beh to2 ti7 tui3-tek8 e5 to-e7, li2 beh chhin-bak8 khoaN3-kiN3; Goa2 beh chiong Iu5-tai7 lang5 long2 kau ti7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 e5 chhiu2, i beh liah8 in kau3 Pa-pi2-lun5, eng7 to thai5--in.  5). Koh Goa2 beh chiong chit e5 siaN5 long2-chong2 e5 he3-chai5, kap tioh8-boa5 sou2 tit-tioh8--e5, kap it-chhe3 e5 po2-poe3, i2-kip8 Iu5-tai7 hiah e5 ong5 e5 po2-mih8, long2 kau ti7 in e5 tui3-tek8 e5 chhiu2; tui3-tek8 beh chhiuN2--in, beh liah8 in; toa3 kau3 Pa-pi2-lun5.  6). Li2 chit e5 Pa-si-hou7-jiN2 ah, li2 kap it-chhe3 tiam3 li2 ke-lai7 e5 lang5, long2 beh hou7 lang5 liah8-khi3; li2 kap li2 e5 cheng3 peng5-iu2, chiu7-si7 li2 tui3 in thoan5 ke2-oe7--e5, long2 beh kau3 Pa-pi2-lun5, si2 ti7-hia, bai5-chong3 ti7-hia.
	7). Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 bat bian2-kiong2 goa2, goa2 ia7 hou7 li2 bian2-kiong2; Li2 pi2 goa2 khah u7 lat8, lai5 iaN5 goa2; goa2 thong-jit8 chiaN5-choe3 chhio3-oe7, lang5 long2 hi3-lang7 goa2.  8). Goa2 tak8-pai2 kong2 e5 si5, chiu7 chhut ai-siong e5 siaN; goa2 kio3 kong2, Kiong5-po7, chhiuN2-kiap; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7, thong-jit8 chiaN5-choe3 Goa2 e5 leng5-jiok8, ki-chhi3.  9). Goa2 na7 kong2, Goa2 bo5 beh koh the5-khi2 Ia5-ho5-hoa, iah8 bo5 beh koh thok I e5 mia5 lai5 kong2; chiu7 ti7 Goa2 e5 sim-lai7 u7 chhin-chhiuN7 toh8 e5 he2, koaiN-bat8 ti7 Goa2 e5 kut-lai7; Goa2 chiu7 lun2-boe7-tiau5, boe7-oe7 ka-ki7 kim3-chi2.  10). Goa2 thiaN-kiN3 choe7-choe7 lang5 e5 hui2-pong3; si3-ui5 long2 si7 kiaN-hiaN5.  Goa2 ti-ki2 e5 peng5-iu2, chiu7-si7 teh tng-tan2 goa2 poah8-to2--e5, kong2, Tioh8 ko3--i, goan2 iah8 beh ko3--i; kiam2-chhai2 i siu7 in2-iu2, lan2 chiu7 oe7 iaN5--i, tui3 i po3-siu5.  11). Chong2-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kap goa2 ti7-teh; chhin-chhiuN7 chin thang kiaN e5 iong2-su7; sou2-i2 khun2-pek goa2--e5 beh poah8-to2, boe7-oe7 iaN5; in beh toa7-toa7 kian3-siau3 chiu7-si7 siu7 eng2 bo5 boe7-ki3-tit e5 lau3-khui3; in-ui7 in kiaN5 tai7-chi3 bo5 ti3-hui7.  12). Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 si7 chhi3-giam7 gi7-lang5, kam3-chhat lang5 e5 sim-pak sin7-tng5--e5; kiu5 Li2 hou7 goa2 khoaN3-kiN3 Li2 tui3 in po3-siu5; in-ui7 goa2 chiong goa2 e5 an3-kiaN7 pin2-beng5 ti7 Li2.  13). Lin2 tioh8 ng3 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhiuN3-koa, o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa; in-ui7 I kiu3 song3-hiong-lang5 e5 siN3-mia7, thoat-li7 phaiN2-lang5 e5 chhiu2.
	14). Goa2 chhut-si3 e5 jit8, goan7 hit e5 jit8-chi2 siu7 chiu3-chou2; goa2 e5 lau7-bu2 siN goa2 e5 jit8, goan7 hit e5 jit8-chi2 bo5 tit-tioh8 hok-khi3.  15). Lang5 po3 goa2 e5 lau7-pe7 kong2, Li2 u7 siN ta-pou-kiaN2, hou7 i chin hoaN-hi2--e5; goan7 hit e5 lang5 siu7 chiu3-chou2.  16). Goan7 hit-lang5 chhin-chhiuN7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 chhia-to2 hiah e5 siaN5, ia7 bo5 the3-hoe2--e5; goan7 i cha2-khi2-si5 thiaN-kiN3 ai-chham2 e5 siaN, jit8 tiong-tau3 thiaN-kiN3 hoah-hiam3 e5 siaN.  17). In-ui7 I bo5 tui3 thai--nih hou7 goa2 si2; hou7 goa2 e5 lau7-bu2 choe3 goa2 e5 bong7, i e5 thai siong5-siong5 toa7--e5.  18). Goa2 siaN2-su7 chhut-thai, lai5 tu2-tioh8 tioh8-boa5 iu-khou2; hou7 goa2 e5 ni5-jit8 in-ui7 kian3-siau3 lai5 siau-biat8 ah?

[21]	Se-ti2-ka ong5 chhe Ma2-ki-nga2 e5 kiaN2 Pa-si-hou7-jiN2, kap che3-si Ma2-se-nga2 e5 kiaN2 Se-hoan-nga2, khi3 kiN3 Ia5-li7-bi2 kong2,  2). Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat beh kap lan2 kau-chian3; kiu5 li2 thoe3 goan2 mng7 Ia5-ho5-hoa; kiam2-chhai2 Ia5-ho5-hoa chiau3 I ki5-biau7 e5 sou2 choe3 khoan2-thai7 lan2; hou7 i li7-khui lan2 chiuN7--khi3.  Hit-si5 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 Ia5-li7-bi2.
	3). Ia5-li7-bi2 tui3 in kong2, Lin2 tioh8 an2-ni ka7 Se-ti2-ka kong2,  4). Ia5-ho5-hoa I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh hou7 lin2 sou2 kiah8 e5 kun-khi3, chiu7-si7 lin2 ti7 siaN5-goa7 kap Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5, i2-kip8 ui5-khun3 lin2 e5 Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5, kau-chian3 e5 kun-khi3 to3-tng2--lai5; koh beh hou7 chiah-e5 long2 chu7-chip8 ti7 chit e5 siaN5-lai7.  5). Koh Goa2 ti7 au3-nau2, siu7-khi3, toa7 thong3-hun7 e5 tiong-kan, eng7 chhun-chhut e5 chhiu2, kap toa7 koan5-leng5 e5 chhiu2-kut, chhin-sin kong-kek lin2.  6). Koh beh phah chit e5 siaN5 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3, bo5-lun7 lang5 kap cheng-siN; in beh tu2-tioh8 toa7 un-ek8 lai5 si2.  7). I2-au7 Goa2 beh chiong Iu5-tai7 ong5 Se-ti2-ka, kap i e5 jin5-sin5 peh-siN3, chiu7-si7 ti7 chit e5 siaN5-lai7, tui3 un-ek8, to-kiam3, ki-hng sou2 chhun--e5, long2 kau ti7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat e5 chhiu2, kap in e5 tui3-tek8 e5 chhiu2, i2-kip8 siau3-siuN7 in e5 siN3-mia7 e5 lang5 e5 chhiu2; i beh eng7 to thai5-si2 in; bo5 po2-sioh, bo5 kho2-lin5, bo5 khoan-iong5; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  8). Li2 tioh8 tui3 chit e5 peh-siN3 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 chiong oah8-lou7 si2-lou7 pai5 ti7 lin2 e5 bin7-cheng5.  9). Tiam3 ti7 chit e5 siaN5-lai7--e5, beh tui3 to-kiam3, tui3 ki-hng, tui3 un-ek8, lai5 si2; tok8-tok8 chhut-khi3 tau5-hang5 ui5-khun3 lin2 e5 Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5--e5, beh tit-tioh8 oah8, lai5 khioh-tioh8 i e5 siN3-mia7.  10). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 e5 bin7 tiaN7-tiaN7 ng3 chit e5 siaN5, beh kang3 chai-e7, m7 kang3 hok-khi3; chit e5 siaN5 beh kau Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 e5 chhiu2; i beh eng7 he2 sio--i.
	11). Lun5-kau3 Iu5-tai7 ong5 e5 ke, lin2 tioh8 thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7.  12). Tai7-pit8 e5 ke ah, Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Lin2 tak8 cha2-khi2 tioh8 kiaN5 kong-peng5; chin2-kiu3 siu7 chhiuN2-kiap--e5 thoat-li7 kiong5-po7 e5 lang5 e5 chhiu2; kiaN-liau2 Goa2 e5 siu7-khi3, in-ui7 lin2 sou2 kiaN5 e5 phaiN2, lai5 hoat-choh; chhin-chhiuN7 he2 toh8--khi2-lai5, sim7-chi3 bo5 lang5 oe7 phah-hoa.  13). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Khia7-khi2 ti7 soaN-kok, piN5-iuN5, chioh8-poaN5-teng2 e5 peh-siN3, lin2 kong2, Chi7-chui7 oe7 loh8--lai5 kong-kek goan2? Chi7-chui7 oe7 jip8 goan2 khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7 ah? KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 kap lin2 choe3 tui3-tek8.  14). Ia5-ho5-hoa koh kong2, Goa2 beh chiau3 lin2 choe3 tai7-chi3 e5 kiat-ko2 heng5-hoat8 lin2; Goa2 iah8 beh hou7 he2 toh8 ti7 i e5 chhiu7-na5-lai7, sio-hui2 i e5 si3-ui5.

[22]	Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Li2 loh8-khi3 Iu5-tai7 ong5 e5 kiong-lai7; ti7-hia kong2 chit e5 oe7, kong2,  2). Che7 Tai7-pit8 po2-cho7 e5 Iu5-tai7 ong5 ah, li2 kap li2 e5 jin5-sin5 i2-kip8 jip8 chiah e5 mng5 e5 peh-siN3, long2 tioh8 thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7.  3). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Lin2 tioh8 kiaN5 kong-peng5 kap kong-gi7, chin2-kiu3 siu7 chhiuN2-toat8--e5 thoat-li7 ap-che3 lang5--e5 e5 chhiu2; m7-thang eng7 kiong5-po7 khi-hu7 chhut-goa7 lang5, kap kou-ji5 koaN2-hu7; ti7 chit e5 sou2-chai7 iah8 m7-thang lau5 bo5-choe7 e5 lang5 e5 huih.  4). Lin2 na7 jin7-chin kiaN5 chit e5 tai7-chi3, chiu7 beh u7 che7 Tai7-pit8 po2-cho7 e5 ong5, i kap i e5 jin5-sin5 peh-siN3, hek8-si7 che7-chhia, hek8-si7 khia5-be2, jip8 chit e5 chhu3 e5 mng5.  5). Lin2 na7 m7-thiaN chiah e5 oe7, Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 ki2 pun2-sin lai5 chiu3-choa7, chit keng chhu3 beh piN3-choe3 pha-hng.  6). Ia5-ho5-hoa lun7-kau3 Iu5-tai7 ong5 e5 ke an2-ni kong2, Goa2 khoaN3 li2 chhin-chhiuN7 Ki-liat8, chhin-chhiuN7 Li7-pa-lun3 e5 be2-liu; chong2-si7 Goa2 tek-khak hou7 li2 piN3-choe3 khong3-ia2, choe3 bo5 lang5 khia7-khi2 e5 siaN5.  7). Goa2 beh pi7-pan7 kiaN5 hui2-biat8 e5 lang5, tak8-e5 kiah8 ke-si kong-kek li2; in beh chho3 li2 siong7-ho2 e5 pek-hiuN-chhiu7, hiat-loh8 he2.  8). Choe7-choe7 kok e5 lang5 beh keng-ke3 chit e5 siaN5, tak8-e5 saN-kap kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa siaN2-su7 an2-ni khoan2-thai7 chit e5 toa7 siaN5 ah?  9). In beh in3 kong2, Si7 in-ui7 in khi3-sak Ia5-ho5-hoa in e5 Siong7-te3 e5 iok, hok8-sai7 keng3-pai3 pat8 e5 siong7-te3.
	10). Boh8-tit ui7-tioh8 si2-lang5 thi5-khau3, boh8-tit ui7-tioh8 i pi-siong; tioh8 in-ui7 siu7 chhian-soa2 e5 lang5 toa7-toa7 thi5-khau3; in-ui7 i boe7 koh to3--lai5, iah8 boe7 koh kiN3-tioh8 i e5 pun2-kok.  11). In-ui7 lun7-kau3 Iu5-tai7 ong5 Iok-se-a e5 kiaN2 Sa-liong5, soa3-chiap i e5 lau7-pe7 Iok-se-a choe3 ong5, au7-lai5 li7-khui chit e5 sou2-chai7--e5, Ia5-ho5-hoa u7 an2-ni kong2,  12). I tek-khak bo5 koh to3--lai5 chia; chiu7-si7 beh si2 ti7 hou7 lang5 liah8-khi3 e5 toe7-hng, bo5 koh khoaN3-kiN3 chit e5 toe7-hng.
	13). Hit e5 eng7 put-gi7 lai5 khi2 chhu3, eng7 bo5 kong-to7 lai5 khi2 lau5; peh8-peh8 kah lang5 choe3 i e5 kang, bo5 hou7 lang5 kang-chiN5; hit lang5 u7 chai-e7 ah.  14). I kong2, Goa2 beh ui7 pun2-sin khi2 toa7-chhu3, kap thong-hong e5 lau5; ui7 ka-ki7 khui toa7 thang, eng7 pek-hiuN-chha5 choe3 thian-lo5-pan2; eng7 gun5-chu lai5 iu5.  15). Li2 jiat8-sim ti7 pek-hiuN-chha5 e5 kong-chok, chiu7 oe7 choe3 ong5 mah? Li2 e5 lau7-pe7 kiam2 m7-si7 iah8 chiah8, iah8 lim, iah8 kiaN5 kong-peng5 kap kong-gi7 mah? Hit-si5 i tit-tioh8 hok-khi3.  16). I pan7-li2 khun3-khou2 kap song3-hiong lang5 e5 an3-kiaN7, i chiu7 tit-tioh8 hok-khi3; an2-ni kiam2 m7-si7 bat Goa2 mah? che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  17). Tok8-tok8 li2 e5 bak8-chiu, li2 e5 sim, chu3-i3 tham-sim, lau5 bo5-choe7 e5 lang5 e5 huih, kiaN5 ap-che3 kap kiong5-po7.  18). Sou2-i2 Ia5-ho5-hoa lun7-kau3 Iu5-tai7 ong5 Iok-se-a e5 kiaN2, Iok-nga2-keng3, an2-ni kong2, Lang5 bo5 beh ui7-tioh8 i ai-siong, kong2, Ai--ah, goa2 e5 hiaN! a2-si7, Ai--ah, goa2 e5 toa7-chi2! iah8 bo5 in-ui7 i ai-siong, kong2, Ai--ah, goa2 e5 chu2! a2-si7, Ai--ah, i e5 eng5-kng!  19). I beh hou7 lang5 tai5, chhin-chhiuN7 tai5 lu5 chit8-iuN7; beh thoa--chhut-khi3, hiat ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 siaN5-goa7.
	20). Li2 tioh8 chiuN7 Li7-pa-lun3 ai-khau3, ti7 Pa-san chhut-siaN, tui3 A-pa-lim5 ai-khau3; in-ui7 li2 sou2 chhin-ai3--e5 long2 hui2-biat8 lah.  21). Tng li2 heng-thong e5 si5, Goa2 chiu7 tui3 li2 kong2; li2 kong2, Goa2 m7 thiaN; li2 tui3 siau3-lian5 i2-lai5, long2 si7 chit-khoan2, m7 thiaN-than3 Goa2 e5 oe7.  22). Li2 e5 bok8-chia2 beh hou7 hong chhe--khi3; li2 sou2 chhin-ai3--e5 beh hou7 lang5 liah8--khi3; hit-si5 li2 tek-khak in-ui7 li2 it-chhe3 e5 phaiN2 lai5 lau3-khui3 kian3-siau3.  23). Li2 khia7-khi2 Li7-pa-lun3, choh siu7 ti7 pek-hiuN-chhiu7--e5, thong3-khou2 lim5-kau3 li2, thang3-thiaN3 chhin-chhiuN7 beh siN-kiaN2 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5; hit-si5 li2 e5 kho2-lin5 kau3 chaiN2-iuN7!  24). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 ki2 Goa2 e5 eng2-oah8 lai5 chiu3-choa7, sui-jian5 Iu5-tai7 ong5, Iok-nga2-keng3 e5 kiaN2 Ko-ni5-nga2, si7 Goa2 chiaN3-chhiu2 kai3-in3 e5 chhiu2-chi2, iah8 beh ka7 li2 pak--khi2-lai5.  25). Koh Goa2 beh chiong li2 kau hou7 siau3-siuN7 li2 e5 siN3-mia7 e5 lang5 e5 chhiu2; kap li2 sou2 m7-kaN2 kiN3 i e5 bin7 e5 lang5 e5 chhiu2, chiu7-si7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat e5 chhiu2, kap Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 e5 chhiu2.  26). Goa2 iah8 beh koaN2 li2, kap siN li2 e5 lau7-bu2, kau3 pat8-kok, m7-si7 lin2 chhut-si3 e5 sou2-chai7; lin2 beh si2 ti7-hia.  27). Chong2-si7 in e5 sim chin ai3 to3--khi3 e5 sou2-chai7 boe7-tit-thang to3--khi3.  28). Ko-ni5-nga2 chit-lang5 si7 siu7 khoaN3-khin, i2-keng phoa3 e5 hui5-khi3 mah? si7 bo5 thang hoaN-hi2 e5 khi3-ku7 mah? i kap i e5 hou7-e3, siaN2-su7 siu7 koaN2, hiat ti7 in sou2 m7 bat e5 toe7 ah?  29). Toe7 ah, toe7 ah, toe7 ah, tioh8 thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7;  30). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Tioh8 ki3 chit-lang5 bo5 kiaN2, it-seng boe7 tit-tioh8 heng-thong--e5; in-ui7 i e5 hou7-e3 e5 tiong-kan, bo5 koh u7 chit8-lang5 tit-tioh8 heng-thong, oe7 che7 ti7 Tai7-pit8 e5 po2-cho7, lai5 ti7-li2 Iu5-tai7.

[23]	Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Bok8-chia2 chan5-hai7 Goa2 e5 chhau2-tiuN5 e5 iuN5, hou7 i si3-soaN3; in u7 chai-e7 ah.  2). Sou2-i2 I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa chek-pi7 hiah-e5 iuN2-chhi7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 e5 bok8-chia2, an2-ni kong2, Lin2 phah-soaN3 Goa2 e5 iuN5-kun5, lai5 koaN2 in khi3, bo5 khoaN3-kou3 in; khoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh chiau3 lin2 sou2 kiaN5 e5 phaiN2 lai5 pan7 lin2; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  3). Goa2 beh chu7-chip8 Goa2 e5 iuN5-kun5 sou2 chhun--e5, tui3 Goa2 sou2 koaN2 in kau3 e5 tak8-kok; chhoa7 in koh to3-lai5 in e5 tiau5, hou7 in siN-thoaN3 choe7-choe7.  4). Goa2 beh siat-lip8 bok8-chia2 ti7-li2 in, iuN2-chhi7 in; hou7 in bo5 koh kiaN-hiaN5 gong5-ngiah8, iah8 bo5 kiam2-chio2; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	5). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Jit8-chi2 beh kau3, Goa2 beh ka7 Tai7-pit8 heng-khi2 gi7 e5 Ki; I beh choe3 ong5 lai5 ti7-li2; kiaN5 tai7-chi3 u7 ti3-hui7, ti7 toe7-chiuN7 kiaN5 kong-peng5 kap kong-gi7.  6). Tng I e5 jit8, Iu5-tai7 beh tit-tioh8 kiu3; I2-sek-liat8 beh an-jian5 khia7-khi2; I e5 mia5 beh chheng-choe3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lan2 e5 gi7.  7). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, KhoaN3 ah, jit8-chi2 beh kau3, lang5 ki2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 eng2-oah8 lai5 chiu3-choa7, bo5 beh kong2, I si7 chhoa7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 hou7-e3 tui3 Ai-kip8 toe7 chiuN7-lai5--e5.  8). In ki2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 eng2-oah8 lai5 chiu3-choa7, si7 beh kong2, I toa3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 hou7-e3 chhoa7 in tui3 pak-hng e5 toe7, iah8 tui3 kiN3-na7 Goa2 sou2 koaN2 in kau3 e5 toe7 chiuN7--lai5; in beh khia7-khi2 ti7 pun2 sou2-chai7.
	9). Lun7-kau3 hiah e5 sian-ti.  Goa2 e5 sim ti7 goa2 e5 lai7-bin7 iu-siong; goa2 e5 kut long2 gi7-gi7-chhoah; ui7-tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa kap I seng3 e5 oe7, goa2 chhin-chhiuN7 chiu2-chui3 e5 lang5, chhin-chhiuN7 hou7 chiu2 sou2 khah-iaN5 e5 lang5.  10). In-ui7 toe7-hng moa2-moa2 kiaN5 im5-loan7 e5 lang5; koh in-ui7 tu2-tioh8 chiu3-chou2, toe7 chiu7 pi-ai; khong3-ia2 e5 chhau2-tiuN5 long2 kou-ta5; in sou2 kiaN5 e5 lou7, chiu7-si7 phaiN2; in e5 se3-lek8 bo5 cheng3-tit8.  11). Lian5 sian-ti kap che3-si, to si7 siat-tok8--e5; chiu7 ti7 Goa2 e5 chhu3-lai7, Goa2 iah8 khoaN3-kiN3 in e5 phaiN2; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  12). In-ui7 an2-ni, in e5 lou7 beh chhin-chhiuN7 ou-am3-tiong kut8-kut8 e5 toe7; in beh tu2-tioh8 koaN2-tiok8, ti7-hia poah8-to2; tng pan7-li2 in e5 ni5, Goa2 beh hou7 chai-e7 kau3 ti7 in; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  13). Ti7 Sat-ma2-li7-a e5 sian-ti, Goa2 i2-keng khoaN3-kiN3 in e5 gu5-gong7; in thok Pa-lek8 lai5 chham3-gu2, hou7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 I2-sek-liat8 kiaN5 chha-lou7.  14). Ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 sian-ti, Goa2 i2-keng khoaN3-kiN3 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7; in kiaN5 kan-im5, choe3 su7 peh8-chhat8; koh chou7 phaiN2 lang5 e5 chhiu2 na2 u7 lat8; ti3-kau3 bo5 lang5 hoe5-thau5 li7-khui i e5 phaiN2; in ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5, long2 chhin-chhiuN7 Sou2-to-ma2; khia7-khi2 ti7-hia e5 peh-siN3 long2 chhin-chhiuN7 Go5-mou5-lah8.
	15). Sou2-i2 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa lun7-kau3 chiah e5 sian-ti, u7 an2-ni kong2; KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh eng7 in-tin5 hou7 in chiah8, koh eng7 khou2 e5 chui2 hou7 in lim; in-ui7 siat-tok8 e5 su7 chhut ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 sian-ti, liu5-heng5 pian3-toe7.  16). Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Chiah e5 sian-ti tui3 lin2 chham3-gu2--e5, lin2 boh8-tit thiaN in e5 oe7; in eng7 hu-ke2 ka3-si7 lin2; sou2 kong2 e5 iN7-siong7 si7 chhut ti7 in e5 sim; m7-si7 chhut ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhui3.  17). In siong5-siong5 tui3 biau2-si7 Goa2 e5 lang5 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2 lin2 beh hiong2-siu7 peng5-an; koh tui3 it-chhe3 chiau3 in sim e5 kong-ngi7 lai5 kiaN5 e5 lang5 kong2, Tek-khak bo5 u7 chai-e7 lim5-kau3 lin2.  18). Chi7-chui7 kap Ia5-ho5-hoa khe3-hap8, tit-tioh8 thiaN I e5 oe7 lai5 hiau2-ngou7 ah?  19). Chi7-chui7 chu3-i3 thiaN I e5 oe7 ah? KhoaN3 ah, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 siu7-khi3 chhin-chhiuN7 toa7 hong hoat-chhut; chiu7-si7 chin thau3 e5 kng2-le5-hong, beh tng2-seh8 lai5 kong-kek phaiN2-lang5 e5 thau5-khak.  20). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 sim sou2 gi2-tiaN7--e5, iau2-be7 choe3, iau2-be7 chiaN5; I e5 siu7-khi3 tek-khak bo5 to3-tng2, jit8-au7 lin2 beh beng5-pek8 thau3-thiat.  21). Hiah e5 sian-ti, Goa2 bo5 chhe in, in ka-ki7 chau2; Goa2 bo5 tui3 in kong2, in ka-ki7 soan-thoan5.  22). In na7 kap Goa2 khe3-hap8, chiu7 tek-khak hou7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 thiaN Goa2 e5 oe7; hou7 in hoe5-thau5 li7-khui in e5 phaiN2-lou7, kap in sou2 kiaN5 e5 phaiN2.  23). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 kiam2 choe3 kun7 e5 Siong7-te3, bo5 choe3 hng7 e5 Siong7-te3 mah?  24). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Lang5 kiam2 oe7 bih ti7 un2-bat8 e5 sou2-chai7, hou7 Goa2 khoaN3 i boe7 tioh8 mah? Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 kiam2 bo5 chhiong-moa2 ti7 thiN-toe7 mah?  25). Goa2 i2-keng thiaN-kiN3 hiah e5 sian-ti sou2 kong2-e5, chiu7-si7 thok Goa2 e5 mia5 soan-thoan5 peh8-chhat8; in kong2, Goa2 u7 bang7-kiN3, goa2 u7 bang7-kiN3.  26). Soan-thoan5 peh8-chhat8 e5 sian-ti, chiu7-si7 soan-thoan5 in e5 sim e5 khui2-cha3; in chun5 chit-ho7 e5 sim, beh kau3 ti7-si5 ah?  27). In tak8-lang5 chiong sou2 bang7--e5 saN-kap kong2-khi2; siuN7 beh hou7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 boe7-ki3-tit Goa2 e5 mia5; chhin-chhiuN7 in e5 liat8-chou2 in-ui7 Pa-lek8, lai5 boe7-ki3-tit Goa2 e5 mia5 chit8-iuN7.  28). Sian-ti na7 u7 bang7-kiN3 thang kong2-khi2 i e5 bang7; tit-tioh8 Goa2 e5 oe7--e5, tioh8 eng7 seng5-sit8 thoan5 Goa2 e5 oe7; chhou-khng kap beh8 thai2 oe7 pi2-tit? Che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  29). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 e5 oe7 kiam2 m7-si7 chhin-chhiuN7 he2, koh chhin-chhiuN7 oe7 phah-phoa3 chioh8-poaN5 e5 toa7-thui5 mah?
	30). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, KhoaN3 ah, hiah e5 sian-ti tui3 i e5 tang5-phoaN7 thau-theh8 Goa2 e5 oe7--e5, Goa2 kong-kek--in.  31). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Hiah e5 sian-ti eng7 chhui3-chih8 kong2, Che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5; Goa2 kong-kek in.  32). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, KhoaN3 ah, hiah-e5 eng7 ke2 e5 bang7 lai5 choe3 sian-ti--e5; in kong2-khi2 in e5 bang7; iah8 eng7 in e5 peh8-chhat8, kap in e5 hong-ham3, hou7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 kiaN5 chha-lou7; Goa2 kong-kek in; in-ui7 Goa2 bo5 chhe in, iah8 bo5 beng7-leng7 in, in long2 bo5 li7-ek chit e5 peh-siN3; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	33). Na7 chit e5 peh-siN3, a2-si7 sian-ti, a2-si7 che3-si, mng7 li2 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa u7 sim2-mih8 tang7-taN3 e5 bek8-si7? li2 chiu7 tioh8 ka7 in kong2, Sim2-mih8 tang7-taN3 e5 bek8-si7 ah! Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 beh khi3-sak lin2, chiu7-si7.  34). KiN3-na7 sian-ti, a2-si7 che3-si, a2-si7 peh-siN3, kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa tang7-taN3 e5 bek8-si7--e5; hit-ho7 lang5, Goa2 beh heng5-hoat8 i kap i e5 ke.  35). Lin2 tak8-lang5 tui3 i e5 chhu3-piN, tak8-lang5 tui3 i e5 hiaN-ti7, tioh8 an2-ni kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa u7 in3 sim2-mih8? Ia5-ho5-hoa u7 kong2 sim2-mih8?  36). Ia5-ho5-hoa tang7-taN3 e5 bek8-si7, chit-ku3 lin2 m7-thang koh kong2; in-ui7 tak8-lang5 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, beh choe3 in pun2-sin e5 tang7-taN3; in-ui7 lin2 chiong eng2-oah8 e5 Siong7-te3, ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 oe7 koe2 hou7 i chhoah8--khi3.  37). Li2 tioh8 tui3 sian-ti an2-ni kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa in3 li2 sim2-mih8? Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2 sim2-mih8?  38). Lin2 na7 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa tang7-taN3 e5 bek8-si7, Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 an2-ni kong2, Goa2 chhe lang5 kau3 lin2 hia, ka7 lin2 kong2, M7-thang kong2 Ia5-ho5-hoa tang7-taN3 e5 bek8-si7; lin2 iau2 teh kong2 chit-ku3 Ia5-ho5-hoa tang7-taN3 e5 bek8-si7;  39). sou2-i2 Goa2 beh choan5-jian5 boe7-ki3-tit lin2, chiong lin2 kap Goa2 sou2 siuN2-su3 lin2, i2-kip8 lin2 e5 liat8-chou2 e5 siaN5, tui3 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5 khi3-sak.  40). Koh beh hou7 eng2-oan2 e5 leng5-jiok8, kap ku2-tng5 e5 kian3-siau3, lim5-kau3 lin2; ku2-tng5 bo5 boe7-ki3--tit.

[24]	Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat chiong Iu5-tai7 ong5 Iok-nga2-keng3 e5 kiaN2 Ia5-ko-ni5-nga2, kap Iu5-tai7 e5 kui3-chok8, i2-kip8 kang-chhiuN7, thih-chhiuN7, tui3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 liah8--khi3 toa3 kau3 Pa-pi2-lun5.  Chit e5 su7 liau2-au7, Ia5-ho5-hoa ki2 hou7 goa2 khoaN3; u7 nng7 kheng e5 bu5-hoa-ko2, he7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 tian7-cheng5.  2). Chit8 khia kheng toe2 siong7-ho2 e5 bu5-hoa-ko2, chhin-chhiuN7 khi2-thau5 sek8 e5 bu5-hoa-ko2; chit8 khia kheng toe2 chin-phaiN2 e5 bu5-hoa-ko2, boe7-chiah8--tit, in-ui7 chin-phaiN2.  3). Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 ka7 goa2 kong2, Ia5-li7-bi2 ah, li2 khoaN3-kiN3 sim2-mih8? Goa2 in3 kong2, Bu5-hoa-ko2; ho2--e5 chin-ho2, phaiN2--e5 chin-phaiN2, boe7-chiah8--tit, in-ui7 chin-phaiN2.  4). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 koh lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  5). Ia5-ho5-hoa I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 an2-ni kong2, Siu7 liah8--khi3 e5 Iu5-tai7 lang5, chiu7-si7 Goa2 chhe in li7-khui chit sou2-chai7 kau3 Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 e5 toe7--e5; Goa2 beh khoaN3 in chhin-chhiuN7 chiah e5 ho2 e5 bu5-hoa-ko2; hou7 in tit-tioh8 hok-khi3.  6). Goa2 beh koan3-kou3 in, hou7 in tit-tioh8 hok-khi3; chhoa7 in to3-lai5 chit sou2-chai7; Goa2 iah8 beh kian3-lip8 in, bo5 koh hui2-hoai7 in; chai-poe5 in, bo5 ka7 i puih8--khi2-lai5.  7). Goa2 beh hou7 in u7 hit-ho7 sim, oe7 bat Goa2; chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa; in beh choe3 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3, Goa2 beh choe3 in e5 Siong7-te3; in-ui7 in beh chit8-sim kui-ng3 Goa2.  8). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Iu5-tai7 ong5 Se-ti2-ka, kap i chiah e5 kui3-chok8, kap Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 sou2 chhun, iau2 lau5 ti7 chit sou2-chai7 e5 peh-siN3, i2-kip8 khia7-khi2 ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7--e5; Goa2 khoaN3 in chhin-chhiuN7 chiah e5 phaiN2 e5 bu5-hoa-ko2, boe7-chiah8--tit, in-ui7 chin phaiN2.  9). Goa2 beh chiong in kau-chhut, hou7 in liu5-loh8 ti7 thiN-e7 ban7-kok, tu2-tioh8 kan-khou2; iah8 ti7 Goa2 koaN2 in kau3 e5 tak8 sou2-chai7, chiaN5-choe3 leng5-jiok8, choe3 oe7-piN3, choe3 ki-chhi3, choe3 chiu3-chou2.  10). Goa2 beh eng7 to-kiam3, eng7 ki-hng, eng7 un-ek8, kau3 in tiong-kan; tit8-kau3 in siu7 biat8 ti7 Goa2 sou2 siuN2-su3 in kap in liat8-chou2 e5 toe7.

[25]	 Tng Iu5-tai7 ong5 Iok-se-a e5 kiaN2 Iok-nga2-keng3 e5 si3--ni5, chiu7-si7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat goan5--ni5, u7 lun7-khi2 Iu5-tai7 peh-siN3 e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 Ia5-li7-bi2.  2). Sian-ti Ia5-li7-bi2 chiu7 chiong chit e5 oe7 tui3 Iu5-tai7 cheng3 peh-siN3, i2-kip8 it-chhe3 khia7-khi2 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 lang5 kong2:  3). Tui3 Iu5-tai7 ong5 A-bun5 e5 kiaN2 Iok-se-a chap8-saN--ni5, kau3 taN, ji7-chap8-saN ni5 ku2, u7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 goa2; goa2 i2-keng tui3 lin2 kong2; koh cha2-cha2 khi2-lai5 kong2; tok8-tok8 lin2 m7-thiaN.  4). Ia5-ho5-hoa ia7 cha2-cha2 khi2--lai5, chhe I e5 lou5-pok8 cheng3 sian-ti kau3 lin2 chia; na7-si7 lin2 bo5 thiaN-than3, iah8 bo5 aN3 hi7-khang lai5 thiaN.  5). I kong2, Lin2 tak8-lang5 tioh8 oat8-thau5 li7-khui i e5 phaiN2-lou7, kap lin2 sou2 choe3 e5 phaiN2; chiu7 thang khia7-khi2 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 siuN2-su3 lin2, kap lin2 e5 liat8-chou2 e5 toe7, tui3 kou2-cha2 kau3 eng2-oan2.  6). M7-thang than3 pat8-ho7 e5 siong7-te3, hok8-sai7 kui7-pai3 in; m7-thang eng7 lin2 e5 chhiu2 sou2 choe3--e5, lai5 jia2 Goa2 e5 siu7-khi3; an2-ni Goa2 chiu7 bo5 kang3 chai-e7 hou7 lin2.  7). Chong2-si7 lin2 bo5 thiaN-than3 Goa2, keng3-jian5 eng7 chhiu2 sou2 choe3--e5, jia2 Goa2 e5 siu7-khi3, ham7-hai7 ka-ki7; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  8). Sou2-i2 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, In-ui7 lin2 bo5 thiaN-than3 Goa2 e5 oe7,  9). khoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh tiau3 pak-hng chiah e5 chok8, kap Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat, lai5 kong-kek chit sou2-chai7, kap chit sou2-chai7 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3, i2-kip8 si3-ui5 e5 liat8-pang, Goa2 beh it-chin7 chau5-biat8 in, hou7 in choe3 thang gong5-ngiah8, thang ki-chhi3, eng2-oan2 pha-hng e5 sou2-chai7; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  10). Koh in tiong-kan hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN, khoai3-lok8 e5 siaN, sin-kiaN2-sai3 e5 siaN, sin-niu5 e5 siaN, oe-bo7 e5 siaN, kap teng e5 kng, Goa2 beh hou7 in long2 soah.  11). Choan5-toe7 tek-khak pha-hng, hou7 lang5 gong5-ngiah8; chiah e5 liat8-pang beh hok8-sai7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 chhit-chap8-ni5.  12). Chhit-chap8-ni5 i2-keng moa2, Goa2 beh heng5-hoat8 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5, kap i e5 kok e5 choe7, koh hou7 Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 e5 toe7 eng2-oan2 pha-hng; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  13). Goa2 beh eng7 Goa2 sou2 kong2 kong-kek hit-e5 toe7 e5 su7, long2 kau3 ti7 in; chiu7-si7 kiN3-na7 ki3 ti7 chit pun2 chheh, Ia5-li7-bi2 sou2 lun7-khi2 chiah e5 kok sou2 chham3-gu2--e5.  14). In-ui7 u7 choe7-choe7 kok, kap toa7 e5 kun-ong5, beh eng7 in Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 choe3 lou5-pok8; Goa2 iah8 beh chiau3 in e5 sou2 kiaN5, kap in e5 chhiu2 sou2 choe3--e5, po3-eng3 in.
	15). Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3, tui3 goa2 an2-ni kong2, Li2 tui3 Goa2 e5 chhiu2 chih chit poe siu7-khi3 e5 chiu2, hou7 Goa2 sou2 chhe li2 khi3 e5 liat8-kok lim.  16). In lim-liau2 chiu7 tian-tian to2-to2, iah8 beh hoat-kong5; in-ui7 Goa2 hou7 to-kiam3 kau3 in tiong-kan.  17). Goa2 chiu7 tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhiu2 chih chit e5 poe; hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 chhe goa2 khi3 e5 liat8-kok lim--i.  18). Chiu7-si7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 kap Iu5-tai7 chiah e5 siaN5, i2-kip8 in e5 liat8-ong5 kui3-chok8; hou7 in pha-hng; choe3 thang gong5-ngiah8, thang ki-chhi3, thang chiu3-chou2--e5, chhin-chhiuN7 kin-a2-jit8 chit8-iuN7.  19). Koh Ai-kip8 ong5 Hoat-lo2, kap i e5 jin5-sin5, kui3-chok8, cheng3 peh-siN3;  20). kap saN-chham-chhap e5 peh-siN3, OU-su toe7 chiah e5 ong5, Hui-li7-su7 toe7 chiah e5 ong5, A-sit8-ki-lun5, Ka-sat, I2-kek-lun5, i2-kip8 A-sit8-tut8 sou2 chhun e5 lang5;  21). koh I2-tong, Mou5-ap, kap A-bun5 e5 hou7-e3;  22). Chhui-lo5 liat8-ong5, Se-tun3 liat8-ong5, hai2-goa7 e5 hai2-su7 e5 liat8-ong5;  23). Ti2-tan3, The5-ma2, Pou3-su, kap it-chhe3 thi3 pin3-piN--e5;  24). A-lat-pek e5 liat8-ong5, tiam3 ti7 khong3-ia2 saN-chham-chhap e5 peh-siN3 e5 liat8-ong5;  25). Sim-li7 e5 liat8-ong5, I2-lan5 e5 liat8-ong5, Bi2-thai3 e5 liat8-ong5;  26). pak-hng hng7-kun7 e5 liat8-ong5, chit-e5 hit-e5, i2-kip8 thiN-e7 ban7-kok lim--i; i2-au7 Si7-sa-khek ong5 iah8 beh lim--i.  27). Li2 tioh8 ka7 in kong2, Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3, an2-ni kong2, Lin2 tioh8 lim, lai5 chui3, lai5 thou3, lai5 poah8-to2; bo5 koh khi2--lai5; in-ui7 Goa2 hou7 to-kiam3 kau3 lin2 tiong-kan.  28). In na7 m7-kheng2 tui3 li2 e5 chhiu2 chih chit e5 poe khi3 lim, li2 chiu7 tioh8 ka7 in kong2, Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Lin2 koat-toan3 tioh8 lim.  29). In-ui7 Goa2 kang3 chai-e7 tui3 hit e5 eng7 Goa2 e5 mia5 lai5 chheng e5 siaN5 khi2-chhiu2, lin2 oe7 it-chin7 bian2 heng5-hoat8 mah? tek-khak boe7 bian2-tit; in-ui7 Goa2 beh beng7-leng7 to-kiam3 lim5-kau3 toe7-chiuN7 long2-chong2 e5 peh-siN3; che si7 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  30). Sou2-i2 li2 tioh8 tui3 in soan-thoan5 che it-chhe3 e5 oe7, lai5 kong-kek in, kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa beh tui3 teng2-bin7 au5-kio3, tui3 I khia7-khi2 e5 seng3-sou2 chhut-siaN, tui3 I e5 iuN5-kun5 toa7-siaN au5-kio3; I beh tui3 toe7-chiuN7 long2-chong2 e5 peh-siN3 hoah-hiam3, chhin-chhiuN7 tah8 phu5-to5--e5 chit8-iuN7.  31). Beh u7 hoah e5 siaN thiaN kau3 toe7-kek8; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh kap liat8-kok ke3-kau3; kiN3 u7 hiat-khi3--e5, I beh kap in cheng-pian7; lun7-kau3 phaiN2-lang5, I beh chiong in kau hou7 to-kiam3; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	32). Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, beh u7 chai-e7 tui3 chit-kok hoat kau3 hit-kok; koh u7 toa7 po3-thau5-hong tui3 toe7-kek8 khi2.  33). Tng hit-jit8, Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 thai5--e5, tui3 toe7 e5 chit-peng5 kau3 toe7 e5 hit-peng5 long2 u7; bo5 lang5 thi5-khau3, bo5 lang5 ka7 i siu-sip8, bo5 lang5 ka7 i bai5-chong3; beh chiaN5-choe3 toe7-chiuN7 e5 pun3-so3.  34). Bok8-chia2 ah, lin2 tioh8 ai-khau3 au5-kio3; iuN5-kun5 e5 thau5-bak8 ah, lin2 tioh8 ko7 ti7 he2-hu-tiong; in-ui7 lin2 siu7-thai5 kap hun-soaN3 e5 jit8-ki5 i2-keng kau3; lin2 beh to2--loh8-khi3 chhin-chhiuN7 lang5 sou2 hoaN-hi2 e5 khi3-ku7 ka-lauh8.  35). Bok8-chia2 bo5 lou7 thang to5-chau2, iuN5-kun5 e5 thau5-bak8 iah8 bo5 lou7 thang thoat-li7.  36). U7 bok8-chia2 au5-kio3 e5 siaN, u7 iuN5-kun5 e5 thau5-bak8 teh ai-khau3; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa hou7 in e5 chhau2-tiuN5 pha-hng.  37). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoat-chhut beng2-liat8 e5 siu7-khi3; peng5-an e5 iuN5-tiau5 chiaN5-choe3 leng2-cheng7.  38). I chhin-chhiuN7 sai li7-khui i e5 hiat8; in-ui7 khi-ap e5 beng2-liat8 koh in-ui7 I siu7-khi3 e5 beng2-liat8; in e5 toe7 long2 chiaN5-choe3 thang gong5-ngiah8--e5.

[26]	Iu5-tai7 ong5 Iok-se-a e5 kiaN2 Iok-nga2-keng3 khi2-thau5 che7-ui7 e5 si5, u7 chit e5 oe7 tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lai5, kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2,  2). Li2 tioh8 khia7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3 e5 iN7-lai7; u7 Iu5-tai7 chiah e5 siaN5 lai5 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3 keng3-pai3--e5; li2 tioh8 eng7 Goa2 long2-chong2 beng7-leng7 li2 tui3 in kong2 e5 oe7, ka7 in kong2; m7-thang chio2 chit8-ku3.  3). Kiam2-chhai2 in kheng2 thiaN-than3, tak8-lang5 hoe5-thau5 li7-khui in e5 phaiN2-lou7; chiu7 Goa2 ui7-tioh8 in sou2 kiaN5 e5 phaiN2, siuN7 beh kang3 hou7 in e5 chai-e7, thang the3-hoe2.  4). Li2 tioh8 ka7 in kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Lin2 na7 m7-kheng2 thiaN Goa2, lai5 kiaN5 Goa2 sou2 siat ti7 lin2 bin7-cheng5 e5 lut8-hoat;  5). lai5 thiaN-than3 Goa2 sou chhe kau3 lin2 hia Goa2 chiah e5 lou5-pok8, cheng3 sian-ti e5 oe7; chiu7-si7 Goa2 cha2-cha2 khi2--lai5 sou2 chhe--e5, (chong2-si7 lin2 bo5 thiaN);  6). chiu7 Goa2 beh hou7 chit keng chhu3 chhin-chhiuN7 Si7-lo5; hou7 chit e5 siaN5 choe3 toe7-chiuN7 ban7-kok chiu3-chou2 e5 oe7-piN3.  7). Ia5-li7-bi2 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3-lai7 kong2 chiah-e5 oe7; che3-si, sian-ti, kap cheng3 peh-siN3 long2 u7 thiaN-kiN3.  8). Ia5-li7-bi2 chiong Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 i tui3 cheng3 peh-siN3 kong2 e5 oe7, it-chin7 kong2-liau2; che3-si, sian-ti, kap cheng3 peh-siN3 long2 lai5 liah8--i, kong2, Li2 tek-khak tioh8 si2.  9). Li2 siaN2-su7 thok Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5 lai5 chham3-gu2, kong2, Chit keng chhu3 beh chhin-chhiuN7 Si7-lo5, chit e5 siaN5 beh pha-hng, bo5 lang5 khia7-khi2 ah? Tui3 an2-ni cheng3 peh-siN3 long2 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3 chu7-chip8 kau3 Ia5-li7-bi2 hia.
	10). Iu5-tai7 e5 kui3-chok8 thiaN-kiN3 chiah e5 tai7-chi3, chiu7 tui3 ong5-kiong chiuN7-kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3; che7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3 sin-mng5 e5 mng5-khau2.  11). Che3-si, sian-ti, tui3 kui3-chok8 kap cheng3 peh-siN3 kong2, Chit lang5 tioh8 gi2 i si2-choe7; in-ui7 i u7 chham3-gu2 kong-kek chit e5 siaN5; tu2-tu2 chhin-chhiuN7 lin2 chhin-hi7 sou2 thiaN--e5.  12). Ia5-li7-bi2 chiu7 tui3 chiah e5 kui3-chok8 kap cheng3 peh-siN3 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa chhe goa2 chham3-gu2, kong-kek chit keng chhu3, kap chit e5 siaN5; kong2-khi2 lin2 sou2 u7 thiaN-kiN3 chiah-e5 it-chhe3 e5 oe7.  13). Sou2-i2 lin2 taN tioh8 koe2 lin2 e5 lou7, kap lin2 e5 sou2 choe3; thiaN-than3 lin2 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 siaN; Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 beh the3-hoe2 I sou2 beh kang3 hou7 lin2 e5 chai-e7.  14). Lun7-kau3 goa2, khoaN3 ah, goa2 ti7 lin2 e5 chhiu2-thau5; lin2 khoaN3 choe3 ho2, khoaN3 choe3 eng-kai--e5, chiu7 chiau3 an2-ni khoan2-thai7 goa2.  15). Chong2-si7 lin2 tioh8 khak-sit8 chai; na7 hai7-si2 goa2, chiu7 beh hou7 bo5-choe7 e5 huih kui ti7 lin2, kap chit e5 siaN5, kap ki5-tiong khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sit8-chai7 u7 chhe goa2 kau3 lin2 chia, chiong chiah-e5 it-chhe3 e5 oe7, thoan5 kau3 lin2 e5 hi7-khang.  16). Kui3-chok8 kap cheng3 peh-siN3 chiu7 ka7 che3-si sian-ti kong2, Chit-lang5 m7 eng-kai gi2 i si2-choe7; in-ui7 i si7 thok Ia5-ho5-hoa, lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 mia5, lai5 tui3 lan2 kong2.  17). Kok-lai7 e5 lau7-toa7 chiu7 u7 kui2-na7 lang5 khi2--lai5, tui3 chu7-hoe7 e5 cheng3 peh-siN3 kong2,  18). Tng Iu5-tai7 ong5 Hi-se-ka e5 jit8, u7 Mou5-li7-sa lang5, Bi2-ka, tui3 Iu5-tai7 e5 cheng3-lang5 chham3-gu2, kong2, Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Sek-an beh hou7 lang5 loe5 chhin-chhiuN7 chhan5-hng5; Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 beh piN3-choe3 thou5-tui; chit keng tian7 e5 soaN beh chhin-chhiuN7 chhiu7-na5 koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7.  19). Iu5-tai7 ong5 Hi-se-ka kap cheng3 Iu5-tai7 lang5, kiam2 u7 hou7 i si2 mah? Hi-se-ka kiam2 m7-si7 keng3-ui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa, khun2-kiu5 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 un; Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 the3-hoe2 I sou2 kong2 beh kang3 hou7 in e5 chai-e7 mah? TaN na7 hai7-si2 chit-lang5, lan2 chiu7-si7 choe3 toa7 phaiN2, hai7 ka-ki7 e5 siN3-mia7.
	20). Koh u7 chit8-lang5 thok Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5 lai5 soan-thoan5; si7 Ki-liat8-ia5-lim5 lang5 Si7-ma2-nga2 e5 kiaN2 OU-li7-a; i chiau3 Ia5-li7-bi2 it-chhe3 e5 oe7 lai5 soan-thoan5, kong-kek chit e5 siaN5 kap chit e5 toe7.  21). Iok-nga2-keng3 ong5 kap i e5 cheng3 iong2-su7 kui3-chok8 thiaN-kiN3 i e5 oe7, ong5 chiu7 siuN7 beh hou7 i si2; OU-li7-a thiaN-kiN3 chiu7 kiaN, chau2-khi3 Ai-kip8.  22). Iok-nga2-keng3 ong5 chhe lang5 khi3 Ai-kip8, chiu7-si7 A-kek-pho e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-na2-tan kap kui2-na7 lang5 kau3 Ai-kip8.  23). In chiu7 tui3 Ai-kip8 liah8 OU-li7-a chhut--lai5, sang3 kau3 Iok-nga2-keng3 ong5 hia; ong5 eng7 to thai5 i, hiat i e5 sin-si ti7 peng5-siong5 lang5 e5 bong7.  24). Chong2-si7 Sa-hoan e5 kiaN2 A-hi-kam po2-hou7 Ia5-li7-bi2, chiah bo5 kau ti7 peh-siN3 e5 chhiu2, hou7 i si2.

[27]	Iu5-tai7 ong5 Iok-se-a e5 kiaN2 Iok-nga2-keng3 khi2-thau5 che7-ui7 e5 si5, u7 chit e5 oe7 tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lim5-kau3 Ia5-li7-bi2 kong2,  2). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 goa2 an2-ni kong2, Li2 ui7 ka-ki7 choe3 soh kap taN, he7 ti7 li2 e5 am7-kun2;  3). thok-tiong7 lai5 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 kiN3 Iu5-tai7 ong5 Se-ti2-ka hiah e5 su3-chia2 e5 chhiu2; hou7 in toa3 hiah e5 mih8 kau3 I2-tong ong5, Mou5-ap ong5, A-bun5 chok8 e5 ong5, Chhui-lo5 ong5, Se-tun3 ong5 hia.  4). Koh beng7-leng7 su3-chia2 tui3 in e5 chu2 kong2, Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 an2-ni kong2, Lin2 tioh8 tui3 lin2 e5 chu2 an2-ni kong2,  5). Goa2 eng7 Goa2 e5 toa7 koan5-leng5, kap Goa2 chhun-chhut e5 chhiu2, chhong3-cho7 toe7 kap toe7-chiuN7 e5 lang5, i2-kip8 cheng-siN; chiong i siuN2-su3 Goa2 sou2 khoaN3-choe3 hap8-gi5--e5.  6). TaN Goa2 chiong chiah e5 toe7 long2 kau hou7 Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5, Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat e5 chhiu2; Goa2 iah8 chiong chhan5-ia2 e5 chau2-siu3 hou7 i, choe3 i e5 chhe-eng7.  7). Liat8-kok long2 beh hok8-sai7 i, i2-kip8 i e5 kiaN2, i e5 sun; tit8-kau3 i pun2-kok tu2-tioh8 po3-eng3 e5 jit8 kau3; hit-si5 choe7-choe7 kok kap toa7 kun-ong5 beh eng7 i choe3 lou5-pok8.  8). Na7 u7 sim2-mih8 peh-siN3, sim2-mih8 kok, m7-kheng2 hok8-sai7 chit e5 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat, iah8 m7-kheng2 chiong am7-kun2 koa3 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 e5 taN--e5; Goa2 beh eng7 to-kiam3, eng7 ki-hng, eng7 un-ek8 heng5-hoat8 hit e5 peh-siN3, tit8-kau3 Goa2 chioh i e5 chhiu2 lai5 it-chin7 biat8 in; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  9). Chong2-si7 lin2, lin2 m7-thang thiaN lin2 e5 sian-ti, lin2 e5 pok-koa3--e5, lin2 e5 oan5-bang7--e5, lin2 e5 kiaN5 sia5-sut8 e5, lin2 e5 sai-kong; in ka7 lin2 kong2, Lin2 boe7 ti3-kau3 hok8-sai7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5.  10). In tui3 lin2 chham3-gu2 peh8-chhat8, beh hou7 lin2 chhian-soa2 li7-khui pun2 sou2-chai7 hng7-hng7; ti3-kau3 Goa2 koaN2 lin2 chhut, hou7 lin2 biat8-bo5.  11). Tok8-tok8 na7 u7 sim2-mih8 peh-siN3 kheng2 chiong am7-kun2 koa3 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 e5 taN, lai5 hok8-sai7 i--e5, Goa2 beh hou7 i iu5-goan5 toa3 ti7 pun2 sou2-chai7, thang cheng3-choh, thang khia7-khi2; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	12). Goa2 chiu7 chiau3 chiah-e5 it-chhe3 e5 oe7, tui3 Iu5-tai7 ong5 Se-ti2-ka kong2, Tioh8 chiong lin2 e5 am7-kun2 koa3 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 e5 taN, lai5 hok8-sai7 i kap i e5 peh-siN3, chiah oe7 tit-tioh8 oah8.  13). Li2 kap li2 e5 peh-siN3 siaN2-su7 beh in-ui7 to-kiam3, in-ui7 ki-hng, in-ui7 un-ek8 lai5 si2, chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lun7-khi2 m7-kheng2 hok8-sai7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 hit-ho7 kok e5 oe7 ah?  14). Hiah e5 sian-ti ka7 lin2 kong2, Lin2 boe7 ti3-kau3 hok8-sai7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5, boh8-tit thiaN--in; in-ui7 in tui3 lin2 sou2 soan-thoan5--e5 si7 peh8-chhat8.  15). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 bo5 chhe in, chong2-si7 in thok Goa2 e5 mia5 soan-thoan5 peh8-chhat8; ti3-kau3 Goa2 chiong lin2 kap hiah e5 tui3 lin2 soan-thoan5 e5 sian-ti, long2 koaN2 chhut, saN-kap biat8-bo5.
	16). Goa2 koh tui3 chiah e5 che3-si kap chit kok e5 cheng3 peh-siN3 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Lin2 m7-thang thiaN hiah e5 sian-ti tui3 lin2 sou2 chham3-gu2--e5; in kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3 e5 khi3-ku7 bo5 joa7-ku2 beh tui3 Pa-pi2-lun5 toa3 to3-lai5; ki5-sit8 in tui3 lin2 sou2 soan-thoan5--e5, si7 peh8-chhat8.  17). Boh8-tit thiaN--in, tioh8 hok8-sai7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5, lai5 tit-tioh8 oah8; mih-sai2 hou7 chit e5 siaN5 piN3-choe3 pha-hng?  18). In na7 ko2-jian5 si7 sian-ti, u7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 kau3 ti7 in, in chiu7 tioh8 kiu5 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, hou7 hiah-e5 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3, kap Iu5-tai7 e5 ong5-kiong, kap Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 chhun e5 khi3-ku7, bo5 poaN khi3 Pa-pi2-lun5.  19). In-ui7 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Lun7-kau3 chiah e5 tang5 thiau7, tang5 hai2, phun5-cho7, kap lau5 ti7 chit e5 siaN5 sou2 chhun e5 khi3-ku7;  20). chiu7-si7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat liah8 Iu5-tai7 ong5 Iok-nga2-keng3 e5 kiaN2 Ia5-ko-ni5-nga2, kap Iu5-tai7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 chiah e5 chun-kui3 e5 lang5, tui3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 kau3 Pa-pi2-lun5 e5 si5, sou2 bo5 chhiuN2--khi3-e5;  21). sit8-chai7 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 an2-ni kong2, Lun7-kau3 lau5 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3, kap Iu5-tai7 ong5-kiong, kap Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 khi3-ku7,  22). hiah-e5 beh poaN kau3 Pa-pi2-lun5 lau5 ti7-hia; kau3 Goa2 koan3-kou3 in e5 jit8, chiu7 Goa2 beh toa3 in chiuN7-lai5, koh kui chit e5 sou2-chai7; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.

[28]	Tng hit-ni5, Iu5-tai7 ong5 Se-ti2-ka khi2-thau5 che7-ui7 e5 te7 si3-ni5 gou7 geh8, Ki-pian3 lang5 Ap-sok e5 kiaN2, sian-ti Hap-na2-ni5-nga2, ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3, tng chiah e5 che3-si kap cheng3 peh-siN3 e5 bin7-cheng5, tui3 goa2 kong2,  2). Bau7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa I2-sek-liat8 e5 siong7-te3 an2-ni kong2, Goa2 i2-keng at-chih8 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 e5 taN.  3). Nng7-ni5-lai7 Goa2 beh chiong Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat tui3 chit sou2-chai7 chhiuN2--khi3 kau3 Pa-pi2-lun5, chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3 it-chhe3 e5 khi3-ku7; long2 beh hou7 i to3-tng2--lai5 chit sou2-chai7.  4). Goa2 koh beh chiong Iu5-tai7 ong5 Iok-nga2-keng3 e5 kiaN2 Ia5-ko-ni5-nga2 kap siu7-liah8 kau3 Pa-pi2-lun5 hiah e5 Iu5-tai7 lang5, hou7 in to3-tng2 lai5 chit sou2-chai7, in-ui7 Goa2 beh at-chih8 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 e5 taN; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  5). Hit-si5 sian-ti Ia5-li7-bi2 tng chiah e5 che3-si e5 bin7-cheng5, kap khia7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3 cheng3 peh-siN3 e5 bin7-cheng5, tui3 sian-ti Hap-na2-ni5-nga2 kong2,  6). sian-ti Ia5-li7-bi2 kong2, A-beng7, goan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kiaN5; goan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa chiaN5 li2 sou2 chham3-gu2 chiah e5 oe7; chiong Ia5-ho5-hoa chhu3-lai7 e5 khi3-ku7, kap it-chhe3 siu7-liah8--khi3 e5 lang5, tui3 Pa-pi2-lun5 to3-lai5 chit sou2-chai7.  7). Chong2-si7 goa2 tui3 li2 kap cheng3 peh-siN3 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, li2 tioh8 thiaN.  8). Tui3 kou2-cha2 i2-lai5, li2 goa2 i2-cheng5 hiah e5 sian-ti, tui3 choe7-choe7 sou2-chai7, kap toa7-kok, chham3-gu2 kau-chian3, chai-e7, un-ek8.  9). Sian-ti chham3-gu2 peng5-an, hit e5 sian-ti e5 oe7 tit-tioh8 eng3-giam7, chiu7 chai hit e5 sian-ti chin-chiaN3 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 chhe--e5.  10). Tui3 an2-ni, sian-ti Hap-na2-ni5-nga2 chiong sian-ti Ia5-li7-bi2 am7-kun2 e5 taN theh8--khi2-lai5, ka7 i at-chih8.  11). Hap-na2-ni5-nga2 koh tng cheng3 peh-siN3 e5 bin7-cheng5 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Nng7-ni5-lai7, Goa2 beh chiau3 an2-ni tui3 liat8-kok e5 am7-kun2 at-chih8 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat e5 taN.  Sian-ti Ia5-li7-bi2 chiu7 choe3 i khi3.  12). Sian-ti Hap-na2-ni5-nga2 chiong sian-ti Ia5-li7-bi2 am7-kun2 e5 taN at-chih8 liau2-au7, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 Ia5-li7-bi2 kong2,  13). Li5 tioh8 khi3 ka7 Hap-na2-ni5-nga2 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Li2 at-chih8 chha5 e5 taN, beh choe3 thih e5 taN lai5 thoe3--in.  14). In-ui7 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 an2-ni kong2, Goa2 chiong thih e5 taN koa3 ti7 liat8-pang e5 am7-kun2, hou7 in hok8-sai7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat; in long2 beh hok8-sai7 i; Goa2 iah8 chiong chhan5-ia2 e5 chau2-siu3 hou7 i.  15). Sian-ti Ia5-li7-bi2 chiu7 tui3 sian-ti Hap-na2-ni5-nga2 kong2, Hap-na2-ni5-nga2 ah, li2 tioh8 thiaN; Ia5-ho5-hoa peng7-bo5 chhe li2, li2 keng2-jian5 hou7 chit e5 peh-siN3 oa2-kho3 peh8-chhat8.  16). Sou2-i2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Li2 khoaN3, Goa2 beh hou7 li2 li7-khui se3-kan; li2 kin-ni5 tek-khak si2, in-ui7 li2 kong2 poe7-gek8 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7.  17). Hit-ni5 chhit-geh8, sian-ti Hap-na2-ni5-nga2 chiu7 si2.

[29]	Sian-ti7 Ia5-li7-bi2 tui3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 kia3-phoe hou7 siu7-liah8 iau2 ti7-teh--e5 e5 lau7-toa7, kap chiah e5 che3-si, sian-ti, cheng3 peh-siN3, chiu7-si7 Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat tui3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 liah8 kau3 Pa-pi2-lun5--e5.  2). (Che si7 ti7 Ia5-ko-ni5-nga2 ong5, kap thai3-hou7, thai3-kam3, kap Iu5-tai7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 kui3-chok8, i2-kip8 kang-chhiuN7, thih-chhiuN7, long2 li7-khui Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 liau2-au7.)  3). Hit-tiuN phoe thok-tiong7 Sa-hoan e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-a-sat, kap Hi-lek8-ka e5 kiaN2 Ki-ma2-li7, toa3--khi3; chi2 nng7 lang5 chiu7-si7 Iu5-tai7 ong5 Se-ti2-ka chhe--khi3 Pa-pi2-lun5, kiN3 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat--e5.  4). Phoe-lai7 kong2: Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3, tui3 it-chhe3 siu7-liah8-khi3--e5, chiu7-si7 Goa2 hou7 in tui3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 siu7-liah8 kau3 Pa-pi2-lun5 e5 lang5, an2-ni kong2,  5). Lin2 tioh8 khi2-chhu3 lai5 khia7-khi2; choh-hng5 lai5 chiah8 i e5 ke2-chi2;  6). Chhoa7-bou2 lai5 siN-kiaN2, cha-bou2-kiaN2; ka7 lin2 e5 kiaN2 chhoa7-bou2; hou7 lin2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 chhut-ke3; hou7 in siN-kiaN2, cha-bou2-kiaN2; thang ti7-hia ke-thiN choe7-choe7, bo5 kiam2-chio2.  7). Goa2 sou2 hou7 lin2 siu7-liah8--khi3 hit e5 siaN5, lin2 tioh8 tou5-bou5 i e5 peng5-an, thoe3 i ki5-to2 Ia5-ho5-hoa; in-ui7 i tit-tioh8 peng5-an, lin2 iah8 te3 i peng5-an.  8). Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3, an2-ni kong2, Boh8-tit hou7 lin2 tiong-kan e5 sian-ti kap pok-koa3--e5 in2-iu2; iah8 boh8-tit sin3 lin2 e5 bang7, chiu7-si7 lin2 sou2 bang7-kiN3--e5.  9). In-ui7 in thok Goa2 e5 mia5 tui3 lin2 soan-thoan5 peh8-chhat8-oe7; Goa2 peng7-bo5 chhe in; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  10). In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Pa-pi2-lun5 chhit-chap8 ni5 e5 ki5-han7 i2-keng moa2, Goa2 beh lim5-kau3 lin2, chiaN5 Goa2 tui3 lin2 sou2 kong2 e5 ho2-oe7; hou7 lin2 to3-lai5 chit e5 sou2-chai7.  11). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 chai Goa2 tui3 lin2 sou2 chun5 e5 i3-su3, si7 siuN2-su3 peng5-an e5 i3-su3, m7-si7 kang3 chai-e7; beh hou7 lin2 be2-keng2 u7 ng3-bang7.  12). Hit-si5 lin2 beh kiu5-kio3 Goa2, beh khi3 ki5-to2 Goa2, Goa2 beh thiaN lin2.  13). Lin2 beh chhe7 Goa2, lai5 tu2-tioh8; in-ui7 lin2 beh choan-sim chhe7 Goa2.  14). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2: Goa2 beh hou7 lin2 chhe7-tioh8; Goa2 iah8 beh hou7 lin2 siu7-liah8 e5 lang5 to3-tng2--lai5; beh tui3 Goa2 sou2 koaN2 lin2 kau3 e5 tak8-kok tak8 sou2-chai7 chu7-chip8 lin2; iah8 beh hou7 lin2 to3-lai5 pun2 sou2-chai7, chiu7-si7 Goa2 sou2 hou7 lin2 tui3 hia siu7-liah8--e5; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	15). In-ui7 lin2 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ka7 goan2 heng-khi2 sian-ti.  16). TaN Ia5-ho5-hoa lun7-kau3 che7 Tai7-pit8 po2-cho7 e5 ong5, iah8 lun7-kau3 tiam3 ti7 chit e5 siaN5 e5 cheng3 peh-siN3, chiu7-si7 bo5 kap lin2 saN-kap siu7-liah8 e5 hiaN-ti7;  17). ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh eng7 to-kiam3, eng7 ki-hng eng7 un-ek8, kau3 ti7 in; hou7 in chhin-chhiuN7 kek8-phaiN2 e5 bu5-hoa-ko2, phaiN2 kau3 boe7-chiah8-tit.  18). Goa2 beh eng7 to-kiam3, eng7 ki-hng, eng7 un-ek8 tui-jip in; hou7 in liu5-loh8 ti7 thiN-e7 ban7-kok; ti7 Goa2 koaN2 in kau3 e5 tak8-kok, choe3 thang chiu3-chou2, thang gong5-ngiah8 thang ki-chhi3, thang leng5-jiok8--e5.  19). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Che si7 in-ui7 in bo5 thiaN-than3 Goa2 e5 oe7, chiu7-si7 Goa2 chhe Goa2 chiah e5 lou5-pok8 cheng3 sian-ti ka7 in kong2 e5 oe7; si7 cha2-cha2 khi2-lai5 chhe in; chong2-si7 lin2 bo5 thiaN; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  20). Sou2-i2 lin2 it-chhe3 siu7-liah8--khi3 e5, chiu7-si7 Goa2 tui3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 chhe kau3 Pa-pi2-lun5--e5, lin2 long2 tioh8 thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7.
	21). Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3, an2-ni kong2, lun7-kau3 Ko-nai7-nga2 e5 kiaN2 A-hap, kap Ma2-se-nga2 e5 kiaN2 Se-ti2-ka, in thok Goa2 e5 mia5 tui3 lin2 soan-thoan5 peh8-chhat8: KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh chiong in kau ti7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat e5 chhiu2; i beh ti7 lin2 e5 bin7-cheng5 thai5 in.  22). Iu5-tai7 siu7-liah8 e5 cheng3-lang5 ti7 Pa-pi2-lun5--e5, beh eng7 chi2 nng7 lang5 choe3 oe7-piN3 chiu3-chou2 lang5, kong2, Goan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa hou7 li2 chhin-chhiuN7 Se-ti2-ka A-hap, hou7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 eng7 he2 sio--i.  23). In ti7 I2-sek-liat8-tiong choe3-chhut kian3-siau3 e5 su7; im5 in chhu3-piN e5 bou2; koh thok Goa2 e5 mia5 soan-thoan5 peh8-chhat8, Goa2 sou2 bo5 beng7-leng7 in--e5; chai--e5 si7 Goa2, choe3 kan-cheng3--e5 iah8 si7 Goa2; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	24). Lun7 Ni5-hi-lan5 lang5 Si7-ma2-nga2, li2 tioh8 kong2,  25). Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3, an2-ni kong2, Li2 bat eng7 ka-ki7 e5 mia5 kia3 phoe hou7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 cheng3 peh-siN3, kap che3-si Ma2-se-nga2 e5 kiaN2 Se-hoan-nga2, kap cheng3 che3-si kong2,  26). Ia5-ho5-hoa u7 siat-lip8 li2 choe3 che3-si, lai5 thoe3 che3-si Ia5-ho5-ia5-tai7, hou7 lin2 kam-tok Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3, thang chiong it-chhe3 khong-kham2 ka-ki7 chheng choe3 sian-ti e5 lang5, eng7 chha5-ke5 ka7 i ke5, eng7 so2 ka7 i so2.  27). Hian7-kim A-na2-tut8 lang5 Ia5-li7-bi2 tui3 lin2 ka-ki7 chheng choe3 sian-ti, lin2 siaN2-su7 bo5 chek-pi7 i ah?  28). In-ui7 i kia3-phoe kau3 Pa-pi2-lun5, ka7 goan2 kong2, Siu7-liah8 e5 si5 beh ku2-tng5; lin2 tioh8 khi2 chhu3 lai5 khia7-khi2; choh-hng5 lai5 chiah8 ke2-chi2.  29). Che3-si Se-hoan-nga2 chiu7 chiong chit tiuN phoe thak8 hou7 sian-ti Ia5-li7-bi2 thiaN.  30). Tui3 an2-ni, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 Ia5-li7-bi2 kong2,  31). Li2 tioh8 kia3 phoe hou7 it-chhe3 siu7-liah8 e5 lang5 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa lun7-kau3 Ni5-hi-lan5 lang5 Si7-ma2-nga2 kong2, In-ui7 Si7-ma2-nga2 tui3 lin2 soan-thoan5--e5; Goa2 bo5 chhe i, i hou7 lin2 oa2-kho3 peh8-chhat8;  32). sou2-i2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 beh heng5-hoat8 Ni5-hi-lan5 lang5 Si7-ma2-nga2, kap i e5 hou7-e3; i tek-khak bo5 lau5 chit8 lang5 khia7-khi2 ti7 chit e5 peh-siN3 e5 tiong-kan; iah8 bo5 thang khoaN3-kiN3 Goa2 sou2 beh siuN2-su3 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 e5 hok-khi3; in-ui7 i kong2 poe7-gek8 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.

[30]	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 Ia5-li7-bi2 kong2,  2). I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KiN3-na7 Goa2 sou2 bat ka7 li2 kong2 e5 oe7, long2 tioh8 sia2 ti7 chheh--nih.  3). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, KhoaN3 ah, jit8-chi2 beh kau3, Goa2 beh hou7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 I2-sek-liat8 kap Iu5-tai7 siu7-liah8 e5 lang5 to3-tng2--lai5; Goa2 iah8 beh hou7 in to3--lai5 Goa2 sou2 siuN2-su3 in e5 liat8-chou2 e5 toe7; in chiu7 tit-tioh8 chit e5 toe7 choe3-giap8; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	4). Ia5-ho5-hoa lun7-kau3 I2-sek-liat8 kap Iu5-tai7 e5 oe7, ki3 ti7 e7-toe2.  5). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goan2 u7 thiaN-kiN3 ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah, kiaN-hiaN5, bo5 peng5-an e5 siaN.  6). TaN lin2 tioh8 khi3 mng7-khoaN3 u7 ta-pou-lang5 siN kiaN2 bo5; chaiN2-iuN7 Goa2 khoaN3-kiN3 lang5-lang5 eng7 chhiu2 jih8 io, chhin-chhiuN7 beh siN-kiaN2 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, bin7 long2 pian3 chhiN?  7). Chham2--ah, hit e5 jit8 si7 toa7, bo5 thang pi2-pheng7; si7 Nga2-kok tu2-tioh8 hoan7-lan7 e5 ki5-jit8; chong2-si7 i beh tit-tioh8 kiu3 lai5 thoat-chhut.  8). Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Kau3 hit-jit8, Goa2 beh tui3 li2 e5 am7-kun2 at-chih8 i e5 taN, chhoah-tng7 pak8 li2 e5 soh; goa7-pang lang5 bo5 koh eng7 i choe3 chhe-eng7.  9). In si7 beh hok8-sai7 in e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa, kap in e5 ong5 Tai7-pit8, chiu7-si7 Goa2 beh ka7 in heng-khi2--e5.  10). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 Nga2-kok ah, an2-ni li2 boh8-tit kiaN; I2-sek-liat8 ah, boh8-tit kiaN-hiaN5; in-ui7 Goa2 beh tui3 hng7 e5 sou2-chai7 chin2-kiu3 li2; iah8 beh tui3 siu7-liah8--khi3 e5 toe7 chin2-kiu3 li2 e5 hou7-e3; Nga2-kok beh to3--lai5 tit-tioh8 an-cheng7, peng5-an; bo5 lang5 hou7 i kiaN.  11). In-ui7 Goa2 kap li2 ti7-teh, lai5 chin2-kiu3 li2; iah8 beh chiong Goa2 sou2 koaN2 li2 kau3 hiah e5 kok it-chin7 chau5-biat8; chong2-si7 bo5 it-chin7 chau5-biat8 li2; beh chiau3 sou2 hap8-gi5--e5 chek-pi7 li2; toan3-toan3 boe7-oe7 bo5 heng5-hoat8 li2; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	12). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Li2 e5 siong boe7 i--tit, li2 e5 siong-hun5 chin siong-tiong7.  13). Bo5 lang5 thoe3 li2 pian7-hou7, hou7 li2 e5 siong-hun5 tit-tioh8 pau; li2 bo5 i-ti7 e5 ho2-ioh8.  14). ThiaN3 li2 e5 lang5 long2 boe7-ki3-tit li2, bo5 lai5 tham3 li2; in-ui7 li2 e5 choe7-koa3 chin-tang7, choe7-ok chin-choe7; Goa2 eng7 tui3-tek8 hit-khoan2 e5 phah lai5 phah li2; iah8 eng7 chan5-jim2--e5 e5 keng2-kai3, lai5 keng2-kai3 li2.  15). Li2 siaN2-su7 in-ui7 li2 e5 siong lai5 au5-kio3 ah? li2 e5 thong3-khou2 boe7 i--tit; in-ui7 li2 e5 choe7-koa3 chin-tang7, choe7-ok chin-choe7; Goa2 sou2-i2 eng7 chiah-e5 khoan2-thai7 li2.  16). Sou2-i2 kiN3-na7 thun-chiah8 li2 e5, beh siu7 thun-chiah8; li2 e5 tui3-tek8, chit8-e5 chit8-e5 long2 hou7 lang5 liah8-khi3; chhiuN2 li2--e5, beh hou7 lang5 chhiuN2, kiap li2--e5, Goa2 beh hou7 i siu7 kiap.  17). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 beh hou7 li2 e5 sin-the2 hok8-goan5, i-ho2 li2 e5 siong-hun5; in-ui7 lang5 long2 chheng li2 choe3 siu7 koaN2-tiok8--e5, kong2, Che si7 Sek-an, bo5 lang5 chhe7-kiN3--e5.
	18). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh hou7 Nga2-kok siu7 chhian-soa2 e5 pou3-piN5 to3-tng2--lai5, iah8 beh kho2-lin5 i khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7; siaN5 beh khi2 ti7 goan5-ku7 e5 chhiuN5-ki, ong5-kiong iah8 chiau3-ku7 u7 lang5 khia7-khi2.  19). Beh u7 kam2-sia7 kap khoai3-lok8--e5 e5 siaN tui3 in tiong-kan chhut--lai5; Goa2 ia7 beh hou7 in ke-thiN choe7-choe7, put-ti3 kiam2-chio2; hou7 in chun-kui3, put-ti3 pi-bi5.  20). In e5 kiaN2-ji5 beh chhin-chhiuN7 cha2-jit8; in e5 hoe7-chiong3 beh khia7-chai7 ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5; hoan7-na7 ap-che3 in--e5, Goa2 beh pan7 i.  21). In e5 kun-ong5 tek-khak si7 siok8 ti7 in--e5; chiang2-koan2 in--e5, beh tui3 in tiong-kan chhut; Goa2 beh hou7 i kun7-oa2, i iah8 beh chhin-kun7 Goa2; na7 m7-si7 an2-ni, chi7-chui7 kaN2 ho2-taN2 chhin-kun7 Goa2; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  22). Lin2 beh choe3 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3, Goa2 beh choe3 lin2 e5 Siong7-te3.
	23). KhoaN3 ah, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 siu7-khi3 chhin-chhiuN7 toa7 hong hoat-chhut; chiu7-si7 sau3-biat8 e5 toa7-hong, beh tng2-seh8 kong-kek phaiN2-lang5 e5 thau5-khak.  24). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 sim sou2 gi2-tiaN7--e5 iau2-be7 choe3, iau2-be7 chiaN5 e5 tai7-seng, I e5 toa7 siu7-khi3 tek-khak bo5 siu to3-tng2; jit8-au7 lin2 beh beng5-pek8.

[31]	Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Hit-si5 Goa2 beh choe3 I2-sek-liat8 tak8 pang5-thau5 e5 Siong7-te3; in beh choe3 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3.  2). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, I2-sek-liat8 hou7 to thai5-bo5-liau2 e5 peh-siN3, ti7 khong3-ia2 tit-tioh8 un-tian2; Goa2 khi3 hou7 in tit-tioh8 an-hioh.  3). Cha2-si5 Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 goa2 hian2-hian7, kong2, Goa2 eng7 eng2-oan2 e5 thiaN3, thiaN3 li2; in-ui7 an2-ni, Goa2 eng7 chu5-ai3 khan li2.  4). I2-sek-liat8 e5 chai7-sek-lu2 ah, Goa2 beh koh kian3-lip8 li2, li2 chiu7 tit-tioh8 kian3-lip8; li2 beh koh eng7 lin-long-kou2 choe3 chng-thaN7, kap khoai3-lok8 e5 lang5 choe3-tin7 thiau3-bu2 chhut-khi3.  5). Li2 beh koh chai-cheng3 phu5-to5-hng5 ti7 Sat-ma2-li7-a chiah e5 soaN chai-cheng3--e5 beh chai-cheng3 i, lai5 hiong2-siu7 i e5 ke2-chi2.  6). In-ui7 beh u7 chit8-jit8, I2-hoat-lian5 soaN siu2-bang7 e5 lang5 beh kio3 kong2, Khi2-lai5, lan2 chiuN7-lai5 khi3 Sek-an, kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 hia.
	7). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Lin2 tioh8 ui7 Nga2-kok chhiuN3 hoaN-hi2 e5 koa, ui7 ban7-kok-tiong choe3-thau5 e5 kok chhut toa7-siaN, thoan5-pou3 o-lo2 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu3 Li2 e5 peh-siN3 I2-sek-liat8 sou2 chhun e5 lang5.  8). KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh chhoa7 in tui3 pak-hng lai5, chu7-chip8 in tui3 toe7-kek8 lai5; kap in lai5--e5, u7 chhiN-mi5--e5, pai2-kha--e5, toa3-sin--e5, beh siN-kiaN2--e5, kui toa7-tin7 saN-kap lai5.  9). In beh thi5-khau3 lai5, Goa2 beh ti7 ki5-to2 chhoa7 in; Goa2 beh ti7 cheng3-tit8 boe7 poah8-to2 e5 lou7 chhoa7 in kau3 ho5-piN; in-ui7 Goa2 si7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 pe7, I2-hoat-lian5 choe3 Goa2 e5 toa7 kiaN2.
	10). Liat8-kok ah, tioh8 thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7, thoan5-po3 ti7 hng7 e5 hai2-su7, kong2, KoaN2-soaN3 I2-sek-liat8--e5 beh chu7-chip8 i, koh kou3-siu2 i, chhin-chhiuN7 bok8-chia2 kou3-siu2 i e5 iuN5-kun5.  11). In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa i2-keng kiu3-siok8 Nga2-kok, siok8 -hoe5 i thoat-li7 pi2 i khah kiong5--e5 e5 chhiu2.  12). In beh kau3 Sek-an koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7 chhiuN3-koa; koh beh chhin-chhiuN7 ho5-chui2 lau5, kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa un-tian2 e5 toe7, tit-tioh8 gou7-kak, chiu2, iu5, iuN5-kun5, gu5-kun5 e5 soe3-chiah--e5; in e5 sim beh chhin-chhiuN7 koan3-ak e5 hng5, long2 bo5 koh iu-khou2.  13). Hit-si5 chai7-sek-lu2 beh thiau3-bu2 lai5 hoaN-hi2, siau3-lian5-lang5 lau7-lang5 iah8 beh saN-kap hoaN-hi2; in-ui7 Goa2 beh hou7 in e5 pi-ai piN3-choe3 hoaN-hi2, iah8 beh an-ui3 in, hou7 in ti7 iu-bun7 liau2-au7 lai5 khoai3-lok8.  14). Goa2 beh eng7 iu5-ji7 hou7 che3-si e5 sim moa2-chiok; Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 iah8 beh in-ui7 Goa2 e5 un-hui7 moa2-i3; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	15). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Ti7 Lah8-ma2 thiaN-kiN3 siaN, thi5-khau3 koh toa7 siong-pi, Lah8-kiat khau3 i e5 kiaN2-ji5, m7-goan7 siu7 an-ui3, in-ui7 i e5 kiaN2 bo5--khi3.  16). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Tioh8 kim3-chi2 li2 e5 siaN, boh8-tit thi5-khau3; kim3-chi2 li2 e5 bak8-chiu, boh8-tit lau5 bak8-sai2; in-ui7 li2 choe3-kang, beh u7 po3-siuN2; in beh tui3 tui3-tek8 e5 kok to3-lai5; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  17). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Li2 e5 be2-keng2 u7 ng3-bang7, li2 e5 kiaN2-ji5 beh to3--lai5 ka-ki7 e5 keng2-lai7.  18). Goa2 sit8-chai7 u7 thiaN-kiN3 I2-hoat-lian5 ka-ki7 thong3-hun7, kong2, Li2 tok-chek goa2, goa2 chiu7 siu7 tok-chek; goa2 chhin-chhiuN7 ka3 be7-chiuN7-choa7 e5 gu5-a2, kiu5 Li2 hou7 goa2 oat8-to3-tng2, goa2 chiu7 oat8-to3-tng2; in-ui7 Li2 si7 goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  19). Goa2 oat8-to3-tng2 i2-au7 chiu7 hoan2-hoe2; siu7 ka3-si7 i2-au7, chiu7 phah kha-thui2; goa2 chiu7 kian3-siau3 lau3-khui3, in-ui7 goa2 tam-tng siau3-lian5 e5 si5 e5 leng5-jiok8.  20). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, I2-hoat-lian5 si7 Goa2 thiaN3 e5 kiaN2 mah? si7 thang hoaN-hi2 e5 gin2-na2 mah? Goa2 kiN3-na7 chek-pi7 i, iau2-ku2 chhim-chhim siau3-liam7 i; sou2-i2 Goa2 e5 sim-tng5 ui7-tioh8 i boe7 peng5-an, Goa2 tek-khak beh lin5-bin2 i.
	21). I2-sek-liat8 e5 peh-siN3 ah, li2 tioh8 ui7 ka-ki7 lip8 chi2-lou7-pai5, khia7 in2-lou7-thiau7; li2 tioh8 liu5-sim ng3 toa7-lou7, chiu7-si7 li2 sou2 khi3 e5 goan5-lou7; li2 tioh8 to3--lai5, to3-lai5 ti7 li2 chiah e5 siaN5.  22). Poe7-biu7 e5 cha-bou2-gin2-na2 ah, li2 si3-koe3 liu5 bo5 tiaN7-tioh8, beh kau3 ti7-si5 ah? Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 toe7-chiuN7 chhong3 chit8-hang7 sin e5 su7, chiu7-si7 cha-bou2-lang5 beh po2-hou7 ta-pou-lang5.
	23). Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3, an2-ni kong2, Goa2 hou7 siu7-liah8 e5 lang5 to3--lai5 e5 si5, ti7 Iu5-tai7 toe7 kap i hiah e5 siaN5, lang5 beh koh eng7 chit e5 oe7 kong2, Kong-gi7 e5 chhu3, seng3 e5 soaN ah, goan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa su3-hok li2.  24). Iu5-tai7 kap hiah e5 siaN5 e5 lang5 i2-kip8 choh-sit lang5, si3-koe3 chhi7-iuN5 e5 lang5, long2 beh saN-kap khia7-khi2 ti7-hia.  25). In-ui7 sim-sin5 ia3-sian7 e5 lang5, Goa2 i2-keng hou7 i moa2-chiok; sim-sin5 iu-bun7 e5 lang5, Goa2 i2-keng hou7 i ti-chiok.  26).  Sian-ti kong2, Goa2 khun3-chhiN2 teh siuN7, goa2 e5 khun3 chin hoaN-hi2.
	27). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, KhoaN3 ah, jit8-chi2 beh kau3, Goa2 beh hou7 I2-sek-liat8 ke kap Iu5-tai7 ke, lang5 kap cheng-siN, long2 thoan5-cheng2.  28). Goa2 cha2-cheng5 chaiN2-iuN7 choan-sim chiong in puih8-chhut, thiah-hui2, chhia-to2, biat8-bo5, khun3-khou2; iah8 beh chiau3 an2-ni choan-sim chiong in kian3-lip8, chai-cheng3; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2-e5.  29). Tng hiah e5 jit8, lang5 bo5 koh kong2, Lau7-pe7 chiah8 sng e5 phu5-to5, kiaN2 e5 chhui3-khi2 sng-nng2.  30). Tak8-lang5 beh in-ui7 ka-ki7 e5 choe7 lai5 si2; kiN3-na7 chiah8 sng e5 phu5-to5--e5, in e5 chhui3-khi2 beh nng2.
	31). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, KhoaN3 ah, jit8-chi2 beh kau3, Goa2 beh kap I2-sek-liat8 ke, Iu5-tai7 ke, lip8 sin e5 iok:  32). m7-si7 chiau3 Goa2 kap in e5 liat8-chou2 sou2 lip8 e5 iok, ti7 Goa2 khan in e5 chhiu2, chhoa7 in chhut Ai-kip8 toe7 e5 si5 sou2 lip8--e5; Goa2 sui-bong2 choe3 in e5 tiong7-hu, in iu5-goan5 poe7 Goa2 e5 iok; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  33). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Hiah e5 jit8 liau2-au7, Goa2 kap I2-sek-liat8 ke sou2 beh lip8 e5 iok si7 chit-e5; chiu7-si7 Goa2 beh eng7 Goa2 e5 lut8-hoat he7 ti7 in e5 sim-lai7, khek ti7 in e5 sim; Goa2 beh choe3 in e5 Siong7-te3, in beh choe3 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3.  34). In bo5 koh tak8-lang5 ka3-si7 in e5 chhu3-piN, kap in tak8-lang5 e5 hiaN-ti7, kong2, Lin2 tioh8 bat Ia5-ho5-hoa; in-ui7 in tui3 toa7 kau3 soe3, long2 beh bat Goa2; in-ui7 Goa2 beh sia3-bian2 in e5 choe7-koa3, bo5 koh ki3-tit in e5 choe7; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  35). Ia5-ho5-hoa siat thai3-iong5 choe3 jit8--si5 e5 kng, siat geh8 kap chhiN e5 teng7-le7 choe3 mi5--si5 e5 kng; io5-tang7 toa7-hai2, hou2 i e5 eng2 hoa7-hoa7-hau2; ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7-si7 I e5 mia5;  36). I u7 an2-ni kong2, Chiah e5 teng7-le7 na7 oe7 ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5 hoe3-bo5, I2-sek-liat8 e5 hou7-e3 chiah oe7 ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5 choat8-tng7, eng2-oan2 boe7 chiaN5-choe3 kok; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  37). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Na7 ti7 teng2-bin7 e5 thiN oe7 niu5--tit, ti7 e7-bin7 e5 toe7 chiah e5 kun-ki oe7 chhek-tok8--tit, chiu7 Goa2 tek-khak in-ui7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 hou7-e3 it-chhe3 e5 sou2-kiaN5 lai5 khi3-sak--i; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  38). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, KhoaN3 ah, jit8-chi2 beh kau3, chit e5 siaN5 beh ka7 Ia5-ho5-hoa khi2-cho7, tui3 Hap-lam5-giap8 e5 lau5, kau3 kak-thau5 e5 mng5.  39). Niu5 e5 soh koh khan chhut--khi3, tit8-kau3 Ka-lip8 soaN; oat8-tng2 kau3 Ko-a.  40). Hiat sin-si kap piaN3 he2-hu ka-nng5 e5 soaN-kok, kap it-chhe3 e5 chhan5-hng5, tit8-kau3 Khip-lun5 khoe, koh tit8-kau3 tang--si3 Be2 e5 mng5 e5 kak-thau5, long2 beh choe3-seng3, kui ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, bo5 koh puih8-chhut, bo5 koh chhia-to2, tit8-kau3 eng2-oan2.

[32]	Iu5-tai7 ong5 Se-ti2-ka te7 chap8--ni5, chiu7-si7 Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat chap8-poeh ni5, u7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 Ia5-li7-bi2.  2). Hit-si5 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 e5 kun-tui7 ui5-khun3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, sian-ti Ia5-li7-bi2 koaiN ti7 khu-liu5-sou2 e5 iN7, ti7 Iu5-tai7 ong5 e5 chhu3.  3). In-ui7 Iu5-tai7 ong5 Se-ti2-ka i2-keng chiong i koaiN-kim3, kong2, Li2 siaN2-su7 chham3-gu2 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh chiong chit e5 siaN5 kau ti7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 e5 chhiu2, i beh chhu2--i;  4). Iu5-tai7 ong5 Se-ti2-ka tek-khak boe7 thoat-li7 Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 e5 chhiu2, tiaN7-tioh8 beh kau ti7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 e5 chhiu2, iah8 beh kap i kong2 oe7, chhui3 tui3 chhui3, i e5 bak8-chiu iah8 beh khoaN3 i e5 bak8-chiu,  5). Se-ti2-ka beh hou7 i toa3 kau3 Pa-pi2-lun5, toa3 ti7-hia, kau3 Goa2 koan3-kou3 i e5 si5; lin2 sui-jian5 kap Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 kau-chian3, iah8 bo5 li7-ek? che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	6). Ia5-li7-bi2 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  7). KhoaN3 ah, li2 e5 chek Sa-liong5 e5 kiaN2 Hap-na2-biat8 beh lai5 kiN3 li2, kong2, Goa2 ti7 A-na2-tut8 hit khu chhan5, chhiaN2 li2 boe2--i; in-ui7 siok8-hoe5 e5 koan5 chai7-ti7 li2, li2 thang boe2.  8). Goa2 e5 chek e5 kiaN2 Hap-na2-biat8 ko2-jian5 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lai5 khu-liu5-sou2 e5 iN7 chhe7 goa2, tui3 goa2 kong2, Goa2 ti7 Pian7-nga2-bin2 e5 keng2-lai7, A-na2-tut8 hit khu chhan5, chhiaN2 li2 boe2; in-ui7 seng5-chiap kap siok8-hoe5 e5 koan5 chai7-ti7 li2, li2 tioh8 boe2 choe3 li2-e5; goa2 chiu7 chai che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7.  9). Goa2 chiu7 tui3 goa2 e5 chek e5 kiaN2, Hap-na2-biat8, boe2 A-na2-tut8 hit khu chhan5, pheng5 hit e5 ke3-gun5 hou7 i, kiong7 chap8-chhit sia3-khek-lek8.  10). Goa2 ti7 khoe3-bin7 chhiam mia5, chiong khoe3 hong-bat8; koh chhiaN2 lang5 lai5 choe3 ti-kiN3, iah8 eng7 thian-pheng5 pheng5 gun5 hou7 i.  11). Goa2 chiu7 theh8 chiau3 kui-le7 sou2 lip8 e5 boe2-khoe3, chiu7-si7 hong-bat8--e5 hit-tiuN, kap bo5 hong--e5 hit-tiuN;  12). tng goa2 e5 chek e5 kiaN2 Hap-na2-biat8, kap chhiam-mia5 ti7 khoe3-bin7 chiah e5 ti-kiN3, i2-kip8 che7 ti7 khu-liu5-sou2 iN7-lai7 it-chhe3 Iu5-tai7 lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5, chiong boe2-boe7 e5 khoe3 kau hou7 Ma2-se-nga2 e5 sun, Ni5-li7-a e5 kiaN2, Pa-liok8.  13). Tng in bin7-cheng5, goa2 hoan-hu3 Pa-liok8 kong2,  14). Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3, an2-ni kong2, Tioh8 chiong hong-bat8--e5 kap bo5 hong--e5, chi2 nng7 tiuN khoe3, siu ti7 hui5-khi3 e5 lai7-bin7, thang liu5-chun5 choe7-choe7 jit8.  15). In-ui7 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3, an2-ni kong2, Chiong-lai5 ti7 chit sou2-chai7 lang5 beh koh boe2 chhu3-theh8, chhan5-hng5, kap phu5-to5-hng5.
	16). Goa2 chiong boe2-khoe3 kau hou7 Ni5-li7-a e5 kiaN2 Pa-liok8 i2-au7, chiu7 ki5-to2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2,  17). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 bat eng7 toa7 koan5-leng5 kap chhun-chhut e5 chhiu2, chhong3-cho7 thiN toe7; chai7-ti7 Li2 bo5 chit8-hang7 oh-chiaN5 e5 su7;  18). Li2 si chu5-ai3 hou7 chheng-ban7 lang5, koh chiong lau7-pe7 e5 choe7-koa3 po3-eng3 ti7 i hou7-e3 e5 sin-chiuN7; chi3-toa7 choan5-leng5 e5 Siong7-te3, ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, si7 I e5 mia5.  19). Li2 e5 ke3-ek8 u7 toa7 pun2-su7, kiaN5 tai7-chi3 u7 toa7 koan5-leng5, chu3-bak8 khoaN3 se3-kan lang5 it-chhe3 e5 kiaN5-choe3, chiau3 tak8-lang5 e5 sou2-kiaN5, kap in e5 sou2-choe3 e5 hau7-ko2, lai5 po3-eng3 i.  20). Ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7 hian2-chhut sin5-jiah ki5-su7, tit8-kau3 kin-a2-jit8; ti7 I2-sek-liat8 kap pat8-lang5 e5 tiong-kan, iah8 si7 an2-ni; hou7 Li2 tit-tioh8 mia5-siaN, chhin-chhiuN7 kin-a2-jit8 chit8-iuN7;  21). eng7 sin5-jiah ki5-su7, kap toa7 koan5-leng5 e5 chhiu2, kap chhun-chhut e5 chhiu2-kut, kap toa7 thang kiaN e5 su7, chhoa7 Li2 e5 peh-siN3 I2-sek-liat8 chhut Ai-kip8 toe7;  22). chiong chit e5 lau5 ni kap bit8 e5 toe7 siuN2-su3 in, chiu7-si7 Li2 tui3 in e5 liat8-chou2 chiu3-choa7 beh hou7 in-e5.  23). In jip8--lai5 tit-tioh8 i choe3-giap8; chong2-si7 bo5 than3 Li2 e5 oe7, bo5 kiaN5 Li2 e5 lut8-hoat; Li2 it-chhe3 beng7-leng7 in kiaN5--e5, in bo5 kiaN5 chit8-hang7; sou2-i2 Li2 hou7 long2-chong2 e5 chai-e7 kau3 ti7 in.  24). KhoaN3 ah, u7 koaiN5 e5 thou5-tui, in i2-keng pek-oa2 chit e5 siaN5, beh chhu2--i; siaN5 iah8 in-ui7 to-kiam3, ki-hng, un-ek8, kau hou7 kong-kek i e5 Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 e5 chhiu2, Li2 sou2 kong2--e5 i2-keng chiaN5, Li2 iah8 chhin-bak8 khoaN3-kiN3.  25). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 ka7 goa2 kong2, tioh8 ui7 ka-ki7 eng7 gun5 boe2 chhan5, koh chhiaN2 lang5 choe3 ti-kiN3; taN chit e5 siaN5 i2-keng kau ti7 Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 e5 chhiu2 lah.
	26). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 Ia5-li7-bi2 kong2,  27). KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, si7 kiN3-u7 hiat-khi3--e5 e5 Siong7-te3, chai7-ti7 Goa2 kiam2 u7 chit8-hang7 oh-chiaN5 e5 su7?  28). Sou2-i2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh chiong chit e5 siaN5 kau hou7 Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 e5 chhiu2, kap Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat e5 chhiu2, i beh chhu2--i.  29). Kong siaN5 e5 Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 beh lai5, pang3 he2 sio chit e5 siaN5, i2-kip8 chhu3-theh8; ti7 chiah e5 chhu3-teng2, lang5 bat ng3 Pa-lek8 sio-hiuN, ng3 pat8 e5 siong7-te3 koan3-tian7, jia2 Goa2 e5 siu7-khi3.  30). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kap Iu5-tai7 lang5, tui3 siau3-lian5 i2-lai5, choan-choan kiaN5 Goa2 bak8-chiu-tiong khoaN3-choe3 phaiN2 e5 su7; I2-sek-liat8 lang5 it-chin7 eng7 chhiu2 sou2 choe3--e5, jia2 Goa2 e5 siu7-khi3; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  31). Chit e5 siaN5 tui3 khi2-cho7 e5 jit8 kau3 kin-a2-jit8, siong5-siong5 jia2 Goa2 e5 siu7-khi3, hou7 goa2 au3-nau2; ti3-kau3 Goa2 ka7 i tu5--khi3 li7-khui Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5.  32). Si7 in-ui7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kap Iu5-tai7 lang5 it-chhe3 e5 sia5-ok; chiu7-si7 in kap in e5 kun-ong5, kui3-chok8, che3-si, sian-ti, kap Iu5-tai7 e5 cheng3-lang5, i2-kip8 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3, sou2 kiaN5--e5, jia2 Goa2 e5 siu7-khi3.  33). In eng7 ka-chiah ng3 Goa2, bo5 eng7 bin7; Goa2 sui-jian5 ka3-si7 in, si7 cha2-cha2 khi2-lai5 ka3-si7 in; chong2-si7 in bo5 thiaN-than3, lai5 siu7 ka3-si7.  34). In keng2-jian5 eng7 in khou2-ouN3 e5 mih8, he7 ti7 eng7 Goa2 e5 mia5 sou2 chheng e5 chhu3, lai5 phah la5-sam5--i.  35). In ti7 Pian7-him-lun3 e5 soaN-kok khi2 Pa-lek8 e5 koaiN5-tai5, beh hou7 in e5 kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2 keng-ke3 he2 kui Mou5-lok8; in kiaN5 che kho2-ouN3 e5 su7, hou7 Iu5-tai7 ham7-loh8 choe7; che m7-si7 Goa2 sou2 beng7-leng7--e5, iah8 m7-si7 Goa2 e5 sim sou2 siuN7--e5.
	36). TaN lun7-kau3 chit e5 siaN5, si7 lin2 sou2 kong2 i2-keng in-ui7 to-kiam3, ki-hng, un-ek8, kau ti7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 e5 chhiu2--e5; I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2:  37). KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 ti7 siu7-khi3, au3-nau2, toa7 siu7-khi3 e5 tiong-kan, chiong in koaN2 kau3 tak8-kok, au7-lai5 Goa2 beh tui3-hia chio-chip8 in chhut--lai5, chhoa7 in to3-lai5 chit sou2-chai7, hou7 in an-jian5 khia7-khi2.  38). In beh choe3 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3, Goa2 beh choe3 in e5 Siong7-te3.  39). Goa2 beh hou7 in it-sim it-lou7, hou7 in siong5-siong5 keng3-ui3 Goa2, hou7 in kap in e5 kiaN2-sun tit-tioh8 hok-khi3.  40). Goa2 beh kap in lip8 eng2-oan2 e5 iok, chiu7-si7 bo5 oat8-tng2 li7-khui in, si7 beh su3-hok hou7 in; koh hou7 in chun5-sim keng3-ui3 Goa2, bo5 oat8-tng2 li7-khui Goa2.  41). Goa2 beh hoaN-hi2 in, su3-hok hou7 in, Goa2 sit8-chai7 beh chin7-sim chin7-i3, chai-poe5 in ti7 chit e5 sou2-chai7.  42). In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 chaiN2-iuN7 hou7 chit-e5 it-chhe3 toa7 e5 chai-e7 lim5-kau3 chit e5 peh-siN3, Goa2 iah8 beh an2-ni hou7 Goa2 sou2 eng3-un2 in it-chhe3 e5 hok-khi3 lim5-kau3 in.  43). Lin2 kong2, Chit e5 sou2-chai7 si7 pha-hng, bo5 lang5, bo5 cheng-siN; si7 kau hou7 Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 e5 chhiu2--e5; chiong-lai5 lang5 beh koh ti7 chit sou2-chai7 boe2 chhan5-hng5.  44). Ti7 Pian7-nga2-bin2 toe7, ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 si3-ui5, ti7 Iu5-tai7 chiah e5 siaN5, ti7 soaN-toe7 chiah e5 siaN5, ti7 piN5-iuN5 chiah e5 siaN5, kap ti7 lam5-hng chiah e5 siaN5, lang5 beh eng7 gun5 boe2-chhan5, ti7 khoe3-bin7 chhiam-mia5, chiong khoe3 hong-bat8, chhiaN2 lang5 choe3 ti-kiN3; in-ui7 Goa2 beh hou7 siu7-liah8 e5 lang5 to3--lai5; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.

[33]	Ia5-li7-bi2 iau2-ku2 koaiN ti7 khu-liu5-sou2 e5 iN7-lai7, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 te7-ji7-pai2 lim5-kau3 i kong2,  2). KiaN5 i--e5 e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, ke3-ek8 lai5 kian3-lip8 i--e5 e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 I e5 mia5, I an2-ni kong2,  3). Li2 kiu5 Goa2, Goa2 chiu7 in3 li2, iah8 chiong li2 sou2 m7-chai, toa7 koh oh-tit e5 su7, chi2-si7 li2.  4). Lun7-kau3 chit e5 siaN5-lai7 e5 chhu3, kap Iu5-tai7 ong5 e5 chhu3, chiu7-si7 thiah-hui2 lai5 ti2-tng tui3-tek8 e5 thou5-tui, kap ti2-tng to-kiam3--e5;  5). I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Lang5 beh lai5 kap Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 kau-chian3, put-ko3 si7 hou7 sin-si chhiong-moa2 chiah e5 chhu3, chiu7-si7 Goa2 ti7 siu7-khi3 kap toa7 siu7-khi3 e5 tiong-kan sou2 thai5-si2 e5 lang5, in-ui7 in it-chhe3 e5 phaiN2, Goa2 chiu7 ng Goa2 e5 bin7, m7-khoaN3 chit e5 siaN5.  6). KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh hou7 i e5 siong hok8-goan5, koh eng7 ho2-ioh8 i-ho2--i; koh chiong hong-seng7 e5 peng5-an kap seng5-sit8 hian2-beng5 ti7 in.  7). Goa2 iah8 beh hou7 Iu5-tai7 siu7-liah8--e5, kap I2-sek-liat8 siu7-liah8--e5, to3-tng2 lai5; koh kian3-lip8 in chhin-chhiuN7 khi2-thau5.  8). Goa2 beh soe2-tu5 in it-chhe3 kan-hoan7 Goa2 e5 choe7; Goa2 iah8 beh sia3-bian2 in it-chhe3 kan-hoan7 Goa2, poe7-poan7 Goa2 chiah e5 choe7.  9). Chit e5 siaN5 beh ti ban7-kok ka7 Goa2 choe3 hoaN-hi2 e5 mia5, choe3 o-lo2, choe3 eng5-kng; in-ui7 ban7-kok thiaN-kiN3 Goa2 sou2 siuN2-su3 ti7 in it-chhe3 e5 hok-khi3, ia7 ui7-tioh8 Goa2 sou2 siuN2-su3 it-chhe3 e5 hok-khi3 kap peng5-an, beh kiaN-hiaN5 ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah.
	10). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Lin2 lun7-kau3 chit e5 toe7-hng u7 kong2, Si7 pha-hng, bo5 lang5, bo5 cheng-siN e5 toe7-hng; chong2-si7 ti7 chit sou2-chai7 i2-kip8 pha-hng, bo5 lang5, bo5 jin5-ian, bo5 cheng-siN e5 Iu5-tai7 chiah e5 siaN5, kap Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 koe-chhi7,  11). beh koh thiaN-kiN3 u7 hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN, khoai3-lok8 e5 siaN, sin-kiaN2-sai3 e5 siaN, sin-niu5 e5 siaN; iah8 u7 lang5 e5 siaN, chiu7-si7 hiah e5 toa3 sia7-un e5 che3 kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3--e5, teh kong2, Tioh8 kam2-sia7 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 ho2, I e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh; in-ui7 Goa2 beh hou7 chit sou2-chai7 siu7-liah8 e5 lang5 to3-tng2--lai5, chhin-chhiuN7 khi2-thau5 chit8-iuN7; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  12). Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Ti7 chit e5 pha-hng, bo5 lang5, bo5 cheng-siN e5 toe7-hng, kap ki5-tiong sou2 u7 e5 siaN5, beh koh u7 bok8-chia2 khia7-khi2, hou7 in e5 iuN5-kun5 to2 ti7-hia.  13). Ti7 soaN-toe7 chiah e5 siaN5, piN5-iuN5 chiah e5 siaN5, lam5-hng chiah e5 siaN5, Pian7-nga2-bin2, Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 chiu-ui5, kap Iu5-tai7 chiah e5 siaN5, beh koh u7 iuN5-kun5 keng-ke3 sng3 e5 lang5 e5 chhiu2; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	14). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, KhoaN3 ah, jit8-chi2 beh kau3, Goa2 eng3-un2 I2-sek-liat8-ke kap Iu5-tai7-ke e5 ho2-oe7, Goa2 beh hou7 i chiaN5.  15). Tng hit-jit8 hit-si5 Goa2 beh ka7 Tai7-pit8 hoat-siN gi7 e5 Ki, I beh ti7 toe7-chiuN7 kiaN5 kong-peng5 kap kong-gi7.  16). Ti7 hit-jit8 Iu5-tai7 beh tit-tioh8 kiu3, Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 beh an-jian5 khia7-khi2; i e5 mia5 beh chheng-choe3, Ia5-ho5-hoa lan2 e5 gi7.  17). In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Tai7-pit8 beh eng2-oan2 u7 lang5 che7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 po2-cho7.  18). Che3-si, Li7-bi7 lang5, iah8 eng2-oan2 u7 lang5 hian3 sio-che3 le2-mih8; siong5-siong5 pan7-li2 hian3-che3 e5 su7 ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5.
	19). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 Ia5-li7-bi2 kong2,  20). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Lin2 na7 oe7 hoe3-bo5 Goa2 sou2 lip8 jit8--si5 e5 iok, mi5--si5 e5 iok, hou7 jit8-mi5 bo5 chiau3 in e5 si5;  21). chiu7 oe7 hoe3-bo5 Goa2 kap Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 Tai7-pit8 sou2 lip8 e5 iok, hou7 i bo5 u7 kiaN2 ti7 i e5 po2-cho7 choe3 ong5; iah8 oe7 hoe3-bo5 Goa2 kap hok8-sai7 Goa2 e5 che3-si Li7-bi7 lang5 sou2 lip8 e5 iok.  22). ThiN e5 siong7 boe7 sng3--tit, hai2 e5 soa boe7 niu5--tit, Goa2 beh chiau3 an2-ni hou7 Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 Tai7-pit8 e5 hou7-e3, kap hok8-sai7 Goa2 e5 Li7-bi7 lang5, ke-thiN choe7-choe7.  23). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 koh lim5-kau3 Ia5-li7-bi2 kong2,  24). Chiah e5 peh-siN3 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, li2 bo5 thiaN-kiN3 mah? in kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 keng2 e5 nng7-chok8, I i2-keng khi3-choat8--i, in an2-ni khoaN3-khin Goa2 e5 peh-siN3, liah8-choe3 boe7 koh chiaN5 kok ti7 in e5 bin7-cheng5.  25). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 sou2 lip8 jit8--si5 mi5--si5 e5 iok na7 oe7 bo5--khi3, Goa2 na7 bo5 siat thiN-toe7 e5 teng7-le7;  26). Goa2 chiu7 oe7 khi3-sak Nga2-kok kap Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 Tai7-pit8 e5 hou7-e3 ti3-kau3 bo5 tui3 i e5 hou7-e3 chhu2 lang5 ti7-li2 A-pek-lah8-han2, I2-sat, Nga2-kok e5 hou7-e3.  In-ui7 Goa2 beh hou7 in siu7-liah8 e5 lang5 to3-lai5, iah8 beh lin5-bin2 in.

[34]	Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat chhoa7 i long2-chong2 e5 kun-peng, kap i sou2 koan2 toe7-chiuN7 e5 ban7-kok tak8-chok8, lai5 kong-kek Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, i2-kip8 hiah-e5 siok8--i e5 siaN5; hit-si5 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 Ia5-li7-bi2 kong2,  2). Ia5-ho5-hoa I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 an2-ni kong2, Li2 tioh8 khi3 ka7 Iu5-tai7 ong5 Se-ti2-ka kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh chiong chit e5 siaN5 kau ti7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 e5 chhiu2, i beh eng7 he2 sio--i.  3). Li2 boe7-oe7 thoat-li7 i e5 chhiu2, tek-khak siu7 liah8, kau ti7 i e5 chhiu2-thau5, li2 e5 bak8-chiu beh khoaN3 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 e5 bak8-chiu, i beh kap li2 chhui3 tui3 chhui3 kong2-oe7, li2 iah8 beh kau3 Pa-pi2-lun5.  4). Iu5-tai7 ong5 Se-ti2-ka ah, Li2 iau2-ku2 tioh8 thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7.  Ia5-ho5-hoa lun7-kau3 li2 an2-ni kong2, Li2 tek-khak bo5 hou7 to-kiam3 thai5-si2; li2 beh peng5-an ke3-si3;  5). lang5 beh ui7 li2 sio phang e5 mih8, chhin-chhiuN7 ui7-tioh8 li2 e5 liat8-chou2, chiu7-si7 li2 i2-cheng5 e5 sian-ong5 sou2 sio--e5 chit8-iuN7.  Lang5 beh ui7-tioh8 li2 ai-siong, kong2, Chham2 ah, goa2 e5 chu2 ah.  Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Chit e5 oe7 Goa2 i2-keng kong2--i lah.  6). Tui3 an2-ni, sian-ti Ia5-li7-bi2 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 chiong che it-chhe3 e5 oe7 ka7 Iu5-tai7 ong5 Se-ti2-ka kong2.  7). Hit-si5 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 e5 kun-peng teh kong-kek Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, koh kong-kek Iu5-tai7 sou2 chhun e5 siaN5, chiu7-si7 Lah8-kiat kap A-se-ka; in-ui7 Iu5-tai7 kian-kou3 e5 siaN5, chi2 u7 chhun chiah-e5.
	8). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 koh lim5-kau3 Ia5-li7-bi2.  9). Si7 in-ui7 Se-ti2-ka ong5 kap Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 cheng3 peh-siN3 lip8-iok, ka7 in soan-pou3 thau2-pang3; chiu7-si7 tak8-lang5 tioh8 thau2-pang3 i e5 lou5-pok8 lu2-pi7, hoan7-na7 Hi-pek-lai5 e5 lam5-lu2, hou7 in chu7-iu5, bo5 lang5 thang koh eng7 i e5 hiaN-ti7 Iu5-tai7 lang5 choe3 lou5-pok8.  10). U7 hun7 chit e5 iok e5 kui3-chok8 kap cheng3 peh-siN3, thiaN-kiN3 tak8-lang5 tioh8 thau2-pang3 i e5 lou5-pok8 lu2-pi7, hou7 i chu7-iu5, bo5 koh eng7 i choe3 chhe-eng7, in chiu7 chun-than3 lai5 thau2-pang3.  11). Au7-lai5 chiu7 the3-hoe2, hou7 in sou2 thau2-pang3 chu7-iu5 e5 lou5-pok8 lu2-pi7 to3--lai5, bian2-kiong2 in iu5-goan5 choe3 lou5-pok8 lu2-pi7.  12). In-ui7 an2-ni, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lim5-kau3 Ia5-li7-bi2, kong2,  13). Ia5-ho5-hoa I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 an2-ni kong2, Goa2 chhoa7 lin2 e5 liat8-chou2 tui3 Ai-kip8 toe7 choe3 lou5-chai5 e5 ke chhut-lai5 e5 jit8, kap in lip8-iok, kong2,  14). Kau3 te7 chhit ni5, lin2 tioh8 tak8-lang5 thau2-pang3 i e5 hiaN-ti7 Hi-pek-lai5 lang5, boe7 hou7 li2--e5; i i2-keng hok8-sai7 li2 lak8-ni5, li2 tioh8 thau2-pang3--i, li7-khui li2 lai5 chu7-iu5; chong2-si7 lin2 e5 liat8-chou2 m7-thiaN Goa2, iah8 bo5 aN3 hi7-khang.  15). TaN lin2 i2-keng koe2-piN3, kiaN5 Goa2 sou2 khoaN3 choe3 cheng3-tit8 e5 su7; tak8-lang5 tui3 chhu3-piN soan-pou3 thau2-pang3, koh ti7 eng7 Goa2 e5 mia5 lai5 chheng e5 chhu3, ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5 lip8-iok.  16). Chong2-si7 lin2 iu7-koh the3-hoe2, siat-tok8 Goa2 e5 mia5, tak8-lang5 hou7 sou2 thau2-pang3 tit-tioh8 chu7-iu5 e5 lou5-pok8 lu2-pi7 to3-tng2, bian2-kiong2 in iu5-goan5 choe3 lin2 e5 lou5-pok8 lu2-pi7.  17). Sou2-i2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Lin2 bo5 thiaN-than3 Goa2, tak8-lang5 tui3 i e5 hiaN-ti7, tui3 i e5 chhu3-piN soan-thoan5 thau2-pang3, khoaN3 ah, Goa2 tui3 lin2 soan-thoan5 thau2-pang3 hou7 to-kiam3, un-ek8, ki-hng, koh hou7 lin2 liu5-loh8 ti7 thiN-e7 ban7-kok tiong; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2-e5.  18). KiN3-na7 poe7 Goa2 e5 iok, bo5 than3 hit e5 iok e5 oe7, chiu7-si7 phoa3-khui gu5-a2 lai5 keng-ke3 hit tiong-kan e5 si5, ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5 sou2 lip8--e5;  19). chiu7-si7 Iu5-tai7 e5 kui3-chok8, Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 kui3-chok8, i2-kip8 thai3-kam3, che3-si, keng2-lai7 cheng3 peh-siN3, kiN3-na7 tui3 phoa3-khui e5 gu5-a2 e5 tiong-kan keng-ke3--e5;  20). Goa2 beh chiong in kau ti7 in e5 tui3-tek8 e5 chhiu2, kap siau3-siuN7 in e5 siN3-mia7 e5 lang5 e5 chhiu2; in e5 sin-si beh hou7 khong-tiong e5 pe-chiau2 kap toe7-chiuN7 e5 ia2-siu3 choe3 chiah8-mih8.  21). Koh Goa2 beh chiong Iu5-tai7 ong5 Se-ti2-ka kap i e5 kui3-chok8 kau ti7 in e5 tui3-tek8 e5 chhiu2, kap siau3-siuN7 i e5 siN3-mia7 e5 lang5 e5 chhiu2; iah8 kau ti7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 kun-peng e5 chhiu2, chiu7-si7 li7-khui lin2 khi3--e5.  22). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 beh beng7-leng7 in, hou7 in koh lai5 chit e5 siaN5; in beh kong-kek--i, chhu2--i, eng7 he2 sio--i; Goa2 iah8 beh hou7 Iu5-tai7 chiah e5 siaN5 pha-hng, bo5 lang5 khia7-khi2.

[35]	Tng Iu5-tai7 ong5 Iok-se-a e5 kiaN2 Iok-nga2-keng3 che7-ui7 e5 si5, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 Ia5-li7-bi2 kong2,  2). Li2 tioh8 khi3 Li7-kah chok8 e5 chhu3, kap in kong2-oe7; chhoa7 in kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3, jip8 chit8 keng pang5, eng7 chiu2 hou7 in lim.  3). Goa2 chiu7 chiong Hap-pa-se2-ni5-nga2 e5 sun, Nga2-li7-bi2-nga2 e5 kiaN2, Nga2-sat-ni5-a, kap i e5 hiaN-ti7, kap i e5 cheng3-kiaN2, i2-kip8 Li7-kah choan5-chok8 e5 lang5,  4). chhoa7 in kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3, jip8 Siong7-te3 e5 lou5-pok8 I-ki-tai7-li7 e5 kiaN2 Hap-lan5 cheng3-kiaN2 e5 pang5; hit keng pang5 ti7 kui3-chok8 e5 pang5 e5 keh-piah, kui3-chok8 e5 pang5 chiu7-si7 ti7 Sa-liong5 e5 kiaN2 pe2-mng5--e5 Ma2-se-nga2 e5 pang5 e5 teng2-bin7.  5).
