Goa2 chiu7 eng7 oaN2 eng7 poe toe2 chiu2 moa2-moa2, pai5 ti7 Li7-kah chok8 lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5; ka7 in kong2, ChhiaN2 lin2 lim chiu2.  6). In chiu7 kong2, Goan2 m7-lim chiu2, in-ui7 goan2 e5 sian-chou2, Li7-kah e5 kiaN2 Iok-na2-tat8, bat hoan-hu3 goan2 kong2, Lin2 kap lin2 e5 kiaN2-sun eng2-eng2 m7-thang lim chiu2.  7). Iah8 m7-thang khi2 chhu3, m7-thang ia7-cheng2, m7-thang chai-cheng3 phu5-to5-hng5, m7-thang u7 chiah-e5; chit8-si3-lang5 tioh8 toa3 ti7 pou3-piN5, hou7 lin2 tng5 he3-siu7 ti7 lin2 kia3-kha e5 toe7-hng.  8). KiN3-na7 goan2 sian-chou2 Li7-kah e5 kiaN2 Iok-na2-tat8 hoan-hu3 goan2 e5 oe7, goan2 long2 thiaN-than3; goan2 kap goan2 e5 bou2, goan2 e5 kiaN2, goan2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, chit8-si3-lang5 long2 bo5 lim-chiu2.  9). Iah8 bo5 khi2-chhu3 lai5 ka-ki7 khia7-khi2, iah8 bo5 u7 phu5-to5-hng5, bo5 u7 chhan5-hng5, bo5 u7 cheng2-chi2.  10). tok8-tok8 khia7-khi2 pou3-piN5, long2 chun-than3 goan2 e5 sian-chou2, Iok-na2-tat8 sou2 beng7-leng7--e5 lai5 kiaN5.  11). Tok8-tok8 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat chiuN7-lai5 chit e5 toe7 e5 si5, goan2 chiu7 kong2, Lai5 ah, lan2 tioh8 chiuN7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, lai5 siam2-pi7 Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 e5 peng, kap A-lan5 e5 peng; in-ui7 an2-ni, goan2 chiah khia7-khi2 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2.
	12). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 Ia5-li7-bi2 kong2,  13). Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3, an2-ni kong2, Li2 tioh8 khi3 ka7 Iu5-tai7 lang5 kap Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Lin2 m7-siu7 ka3-si7, m7 thiaN-than3 Goa2 e5 oe7 mah?  14). Li7-kah e5 kiaN2 Iok-na2-tat8 sou2 hoan-hu3 i e5 kiaN2-sun m7-thang lim chiu2 e5 oe7, in long2 chun-siu2, kau3 kin-a2-jit8 iah8 bo5 lim; in-ui7 in thiaN-than3 sian-chou2 e5 beng7-leng7; chong2-si7 Goa2 u7 tui3 lin2 kong2, cha2-cha2 khi2-lai5 kong2; na7-si7 lin2 m7-thiaN Goa2.  15). Goa2 iah8 chhe Goa2 e5 cheng3 lou5-pok8 chiah e5 sian-ti chiu7-kun7 lin2, cha2-cha2 khi2-lai5 chhe in, kong2, Lin2 tioh8 oat8-thau5, tak8-lang5 li7-khui i e5 phaiN2-lou7, koe2-oaN7 lin2 e5 sou2-choe3; bo5 than3 pat8-ho7 e5 siong7-te3 lai5 hok8-sai7 in, lin2 chiu7 thang khia7-khi2 Goa2 sou2 siuN2-su3 lin2 kap lin2 liat8-chou2 e5 toe7; chong2-si7 lin2 m7 aN3 hi7-khang, iah8 m7-thiaN Goa2.  16). In-ui7 Li7-kah e5 kiaN2 Iok-na2-tat8 e5 kiaN2-sun u7 chun-siu2 in e5 sian-chou2 sou2 hoan-hu3 in e5 beng7-leng7, tok8-tok8 chit e5 peh-siN3 bo5 u7 thiaN-than3 Goa2;  17). sou2-i2 Ia5-ho5-hoa, ban7-kun e5 Siong7-te3, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh hou7 Goa2 sou2 kong2 kong-kek in it-chhe3 e5 chai-e7 lim5-kau3 Iu5-tai7 lang5 kap Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 it-chhe3 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3; in-ui7 Goa2 tui3 in kong2, in bo5 u7 thiaN-than3; Goa2 kio3--in, in bo5 in3.  18). Ia5-li7-bi2 tui3 Li7-kah chok8 e5 lang5 kong2, Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3, an2-ni kong2, In-ui7 lin2 thiaN-than3 lin2 e5 sian-chou2 Iok-na2-tat8 e5 beng7-leng7, siu2 i it-chhe3 e5 kai3-beng7, kiaN5 i long2-chong2 sou2 beng7-leng7 lin2--e5;  19). sou2-i2 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3, an2-ni kong2, Li7-kah e5 kiaN2 Iok-na2-tat8 tek-khak eng2-oan2 u7 lang5 khia7 ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5.

[36]	Iu5-tai7 ong5 Iok-se-a e5 kiaN2 Iok-nga2-keng3 te7 si3--ni5, u7 oe7 tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lim5-kau3 Ia5-li7-bi2 kong2,  2). Li2 tioh8 theh8 chit8 pun2 chheh, chiong Goa2 sou2 tui3 li2 kong2 beh kong-kek I2-sek-liat8 kap Iu5-tai7, kap tak8-kok, it-chhe3 e5 oe7; tui3 Goa2 ka7 li2 kong2-oe7 e5 hit-jit8, chiu7-si7 tui3 Iok-se-a hiah e5 jit8 khi2, kau3 ti7 kin-a2-jit8; long2 sia2 ti7 hi2 lai7-bin7.  3). Kiam2-chhai2 Iu5-tai7 ke beh thiaN Goa2 sou2 an3-sng3 beh kang3 hou7 in it-chhe3 e5 chai-e7; ti3-kau3 in beh oat8-thau5, tak8-lang5 li7-khui i e5 phaiN2-lou7; Goa2 chiu7 thang sia3-bian2 in e5 choe7-koa3 kap choe7-ok.
	4). Ia5-li7-bi2 chiu7 kio3 Ni5-li7-a e5 kiaN2 Pa-liok8 lai5; Pa-liok8 chiu7 chiong Ia5-li7-bi2 sou2 thoan5 Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 i kong2 it-chhe3 e5 oe7, long2 ki3 ti7 chheh.  5). Ia5-li7-bi2 hoan-hu3 Pa-liok8 kong2, Goa2 siu7 chou2-gai7, boe7-oe7 jip8 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3.  6). Li2 tioh8 khi3, chiong goa2 sou2 thoan5, li2 sou2 sia2 ti7 chheh--nih Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7, ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3, ti7 kim3-chiah8 e5 jit8 thak8 hou7 peh-siN3 thiaN; iah8 thak8 hou7 tui3 chiah e5 siaN5 lai5 e5 Iu5-tai7 lang5 thiaN.  7). Kiam2-chhai2 in beh ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5 khiam-pi ki5-to2; in beh hoe5-thau5, tak8-lang5 li7-khui i e5 phaiN2-lou7; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 chit e5 peh-siN3 sou2 kong2 beh hoat-chhut e5 siu7-khi3, hit e5 siu7-khi3 chin toa7.  8). Ni5-li7-a e5 kiaN2 Pa-liok8 chiu7 chiau3 sian-ti Ia5-li7-bi2 it-chhe3 sou2 hoan-hu3--e5 khi3 kiaN5; ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3, thak8 chheh-lai7 sou2 ki3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7.
	9). Iu5-tai7 ong5 Iok-se-a  e5 kiaN2 Iok-nga2-keng3 gou7--ni5, kau2 geh8, Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 cheng3 peh-siN3, kap hiah-e5 tui3 Iu5-tai7 siaN5 lai5 kau3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 cheng3 peh-siN3; soan-pou3 kim3-chiah8 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5.  10). Hit-si5 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3, su-ki3 Sa-hoan e5 kiaN2 Ki-ma2-li7-nga2 e5 pang5, ti7 teng2-iN7, kun7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3, sin-mng5 e5 mng5-khau2, Pa-liok8 tui3 hit pun2 chheh thak8 Ia5-li7-bi2 e5 oe7, hou7 cheng3 peh-siN3 chhin-hi7 thiaN.  11). Sa-hoan e5 sun, Ki-ma2-li7-nga2 e5 kiaN2, Bi2-kai-a thiaN-kiN3 chheh-lai7 Ia5-ho5-hoa it-chhe3 e5 oe7,  12). i chiu7 loh8-khi3 ong5-kiong, jip8 su-ki3 e5 pang5; khoaN3 ah, cheng3 kui3-chok8 long2 che7 ti7-hia, chiu7-si7 su-ki3 I2-li7-sa-ma2, Si7-ma2-nga2 e5 kiaN2 Te7-lai5-nga2, A-kek-pho e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-na2-tan, Sa-hoan e5 kiaN2 Ki-ma2-li7-nga2, Hap-na2-ni5-nga2 e5 kiaN2 Se-ti2-ka, kap long2-chong2 e5 kui3-chok8.  13). Tui3 an2-ni Bi2-kai-a tui3 in kong2-khi2 i sou2 thiaN-kiN3 it-chhe3 e5 oe7, chiu7-si7 Pa-liok8 tui3 peh-siN3 thak8 hit pun2 chheh e5 si5 i sou2 thiaN-kiN3 e5.  14). In-ui7 an2-ni chiah e5 kui3-chok8 chiu7 chhe Kou2-si7 e5 cheng-sun, Si7-li7-bi2-nga2 e5 sun, Ni5-tham3-nga2 e5 kiaN2 Iu5-ti2 kau3 Pa-liok8 hia, tui3 i kong2, Li2 chiong sou2 thak8 hou7 peh-siN3 thiaN e5 chheh chhin-chhiu2 theh8--lai5.  Ni5-li7-a e5 kiaN2 Pa-liok8 chiu7 chhin-chhiu2 theh8 hit pun2 chheh lai5 in hia.  15). In tui3 i kong2, ChhiaN2 che7, thak8 hou7 goan2 thiaN; Pa-liok8 chiu7 thak8 hou7 in thiaN.  16). In thiaN che it-chhe3 e5 oe7, chiu7 tai7-ke kiaN-hiaN5 saN-khoaN3; ka7 Pa-liok8 kong2, Goan2 koat-toan3 beh chiong chiah e5 oe7 long2 ka7 ong5 kong2.  17). In koh mng7 Pa-liok8 kong2, ChhiaN2 li2 ka7 goan2 kong2, li2 eng7 siaN2 khoan2 lai5 sia2 i sou2 thoan5 it-chhe3 e5 oe7?  18). Pa-liok8 in3 kong2, I chhin-chhui3 tui3 goa2 kong2 chiah e5 oe7, goa2 chiu7 eng7 pit-bak8 sia2 ti7 chheh--nih.  19). Hiah e5 kui3-chok8 tui3 Pa-liok8 kong2, Li2 kap Ia5-li7-bi2 tioh8 khi3 bih--teh, m7-thang hou7 lang5 chai lin2 ti7 toh-loh8.
	20). Hiah e5 kui3-chok8 chiong hit pun2 he7 ti7 su-ki3 I2-li7-sa-ma2 e5 pang5, chiah jip8 iN7 kiN3 ong5, chiong chiah e5 oe7 long2 kong2-khi2 hou7 ong5 thiaN.  21). Ong5 chhe Iu5-ti2 khi3 theh8 hit-pun2 lai5, i chiu7 tui3 su-ki3 I2-li7-sa-ma2 e5 pang5 theh8--lai5.  Iu5-ti2 thak8 hou7 ong5 thiaN, iah8 hou7 khia7 ti7 ong5 cho2-iu7 chiah e5 kui3-chok8 thiaN.  22). Hit-si5 si7 kau2--geh8, ong5 che7 ti7 ke3 tang-thiN e5 chhu3, bin7-thau5-cheng5 u7 he2-lou5 teh toh8.  23). Iu5-ti2 kian3 thak8 saN-phiN a2 si3-phiN, ong5 chiu7 eng7 su-ki3 e5 to ka7 i koah-khi2--lai5, hiat ti7 he2-lou5, kau3 choan5-pun2 long2 sio ti7 lou5-tiong e5 he2.  24). Ong5 kap thiaN-kiN3 chiah e5 oe7 e5 jin5-sin5, in long2 bo5 kiaN iah8 bo5 thiah-lih8 in e5 saN.  25). I2-li7-na2-tan kap Te7-lai5-nga2, Ki-ma2-li7-nga2, kiu5 ong5 boh8-tit sio hit-pun2; chong2-si7 i m7 thiaN.  26). Ong5 chiu7 beng7-leng7 Hap-bi2-lek8 e5 kiaN2 Ia5-lah8-biat8, kap A-su-liat8 e5 kiaN2 Se-lai5-nga2, kap A-pek-tiap8 e5 kiaN2 Si7-li7-bi2-nga2; khi3 liah8 su-ki3 Pa-liok8 kap sian-ti Ia5-li7-bi2; chong2-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa ka7 in khng3-bat8.
	27). Ong5 chiong hit-pun2, chiu7-si7 Pa-liok8 sou2 sia2 Ia5-li7-bi2 sou2 thoan5 e5 oe7, sio--khi3 liau2-au7, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 Ia5-li7-bi2 kong2,  28). Li2 koh theh8 chit8-pun2, chiong Iu5-tai7 ong5 Iok-nga2-keng3 sou2 sio chiong5-cheng5 hit-pun2 hiah e5 oe7 long2 sia2 ti7 hit lai7-bin7.  29). Lun7-kau3 Iu5-tai7 ong5 Iok-nga2-keng3, li2 tioh8 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Li2 sio hit pun2, kong2, Li2 siaN2-su7 ti7 hit lai7-bin7 sia2 kong2, Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 koat-toan3 beh lai5 hui2-biat8 chit e5 thou2-toe7, hou7 chit sou2-chai7 e5 lang5 kap cheng-siN long2 bo5--khi3 ah?  30). Sou2-i2 Ia5-ho5-hoa lun7 Iu5-tai7 ong5 Iok-nga2-keng3 kong2, I beh bo5 lang5 thang che7 Tai7-pit8 e5 po2-cho7, i e5 sin-si beh hiat-kak8 ti7 goa7-bin7, jit8--si5 hou7 jit8 phak8, mi5--si5 hou7 sng tang3.  31). Goa2 beh in-ui7 i kap i e5 hou7-e3, kap i e5 jin5-sin5 e5 che7-koa3, heng5-hoat8 in; Goa2 beh7 hou7 Goa2 sou2 kong2 it-chhe3 e5 chai-e7 lim5-kau3 in, i2-kip8 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 peh-siN3, kap Iu5-tai7 lang5; chong2-si7 in m7 thiaN.  32). Tui3 an2-ni Ia5-li7-bi2 koh theh8 chit8-pun2, kau hou7 Ni5-li7-a e5 kiaN2 su-ki3 Pa-liok8; i chiu7 chiong Ia5-li7-bi2 sou2 thoan5 e5 oe7 sia2 ti7 hit lai7-bin7; chiu7-si7 Iu5-tai7 ong5 Iok-nga2-keng3 sou2 sio--khi3 hit-pun2 it-chhe3 e5 oe7; leng7-goa7 koh thiN choe7-choe7 saN-chhin-chhiuN7 e5 oe7.

[37]	Iok-se-a e5 kiaN2 Se-ti2-ka ong5 thoe3 Iok-nga2-keng3 e5 kiaN2 Ko-ni5-nga2 choe3 ong5; Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat bat siat-lip8 i choe3 ong5 ti7 Iu5-tai7 toe7.  2). Chong2-si7 i kap i e5 jin5-sin5, kap kok-lai7 e5 peh-siN3, long2 m7-thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7, chiu7-si7 i thok sian-ti Ia5-li7-bi2 sou2 kong2--e5.
	3). Se-ti2-ka ong5 chhe Si7-li7-bi2-nga2 e5 kiaN2 Iu5-kah, kap che3-si Ma2-se-nga2 e5 kiaN2 Se-hoan-nga2, khi3 kiN3 sian-ti Ia5-li7-bi2; kong2, Kiu5 li2 thoe3 goan2 ki5-to2 Ia5-ho5-hoa lan2 e5 Siong7-te3.  4). Hit-si5 Ia5-li7-bi2 chhut-jip8 ti7 peh-siN3 e5 tiong-kan; in-ui7 in iau2-be7 ka7 i koaiN-loh8 kaN.  5). Hoat-lo2 e5 kun-peng i2-keng tui3 Ai-kip8 chhut-lai5, hiah-e5 ui5-khun3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 thiaN-kiN3 in e5 hong-siaN, chiu7 thiat-iaN5 li7-khui Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2.  6). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 sian-ti Ia5-li7-bi2 kong2:  7). Ia5-ho5-hoa I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 an2-ni kong2, Iu5-tai7 ong5 chhe lin2 lai5 goa2 chia mng7 goa2, lin2 tioh8 an2-ni ka7 i kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Hoat-lo2 e5 kun-peng hiah e5 chhut-lai5 beh pang-chan7 lin2--e5, beh to3--khi3 Ai-kip8 pun2-kok.  8). Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 beh koh lai5, kong-kek chit e5 siaN5, beh chhu2--i, iah8 beh eng7 he2 sio--i.  9). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Lin2 m7-thang ka-ki7 phian3, kong2, Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 tek-khak beh li7-khui goan2, in-ui7 in bo5 beh li7-khui.  10). Lin2 chiu7 na7 phah-pai7 kong-kek lin2 e5 Ka-lek8-ti2 e5 choan5-kun, in tiong-kan chi2 chhun siu7-siong e5 lang5, in tak8-lang5 iah8 beh tui3 i e5 pou3-piN5-lai7 khi2-lai5, eng7 he2 sio chit e5 siaN5.
	11). Ka-lek8-ti2 e5 kun-peng, in-ui7 kiaN Hoat-lo2 e5 kun-peng, chiu7 thiat-iaN5 li7-khui Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2;  12). hit-si5 Ia5-li7-bi2 chhut Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, beh khi3 Pian7-nga2-bin2 e5 toe7; ai3 tit-tioh8 i e5 hun7-giah8 ti7 peh-siN3 e5 tiong-kan.  13). I kau3 Pian7-nga2-bin2 mng5 hia, u7 kou3-mng5 e5 koaN, mia5 kio3 I-li7-nga2, si7 Hap-na2-ni5-a e5 sun, Si7-li7-bi2-nga2 e5 kiaN2; i chiu7 liah8 sian-ti Ia5-li7-bi2, kong2, Li2 si7 teh tau5-hang5 Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 ouh.  14). Ia5-li7-bi2 kong2, Bo5-iaN2, goa2 m7-si7 tau5-hang5 Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5; I-li7-nga2 m7-thiaN i, chiu7 liah8 Ia5-li7-bi2, sang3 i kau3 kui3-chok8 hia.  15). Chiah e5 kui3-chok8 siu7-khi3 Ia5-li7-bi2, chiu7 phah i, koaiN i ti7 kaN--nih, ti7 su-ki3 Iok-na2-tan e5 chhu3, in-ui7 in eng7 hit-keng choe3 kaN-lo5.  16). Ia5-li7-bi2 i2-keng kau3 toe7-ham7 e5 hiat8-lai7, Ia5-li7-bi2 toa3 hia choe7-choe7 jit8.  17). Se-ti2-ka ong5 chhe lang5 toa3 i lai5, ong5 ti7 i e5 kiong-lai7 am3-chiN7 mng7 i kong2, U7 sim2-mih8 oe7 tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lai5 bo5? Ia5-li7-bi2 kong2, U7; koh kong2, Li2 beh kau ti7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 e5 chhiu2.  18). Ia5-li7-bi2 koh tui3 Se-ti2-ka ong5 kong2, Goa2 u7 sim2-mih8 tek-choe7 li2, a2-si7 tek-choe7 li2 e5 jin5-sin5 kap chit e5 peh-siN3, chiah hou7 li2 ka7 goa2 koaiN-kaN?  19). Li2 chiah e5 sian-ti tui3 lin2 chham3-gu2, kong2, Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 tek-khak bo5 lai5 kong-kek lin2 kap chit e5 sou2-chai7; taN in ti7 toh-loh8?  20). TaN goa2 e5 chu2 goa2 e5 ong5 ah, chhiaN2 li2 thiaN goa2, chun2 goa2 sou2 kiu5, m7-thang hou7 goa2 to3-tng2--khi3 su-ki3 Iok-na2-tan e5 chhu3, bian2-tit goa2 si2 ti7-hia.  21). Se-ti2-ka ong5 chiu7 beng7-leng7 koaiN Ia5-li7-bi2 ti7 khu-liu5-sou2 e5 iN7; tak8-jit8 tui3 choe3-piaN2 e5 koe theh8 chit8-liap8 mi7-pau hou7 i; tit8-kau3 siaN5-lai7 bo5 mi7-pau chiah soah; an2-ni Ia5-li7-bi2 iu5-goan5 toa3 ti7 khu-liu5-sou2 e5 iN7-lai7.

[38]	Ma2-than2 e5 kiaN2 Si7-hoat-the5-nga2, Pa-si-hou7-jiN2 e5 kiaN2 Ki-tai7-li7, Si7-li7-bi2-nga2 e5 kiaN2 Iu5-kah, Ma2-ki-nga2 e5 kiaN2 Pa-si-hou7-jiN2, thiaN-kiN3 Ia5-li7-bi2 tui3 cheng3-lang5 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, kong2,  2). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KiN3-na7 toa3 ti7 chit e5 siaN5-lai7--e5 beh tui3 to-kiam3, tui3 ki-hng, tui3 un-ek8 lai5 si2; tok8-tok8 chhut-khi3 kui Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5--e5 oe7 tit-tioh8 oah8, beh khioh-tioh8 i e5 siN3-mia7 lai5 oah8--teh.  3). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Chit e5 siaN5 koat-toan3 beh kau ti7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 kun-peng e5 chhiu2; i beh chhu2--i.  4). Tui3 an2-ni, kui3-chok8 ka7 ong5 kong2, Kiu5 li2 hou7 chit lang5 si2; in-ui7 i tui3 siaN5-lai7 chhun e5 peng-teng, kap cheng3 peh-siN3, kong2 chit-ho7 e5 oe7, hou7 in e5 chhiu2 nng2; chit e5 lang5 m7-si7 kiu5 hou7 peh-siN3 peng5-an, si7 hou7 in tu2-tioh8 chai-e7.  5). Se-ti2-ka ong5 kong2, KhoaN3 ah, i ti7 lin2 e5 chhiu2-thau5, ong5 boe7-oe7 kan-siap8 lin2 sim2-mih8 tai7-chi3.  6). In chiu7 liah8 Ia5-li7-bi2, hiat i ti7 Hap-bi2-lek8 e5 kiaN2 Ma2-ki-nga2 e5 chiN2; hit e5 chiN2 ti7 khu-liu5-sou2 e5 iN7-lai7; in eng7 soh chiong Ia5-li7-bi2 tui7--loh8-khi3; chiN2-lai7 bo5 chui2, chi2-u7 thou5-be5; Ia5-li7-bi2 chiu7 ham7 ti7 thou5-be5.  7). Ti7 ong5-kiong-lai7 e5 thai3-kam3, Kou2-sit8 lang5 I2-pek-bi2-lek8, thiaN-kiN3 in chiong Ia5-li7-bi2 tui7-loh8 chiN2; hit-si5 ong5 che7 ti7 Pian7-nga2-bin2 mng5-khau2.  8). I2-pek-bi2-lek8 chiu7 chhut ong5-kiong, tui3 ong5 kong2,  9). Goa2 e5 chu2, goa2 e5 ong5 ah, chiah e5 lang5 khoan2-thai7 sian-ti Ia5-li7-bi2--e5, long2 si7 phaiN2; u7 ka7 i hiat-loh8 chiN2, i oe7 go7-si2 ti7-hia; in-ui7 siaN5-lai7 bo5 bi2-niu5.  10). Ong5 chiu7 hoan-hu3 Kou2-sit8 lang5 I2-pek-bi2-lek8 kong2, Li2 tui3 chia toa3 saN-chap8 lang5, than3 sian-ti Ia5-li7-bi2 iau2-be7 si2, kiu3 i chhut chiN2.  11). Tui3 an2-ni, I2-pek-bi2-lek8 chhoa7 chiah e5 lang5 saN-kap khi3, jip8 ong5-kiong, kau3 khou3-pang5 e7, tui3-hia theh8 phoa3-pou3 ku7-saN, eng7 soh tui7-loh8 chiN2, kau3 Ia5-li7-bi2 hia.  12). Kou2-sit8 lang5 I2-pek-bi2-lek8 ka7 Ia5-li7-bi2 kong2, Li2 eng7 chiah e5 phoa3-pou3 kap ku7-saN, chu7 ti7 koh-e7-khang.  he7 ti7 soh-teng2; Ia5-li7-bi2 chiu7 chiau3 an2-ni kiaN5.  13). An2-ni, in chiu7 eng7 soh puih8 Ia5-li7-bi2 chhut chiN2; Ia5-li7-bi2 iu5-goan5 toa3 ti7 khu-liu5-sou2 e5 iN7.
	14). Se-ti2-ka ong5 chhe lang5 toa3 sian-ti Ia5-li7-bi2 jip8 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3 te7 saN e5 mng5, kau3 i hia; ong5 chiu7 tui3 Ia5-li7-bi2 kong2, Goa2 mng7 li2 chit8-hang7-su7, li2 long2 m7-thang un2-bat8 ti7 goa2.  15). Ia5-li7-bi2 in3 Se-ti2-ka kong2, Goa2 na7 ka7 li2 kong2, li2 kiam2 bo5 beh thai5-si2 goa2 mah? goa2 na7 chi2-tiam2 li2, li2 bo5 beh thiaN.  16). Se-ti2-ka ong5 am3-chiN7 tui3 Ia5-li7-bi2 chiu3-choa7 kong2, Hit-e5 chhong3-cho7 lan2 e5 oah8-mia7 e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 oah8--e5, goa2 chi2 I lai5 chiu3-choa7, goa2 tek-khak bo5 thai5 li2, iah8 m7 chiong li2 kau hou7 chiah-e5 siau3-siuN7 li2 e5 siN3-mia7 e5 lang5 e5 chhiu2.  17). Ia5-li7-bi2 tui3 Se-ti2-ka kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa ban7-kun e5 Siong7-te3, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3, an2-ni kong2, Li2 na7 chhut-khi3 tau5-hang5 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 e5 kui3-chok8, li2 e5 siN3-mia7 chiu7 oe7 oah8-teh, chit e5 siaN5 put-ti3 hou7 he2 sio; li2 kap li2 e5 choan5-ke long2 oe7 oah8.  18). Li2 na7 m7 chhut--khi3 tau5-hang5 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 e5 kui3-chok8, chiu7 chit e5 siaN5 beh kau ti7 Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 e5 chhiu2; in beh eng7 he2 sio--i; li2 iah8 boe7 thoat-li7 in e5 chhiu2.  19). Se-ti2-ka ong5 tui3 Ia5-li7-bi2 kong2, Goa2 kiaN hiah-e5 tau5-hang5 Ka-lek8-ti2 e5 Iu5-tai7 lang5, kiaN-kiN3 Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 chiong goa2 kau ti7 in e5 chhiu2, in oe7 leng5-jiok8 goa2.  20). Ia5-li7-bi2 kong2, Boe7--lah.  Kiu5 li2 thiaN goa2 tui3 li2 sou2 kong2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7, an2-ni li2 chiu7 tit-tioh8 li7-ek, li2 e5 siN3-mia7 ia7 oe7 oah8--teh.  21). Li2 na7 m7-kheng2 chhut--khi3, Ia5-ho5-hoa chi2-si7 goa2 e5 oe7 chiu7-si7 che:  22). KhoaN3 ah, Iu5-tai7 ong5-kiong sou2 chhun e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 beh toa3 kau3 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 e5 kui3-chok8 hia, chiah e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 beh kong2, Li2 ti-ki2 e5 peng5-iu2 sai2-so7 li2, khah-iaN5 li2; li2 e5 kha lok--loh8 thou5-be5, in chiu7 oat8-tng2-sin the3--khi3.  23). Lang5 beh chiong li2 chiah e5 bou2 kap li2 chiah e5 kiaN2, toa3 kau3 Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 hia, li2 iah8 boe7-oe7 thoat-li7 in e5 chhiu2; beh hou7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 e5 chhiu2 liah8-tioh8; li2 ia7 beh lian5-lui7 chit e5 siaN5 siu7 he2 sio.  24). Se-ti2-ka tui3 Ia5-li7-bi2 kong2, Boh8-tit hou7 lang5 chai chiah e5 oe7, li2 chiu7 boe7 si2.  25). Kui3-chok8 na7 thiaN-kiN3 goa2 u7 kap li2 kong2-oe7, in chiu7 lai5 chhe7 li2, mng7 li2 kong2, Li2 ka7 ong5 kong2 sim2-mih8, m7-thang tui3 goan2 un2-bat8, goan2 chiu7 bo5 hou7 li2 si2; ong5 tui3 li2 kong2 sim2-mih8, iah8 long2 tioh8 ka7 goan2 kong2;  26). li2 chiu7 tioh8 ka7 in kong2, Goa2 ti7 ong5 e5 bin7-cheng5 khun2-kiu5 i boh8-tit hou7 goa2 koh jip8 Iok-na2-tan e5 chhu3, lai5 si2 ti7-hia.  27). Au7-lai5 cheng3 kui3-chok8 lai5 chhe7 Ia5-li7-bi2, mng7 i; i chiu7 chiau3 ong5 sou2 hoan-hu3 it-chhe3 e5 oe7 lai5 in3 in.  In chiu7 soah, bo5 koh kap i kong2-oe7; in-ui7 su7-cheng5 bo5 lou7-chhut.  28). Tui3 an2-ni, Ia5-li7-bi2 iu5-goan5 toa3 ti7 khu-liu5-sou2 e5 iN7-lai7; tit8-kau3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 siu7-chhu2 e5 jit8.

[39]	Iu5-tai7 ong5 Se-ti2-ka kau2-ni5 chap8-geh8, Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5, Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat, chhoa7 i long2-chong2 e5 kun-peng lai5 ui5-khun3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2.  2). Se-ti2-ka chap8-it--ni5, si3 geh8, chhoe kau2-jit8, siaN5 chiu7 phoa3.  3). Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 siu7 chhu2 e5 si5, Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 e5 kui3-chok8 Ni5-kah-sa-li7-siat, Sam-kah-ni5-pho, thai3-kam3-thau5 Sat-se-kim, phok-su7-tiuN2 Ni5-kah-sat-li7-siat, kap Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 ki5-u5 it-chhe3 e5 kui3-chok8, long2 lai5 che7 ti7 tiong-mng5.  4). Iu5-tai7 ong5 Se-ti2-ka kap it-chhe3 e5 chian3-su7, khoaN3-kiN3 in, chiu7 chau2; thau3-mi5 tui3 ong5 e5 hng5 e5 lou7, nng7 e5 siaN5-chhiuN5 tiong-kan e5 mng5, chhut-siaN5, ng3 PiN5-iuN5 chau2-khi3.  5). Ka-lek8-ti2 e5 kun-peng tui-jip in, ti7 Ia5-li7-ko e5 piN5-iuN5 jip--tioh8 Se-ti2-ka; liah8--i, chiu7 toa3 kau3 Hap-ma2 toe7 e5 Li7-pi2-lah8, Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat hia; i chiu7 sim2-phoaN3--i.  6). Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 ti7 Li7-pi2-lah8 thai5 Se-ti2-ka chiah e5 kiaN2, hou7 i chhin-bak8 khoaN3-kiN3; Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 koh thai5 Iu5-tai7 it-chhe3 chun-kui3 e5 lang5.  7). Iah8 koh iah Se-ti2-ka e5 bak8-chiu, eng7 thih-lian7 lian7--i, beh toa3 i kau3 Pa-pi2-lun5.  8). Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 eng7 he2 sio ong5-kiong kap peh-siN3 e5 chhu3; koh thiah-hui2 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 siaN5-chhiuN5.  9). Hit-si5 Si7-oe7-tiuN2 Ni5-pou3-sat-lah8-tan3 chiong siaN5-lai7 sou2 chhun e5 peh-siN3, kap tau5-hang5 kui-hok8 i--e5, i2-kip8 ki5-u5 sou2 chhun e5 peh-siN3, long2 liah8-khi3 Pa-pi2-lun5.  10). Si7-oe7-tiuN2 Ni5-pou3-sat-lah8-tan3 chiu7 chiong peh-siN3-tiong song3 kau3 bo5 poaN3-hang7 e5 lang5 lau5 ti7 Iu5-tai7 toe7; tng-si5 iah8 hou7 in phu5-to5-hng5 kap chhan5.  11). Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat lun7-kau3 Ia5-li7-bi2, chiu7 hoan-hu3 Si7-oe7-tiuN2 Ni5-pou3-sat-lah8-tan3, kong2,  12). Chiong i kau-tai3 li2, tioh8 ho2 khoan2-thai7 i, m7-thang hai7 i; i tui3 li2 kong2 sim2-mih8, li2 chiu7 chiau3 an2-ni ka7 i choe3.  13). Si7-oe7-tiuN2 Ni5-pou3-sat-lah8-tan3, thai3-kam3-thau5 Ni5-pou3-sa-su-pan, phok-su7-tiuN2 Ni5-pou3-sa-li2-siat, kap Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 chiah e5 koaN-tiuN2,  14). chhe lang5 chhoa7 Ia5-li7-bi2 chhut khu-liu5-sou2 e5 iN7, kau-tai3 Sa-hoan e5 sun, A-hi-kam e5 kiaN2, Ki-tai7-li7, chhoa7 i to3-khi3 in tau; tui3 an2-ni i chiu7 khia7-khi2 peh-siN3 e5 tiong-kan.
	15). Ia5-li7-bi2 iau2 koaiN ti7 khu-liu5-sou2 iN7-lai7 e5 si5, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 i kong2,  16). Li2 tioh8 khi3 ka7 Kou2-sit8 lang5 I2-pek-bi2-lek8 kong2, Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3, an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 kong2 kang3 chai-e7, bo5 kang3 hok-khi3 e5 oe7, tek-khak kau3 chit e5 siaN5; kau3 hit-jit8 beh chiaN5 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5.  17). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Kau3 hit-jit8 Goa2 beh chin2-kiu3 li2; li2 tek-khak put-ti3 kau-hu3 ti7 li2 sou2 kiaN hiah-e5 lang5 e5 chhiu2.  18). Goa2 tiaN7-tioh8 beh chin2-kiu3 li2, li2 put-ti3 to2 ti7 to-e7; li2 beh khioh-tioh8 li2 e5 siN3-mia7; in-ui7 li2 oa2-kho3 Goa2; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.

[40]	Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 lang5, kap Iu5-tai7 lang5, siu7-liah8 khi3 Pa-pi2-lun5; ki5-tiong Ia5-li7-bi2 iah8 hou7 Si7-oe7-tiuN2 liah8--khi3, eng7 thih-lian7 pak8--i; au7-lai5 tui3 Lah8-ma2 pang3 i khi3; jian5-au7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 Ia5-li7-bi2.  2). Si7-oe7-tiuN2 kio3 Ia5-li7-bi2 lai5, ka7 i kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 bat kong2, beh kang3 chit e5 chai-e7 hou7 chit e5 sou2-chai7.  3). TaN Ia5-ho5-hoa hou7 i kau3, chiau3 I sou2 kong2--e5 lai5 kiaN5.  In-ui7 lin2 tek-choe7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, bo5 thiaN-than3 I e5 oe7, sou2-i2 chit e5 tai7-chi3 kau3 ti7 lin2.  4). KhoaN3 ah, goa2 kin-a2-jit8 thau2-khui li2 chhiu2--nih e5 thih-lian7; li2 na7 khoaN3 kap goa2 khi3 Pa-pi2-lun5 si7 ho2, chiu7 thang lai5 khi3, goa2 beh ho2 khoan2-thai7 li2; li2 na7 khoaN3 kap goa2 khi3 Pa-pi2-lun5 m7-ho2, chiu7 boh8-eng7 khi3.  KhoaN3 ah, choan5-toe7 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5, li2 khoaN3 toh-loh8 si7 ho2, si7 hap8-gi5, choe3 li2 thang khi3.  5). I iau2-be7 to3-khi3, Si7-oe7-tiuN2 koh ka7 i kong2, Li2 thang to3--khi3 Sa-hoan e5 sun, A-hi-kam e5 kiaN2, Ki-tai7-li7 hia; hian7-kim Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 siat-lip8 i koan2-hat Iu5-tai7 chiah e5 siaN5; li2 thang kap i khia7-khi2 ti7 peh-siN3-tiong, a2-si7 li2 sou2 khoaN3-choe3 hap8-gi5 e5 sou2-chai7, chiu7 thang khi3.  Tui3 an2-ni, Si7-oe7-tiuN2 sang3 i bi2-niu5 kap le2-mih8, hou7 i khi3.  6). Ia5-li7-bi2 chiu7 kau3 Bi2-su-pa, kiN3 A-hi-kam e5 kiaN2 Ki-tai7-li7; kap i khia7-khi2 ti7 keng2-lai7 chhun e5 peh-siN3 e5 tiong-kan.
	7). Ti7 chhan5-ia2 it-chhe3 e5 kun-tiuN2, kap siok8 in e5 lang5, thiaN-kiN3 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 siat-lip8 A-hi-kam e5 kiaN2 Ki-tai7-li7 koan2-hat chit sou2-chai7; iah8 chiong bo5 liah8-khi3 Pa-pi2-lun5 e5 ta-pou-lang5, hu7-jin5-lang5, gin2-a2, kap keng2-lai7 kek8 song3-hiong e5 lang5, long2-chong2 kau i;  8). in chiu7 lai5 Bi2-su-pa Ki-tai7-li7 hia; chiu7-si7 Ni5-tham3-nga2 e5 kiaN2 I2-sit8-ma2-li7, Ka-li7-a nng7 e5 kiaN2 Iok-hap-lan5 kap Iok-na2-tan, Tan-hou7-biat8 e5 kiaN2 Se-lai5-nga2, kap Ni5-to5-hoat lang5 I2-hui2 e5 cheng3-kiaN2, Ma2-ka lang5 e5 kiaN2 Ia5-sat-ni5-a, kap siok8 in e5 lang5.  9). Sa-hoan e5 sun, A-hi-kam e5 kiaN2, Ki-tai7-li7 tui3 in kap siok8 in e5 lang5 chiu3-choa7, kong2, Boh8-tit kiaN hok8-sai7 Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5; choe3 lin2 khia7-khi2 chia, hok8-sai7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5, lin2 chiu7 oe7 tit-tioh8 hok-khi3.  10). Lun7-kau3 goa2, goa2 beh tiam3 ti7 Bi2-su-pa, su-hau7 hiah e5 oe7 lai5 lan2 chia e5 Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5; na7-si7 lin2 chiah-e5, lin2 tioh8 chek-chu7 chiu2, he7-thiN e5 ke2-chi2, kap iu5, siu ti7 khi3-ku7 lai7, khia7-khi2 ti7 lin2 sou2 chiam3 e5 siaN5.  11). Koh u7 ti7 Mou5-ap, kap A-bun5 chok8 e5 tiong-kan, ti7 I2-tong, kap liat8-kok tiong-kan it-chhe3 e5 Iu5-tai7 lang5, thiaN-kiN3 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 u7 lau5 sou2 chhun e5 Iu5-tai7 lang5, koh siat-lip8 Sa-hoan e5 sun, A-hi-kam e5 kiaN2, Ki-tai7-li7 koan2-hat in;  12). chiah e5 it-chhe3 e5 Iu5-tai7 lang5 tui3 in hou7 lang5 koaN2-khi3 e5 tak8 sou2-chai7 to3--lai5, kau3 Iu5-tai7 toe7 e5 Bi2-su-pa, Ki-tai7-li7 hia, soa3 chek-chu7 choe7-choe7 chiu2 kap he7-thiN e5 ke2-chi2.
	13). Ka-li7-a e5 kiaN2, Iok-hap-lan5, kap ti7 chhan5-ia2 it-chhe3 e5 kun-tiuN2 lai5 Bi2-su-pa kiN3 Ki-tai7-li7, tui3 i kong2,  14). A-bun5-chok8 e5 ong5, Pa-li7-su, u7 chhe Ni5-tham3-nga2 e5 kiaN2 I2-sit8-ma2-li7 lai5 beh chhu2 li2 e5 siN3-mia7, li2 chai mah? chong2-si7 A-hi-kam e5 kiaN2 Ki-tai7-li7 m7-sin3 in.  15). Ka-li7-a e5 kiaN2, Iok-hap-lan5 ti7 Bi2-su-pa am3-chiN7 tui3 Ki-tai7-li2 kong2, Kiu5 li2 chun2 goa2 khi3, goa2 beh thai5 Ni5-tham3-nga2 e5 kiaN2 I2-sit8-ma2-li7, tek-khak bo5 lang5 chai; kiam2 thang hou7 i chhu2 li2 e5 siN3-mia7, ti3-kau3 kui-oa2 li2 e5 Iu5-tai7 lang5 si3-soaN3, hou7 Iu5-tai7 sou2-chhun e5 lang5 long2 biat8-bo5 ah?  16). A-hi-kam e5 kiaN2 Ki-tai7-li7 ka7 Ka-li2-a e5 kiaN2 Iok-hap-lan5 kong2, Li2 m7-thang choe3 chit e5 su7; li2 sou2 kong2 I2-sit8-ma2-li7 e5 su7 si7 bo5-iaN2.

[41]	Chhit-geh8-kan, I2-li7-sa-ma2 e5 sun, Ni5-tham3-nga2 e5 kiaN2, I2-sit8-ma2-li7, i si7 ong5-chhin, iah8 si7 ong5 e5 tai7-sin5, chhoa7 chap8-lang5 lai5 Bi2-su-pa, kiN3 A-hi-kam e5 kiaN2 Ki-tai7-li7; in ti7 Bi2-su-pa saN-kap chiah8.  2). Ni5-tham3-nga2 e5 kiaN2 I2-sit8-ma2-li7, i2-kip8 kap i lai5 e5 hit chap8-lang5, khi2-lai5, eng7 to thai5-si2 Sa-hoan e5 sun, A-hi-kam e5 kiaN2, Ki-tai7-li7, chiu7-si7 Pa-pi2-lun5 sou2 lip8 lai5 koan2-hat chit e5 toe7--e5.  3). I2-sit8-ma2-li7 koh thai5-si2 ti7 Bi2-su-pa kui-oa2 Ki-tai7-li7 long2-chong2 e5 Iu5-tai7 lang5; i2-kip8 ti7-hia sou2 tu2-tioh8 Ka-lek8-ti2 e5 kun-peng.  4). I thai5-si2 Ki-tai7-li7 liau2-au7, te7-ji7-jit8 iau2 bo5 lang5 chai;  5). hit-tiap8 u7 poeh-chap8 lang5 tui3 Si7-kiam3, tui3 Si7-lo5, tui3 Sat-ma2-li7-a lai5; thi3 chhui3-chhiu, thiah-lih8 saN, ka-ki7 koah sin-khu, chhiu2 theh8 le2-mih8 kap ju2-hiuN, beh toa3 i kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3.  6). Ni5-tham3-nga2 e5 kiaN2, I2-sit8-ma2-li7, tui3 Bi2-su-pa chhut-lai5 ngia5-chih in; na2-kiaN5 na2-khau3; kau3 tu2-tioh8 in, chiu7 ka7 in kong2, Lin2 lai5 khi3 kiN3 A-hi-kam e5 kiaN2 Ki-tai7-li7.  7). In kau3 siaN5-tiong, Ni5-tham3-nga2 e5 kiaN2 I2-sit8-ma2-li7, kap te3 i e5 lang5, chiu7 thai5-is2 in, hiat in ti7 ta-chiN2.  8). In tiong-kan u7 chap8-lang5 tui3 I2-sit8-ma2-li7 kong2, Boh8-tit thai5-si2 goan2; in-ui7 goan2 u7 choe7-choe7 sio2-beh8, toa7-beh8, iu5, bit8, khng3 ti7 chhan5--nih; i chiu7 theng5-chhiu2, bo5 thai5 in ti7 in e5 hiaN-ti7-tiong.  9). I2-sit8-ma2-li7 thai5 chiah e5 lang5, oa2-kun7 Ki-tai7-li7 hia, chiong in e5 sin-si hiat ti7 chiN2--nih; chit e5 chiN2 si7 chiong5-cheng5 A-sat ong5 in-ui7 kiaN I2-sek-liat8 ong5 Pa-sa e5 ian5-kou3 sou2 khui--e5; Ni5-tham3-nga2 e5 kiaN2 I2-sit8-ma2-li7 chiong sou2 thai5 e5 sin-si thun7-moa2--i.  10). I2-sit8-ma2-li7 liah8 Bi2-su-pa sou2 chhun e5 peh-siN3, chiu7-si7 ong5 e5 cheng3 cha-bou2-kiaN2, i2-kip8 iau2 toa3 ti7 Bi2-su-pa e5 peh-siN3, chiu7-si7 si7-oe7-tiuN2 Ni5-pou3-sat-lah8-tan3 sou2 kau-tai3 A-hi-kam e5 kiaN2 Ki-tai7-li7--e5.  Ni5-tham3-nga2 e5 kiaN2 I2-sit8-ma2-li7 liah8 i khi3, beh ke3--khi3 A-bun5 chok8 hia.
	11). Ka-li7-a e5 kiaN2 Iok-hap-lan5, i2-kip8 kap i ti7-teh e5 cheng3 kun-tiuN2, thiaN-kiN3 Ni5-tham3-nga2 e5 kiaN2 I2-sit8-ma2-li7 sou2 kiaN5 it-chhe3 e5 phaiN2,  12). chiu7 chhoa7 cheng3-lang5 chin3-cheng5 khi3, beh kap Ni5-tham3-nga2 e5 kiaN2 I2-sit8-ma2-li7 kau-chian3; ti7 Ki-pian3 e5 toa7-chui2-piN chhe7--tioh8-e5.  13). I2-sit8-ma2-li7 sou2 toa3--khi3 hiah e5 peh-siN3 khoaN3-khi3 Ka-li7-a e5 kiaN2 Iok-hap-lan5, i2-kip8 kap i lai5 e5 cheng3 kun-tiuN2, chiu7 long2 hoaN-hi2.  14). Tui3 an2-ni I2-sit8-ma2-li7 tui3 Bi2-su-pa sou2 liat8-khi3 e5 cheng3-peh-siN3 long2 oat8-tng2 lai5 kui Ka-li7-a e5 kiaN2 Iok-hap-lan5.  15). Ni5-tham3-nga2 e5 kiaN2 I2-sit8-ma2-li7, kap poeh e5 lang5 thoat-li7 Iok-hap-lan5 e5 chhiu2, chau2-khi3 A-bun5 chok8 hia.  16). Au7-lai5 Ka-li7-a e5 kiaN2 Iok-hap-lan5, kap te3--i e5 cheng3 kun-tiuN2, chiong sou2 chhun e5 peh-siN3, chiu7-si7 Ni5-tham3-nga2 e5 kiaN2 I2-sit8-ma2-li7 phah-si2 A-hi-kam e5 kiaN2 Ki-tai7-li7 i2-au7, tui3 Bi2-su-pa sou2 toa3--khi3 e5 ta-pou-lang5, iong2-su7, hu7-lu2, gin2-a2, thai3-kam3, koh si7 i tui3 Ki-pian3 toa3--lai5-e5.  17). In chiu7 khi2-sin kau3 Pek-li7-heng5 piN-a2 Kim-han2 e5 kheh-tiam3 theng5-hioh, siuN7 beh khi3 Ai-kip8.  18). Che si7 in-ui7 Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 e5 ian5-kou3; in-ui7 Ni5-tham3-nga2 e5 kiaN2 I2-sit8-ma2-li7 u7 thai5-si2 A-hi-kam e5 kiaN2 Ki-tai7-li7, chiu7-si7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 sou2 lip8 lai5 koan2-hat chit e5 thou2-toe7--e5, sou2-i2 in kiaN.

[42]	Cheng3 kun-tiuN2 kap Ka-li7-a e5 kiaN2 Iok-hap-lan5, kap Ho5-sa-nga2 e5 kiaN2 Ia5-sat-ni5-a, i2-kip8 cheng3 peh-siN3, tui3 soe3 kau3 toa7, long2 chin3-cheng5 lai5.  2). Tui3 sian-ti Ia5-li7-bi2 kong2, Kiu5 li2 chun2 goan2 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 sou2 kiu5, thoe3 goan2 chiah e5 chhun e5 lang5 ki5-to2 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3; goan2 pun2-jian5 chin-choe7, taN sou2-chhun-e5 chin-chio2, che si7 li2 chhin-bak8 khoaN3-kiN3--e5.  3). Goan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 chi2-si7 goan2 sou2 tioh8 kiaN5 e5 lou7, sou2 tioh8 choe3 e5 su7.  4). Sian-ti Ia5-li7-bi2 ka7 in kong2, Goa2 i2-keng thiaN-kiN3; ho2, goa2 beh chiau3 lin2 e5 oe7, ki5-to2 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3; bo5-lun7 Ia5-ho5-hoa in3 lin2 sim2-mih8, goa2 tek-khak long2 beh ka7 lin2 kong2, bo5 tui3 lin2 khng3-bat8 chit8-ku3.  5). Tui3 an2-ni in ka7 Ia5-li7-bi2 kong2, Goan2 na7 bo5 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 chhe li2 lai5 kong2 it-chhe3 e5 oe7 khi3 kiaN5, chiu7 goan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 li2 goan2 e5 tiong-kan choe3 chin-sit8 tiong-sin3 e5 kan-cheng3.  6). Goan2 chit-si5 chhiaN2 li2 kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa goan2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5; I sou2 kong2--e5, bo5 lun7 si7 ho2 si7 phaiN2, goan2 long2 beh thiaN-than3 I e5 oe7; goan2 thiaN-than3 Ia5-ho5-hoa goan2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 oe7, chiu7 thang tit-tioh8 heng-thong.
	7). Ke3 chap8-jit8, u7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 Ia5-li7-bi2.  8). I chiu7 chiong Ka-li7-a e5 kiaN2 Iok-hap-lan5, i2-kip8 kap i saN-kap ti7-teh e5 cheng3 kun-tiuN2, kap cheng3 peh-siN3, tui3 soe3 kau3 toa7, long2 kio3 in lai5;  9). tui3 in kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3, chiu7-si7 lin2 chhe goa2 kau3 I e5 bin7-cheng5 lai5 hian3 lin2 sou2 kiu5--e5,  10). I an2-ni kong2, Lin2 na7 iu5-goan5 beh tiam3 ti7 chit sou2-chai7, Goa2 chiu7 beh kian3-cho7 lin2, bo5 hui2-hoai7 lin2; beh chai-poe5 lin2, bo5 puih8-chhut lin2; in-ui7 Goa2 u7 the3-hoe2 Goa2 sou2 kang3 hou7 lin2 e5 chai-e7.  11). Boh8-tit kiaN lin2 sou2 kiaN e5 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5; Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Boh8-tit kiaN--i; in-ui7 Goa2 kap lin2 ti7-teh, beh chin2-kiu3 lin2, hou7 lin2 thoat-li7 i e5 chhiu2.  12). Goa2 beh lin5-bin2 lin2, hou7 in iah8 lin5-bin2 lin2; hou7 lin2 to3-lai5 pun2 sou2-chai7.  13). Siat-su2 lin2 kong2, Goan2 m7 tiam3 chit sou2-chai7, an2-ni chiu7-si7 lin2 m7 thiaN-than3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 oe7.  14). Na7 kong2, M7--ah, goan2 beh jip8--khi3 Ai-kip8 toe7; ti7-hia bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 kau-chian3, bo5 thiaN-kiN3 sau3-kak e5 siaN, iah8 put-ti3 bo5 thang chiah8 lai5 iau-go7; goan2 beh toa3 hia khia7-khi3.  15). TaN lin2 Iu5-tai7 sou2 chhun e5 peh-siN3 ah, tioh8 thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7; ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 an2-ni kong2, Lin2 na7 keng3-jian5 ngi7-phiN7 beh khi3 Ai-kip8, toa3 hia kia3-kha,  16). chiu7 lin2 sou2 kiaN e5 to-kiam3 beh ti7-hia jip-tioh8 lin2 ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7; koh lin2 sou2 kiaN e5 ki-hng, beh ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7 ka7 lin2 te3-tiau5-tiau5; lin2 beh si2 ti7-hia.  17). KiN3-na7 ngi7-phiN7 beh khi3 Ai-kip8, kia3-kha ti7-hia e5 lang5, long2 beh an2-ni; in beh tui3 to-kiam3, tui3 ki-hng, tui3 un-ek8 lai5 si2; ki5-tiong bo5 chit8-e5 lau5--teh, iah8 bo5 chit8-e5 thoat-li7 Goa2 sou2 kang3 hou7 in e5 chai-e7.  18). In-ui7 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3, an2-ni kong2, Goa2 u7 chaiN2-iuN7 chiong Goa2 e5 siu7-khi3 kap toa7 siu7-khi3 piaN3 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3; lin2 khi3 Ai-kip8 e5 si5, Goa2 iah8 beh chiau3 an2-ni chiong Goa2 e5 toa7 siu7-khi3 piaN3 ti7 lin2 e5 sin-chiuN7; hou7 lin2 chiaN5-choe3 thang chiu3-chou2, thang gong5-ngiah8, thang loe2-me7, thang leng5-jiok8; lin2 iah8 bo5 koh khoaN3-kiN3 chit e5 sou2-chai7.  19). Lin2 Iu5-tai7 sou2 chhun e5 peh-siN3 ah, Ia5-ho5-hoa lun7-kau3 lin2 u7 kong2, Boh8-tit khi3 Ai-kip8; lin2 tioh8 khak-sit8 chai, goa2 kin-a2-jit8 u7 cheng3-beng5 khoan3-kai3 lin2 lah.  20). Lin2 kiaN5 chha-biu7 lian5-lui7 ka-ki7; in-ui7 lin2 chhe goa2 kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3 hia, kong2, Kiu5 li2 thoe3 goan2 ki5-to2 Ia5-ho5-hoa, lan2 e5 Siong7-te3; chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 it-chhe3 sou2 kong2--e5, ka7 goan2 kong2; goan2 beh kiaN5--i.  21). Goa2 kin-a2-jit8 u7 ka7 lin2 kong2 lah; na7-si7 lin2 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 siaN, kap I chhe goa2 it-chhe3 chi2-si7 lin2--e5, lin2 long2 bo5 chun-than3.  22). TaN lin2 tioh8 khak-sit8 chai, lin2 ti7 sou2 beh khi3 kia3-kha e5 toe7, beh tui3 to-kiam3, tui3 ki-hng, tui3 un-ek8 lai5 si2.

[43]	Ia5-li7-bi2 tui3 cheng3 peh-siN3 kong2 beng5-pek8 Ia5-ho5-hoa in e5 Siong7-te3 it-chhe3 e5 oe7, chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa in e5 Siong7-te3 chhe--i sou2 kong2 it-chhe3 e5 oe7.  2). Ho5-sa-nga2 e5 kiaN2 A-sat-li7-nga2, kap Ka-li7-a e5 kiaN2 Iok-hap-lan5, kap it-chhe3 kiau-ngou7 e5 lang5, chiu7 tui3 Ia5-li7-bi2 kong2, Li2 kong2 bo5-iaN2 oe7, Ia5-ho5-hoa lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 peng7-bo5 chhe li2 lai5 kong2, Lin2 m7-thang khi3 Ai-kip8, lai5 kia3-kha ti7-hia;  3). che si7 Ni5-li7-a e5 kiaN2 Pa-liok8 kiau-so li2 hai7 goan2, beh chiong goan2 kau ti7 Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 e5 chhiu2, hou7 in thai5-si2 goan2, a2-si7 liah8 goan2 kau3 Pa-pi2-lun5.  4). Tui3 an2-ni, Ka-li7-a e5 kiaN2 Iok-hap-lan5, kap it-chhe3 kun-tiuN2, kap cheng3 peh-siN3, m7 thiaN-than3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7, lai5 tiam3 ti7 Iu5-tai7 toe7.  5). Ka-li7-a e5 kiaN2 Iok-hap-lan5, kap it-chhe3 e5 kun-tiuN2, chiu7 chiong chhun e5 Iu5-tai7 lang5, chiu7-si7 tui3 in siu7 koaN2--khi3 hiah e5 kok to3-lai5, beh kia3-kha ti7 Iu5-tai7 toe7--e5,  6). put-lun7 ta-pou-lang5, hu7-jin5-lang5, gin2-a2 kap ong5 hiah e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, kap si7-oe7-tiuN2 Ni5-pou3-sat-lah8-tan3 sou2 lau5 lai5 kau-tai3 Sa-hoan e5 sun, A-hi-kam e5 kiaN2, Ki-tai7-li7 e5 cheng3-lang5, kap sian-ti Ia5-li7-bi2, i2-kip8 Ni5-li7-a e5 kiaN2 Pa-liok8, long2 toa3 khi3 Ai-kip8 toe7, kau3 Tap-pi2-lek8.  7). Che si7 in-ui7 in m7 thiaN-than3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7.
	8). Ti7 Tap-pi2-lek8, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 Ia5-li7-bi2 kong2,  9). Li2 tioh8 eng7 chhiu2 theh8 kui2-te3 toa7 liap8 chioh8, ti7 Iu5-tai7 lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5, khng3 ti7 thiap8-chng e5 he-thou5-lai7, chiu7-si7 ti7 Tap-pi2-lek8 Hoat-lo2 e5 ong5-kiong-mng5 hia;  10). ka7 in kong2, Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh tiau3 Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat lai5; ti7 sou2 khng3 e5 chioh8-thau5-teng2, Goa2 beh an-ti3 i e5 po2-cho7, i beh ti7 hi2 chioh8-teng2 tah sui2 e5 pou3-piN5.  11). I beh lai5 kong-kek Ai-kip8 toe7, eng-kai si2-e5 chiu7 si2, eng-kai liah8-e5 chiu7 siu7-liah8, eng-kai hou7 to thai5-e5 chiu7 hou7 to thai5.  12). Goa2 ia7 beh khi2 he2 ti7 Ai-kip8 hiah e5 sin5-beng5 e5 bio7; i beh sio i, liah8 in khi3; i beh tit-tioh8 Ai-kip8 toe7 chhin-chhiuN7 bok8-chia2 chheng7 i e5 saN; tui3 hia an-jian5 chhut-khi3.  13). I tek-khak phah-chhui3 Ai-kip8 toe7 Pek-si7-bek8 tiau-khek e5 thiau7, eng7 he2 sio Ai-kip8 chiah e5 sin5-beng5 e5 bio7.

[44]	U7 oe7 lim5-kau3 Ia5-li7-bi2, lun7-kau3 it-chhe3 khia7-khi2 ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7 e5 Iu5-tai7 lang5; chiu7-si7 khia7-khi2 ti7 Bit8-toat8, Tap-pi2-lek8, Lo5-hut, Pa-thek-lo5 keng2-lai7 e5 Iu5-tai7 lang5, kong2,  2). Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 an2-ni kong2:  Goa2 sou2 kang3-loh8 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, kap Iu5-tai7 chiah e5 siaN5 it-chhe3 e5 chai-e7, lin2 long2 khoaN3-kiN3; khoaN3 ah, taN in long2 pha-hng, bo5 lang5 khia7-khi2.  3). Che si7 in-ui7 in sou2 kiaN5 e5 phaiN2, in khi3 sio-hiuN hok8-sai7 pat8 e5 siong7-te3, chiu7-si7 in kap lin2 i2-kip8 lin2 e5 liat8-chou2 sou2 m7-bat--e5; an2-ni jia2 Goa2 e5 siu7-khi3.  4). Chong2-si7 Goa2 bat chhe Goa2 e5 cheng3 lou5-pok8 sian-ti chiu7-kun7 lin2; si7 cha2-cha2 khi2-lai5 chhe i, kong2, Chhiat-chhiat goan7 lin2 m7-thang kiaN5 chit e5 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7, Goa2 sou2 oan3-hun7--e5.  5). Tok8-tok8 in bo5 thiaN, iah8 bo5 aN3 hi7-khang, bo5 oat8-tng2 li7-khui in e5 phaiN2; iu5-goan5 sio-hiuN ti7 pat8-ho7 e5 siong7-te3.  6). In-ui7 an2-ni, Goa2 e5 toa7 siu7-khi3 kap Goa2 e5 siu7-khi3 piaN3-chhut ti7 Iu5-tai7 chiah e5 siaN5, kap Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 koe-chhi7, chhin-chhiuN7 he2 toh8--khi2-lai5; ti3-kau3 in pha-hng leng2-cheng7; chhin-chhiuN7 kin-a2-jit8 an2-ni.  7). TaN Ia5-ho5-hoa ban7-kun e5 Siong7-te3, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3, an2-ni kong2, Lin2 siaN2-su7 kiaN5 chit e5 toa7 phaiN2, hai7 lin2 ka-ki7; hou7 lin2 e5 ta-pou-lang5, hu7-jin5-lang5, gin2-a2, kap chiah8-ni e5 eN-a2, long2 tui3 Iu5-tai7 tiong ka7 lin2 tu5-khi3, bo5 lau5 chit8-e5? Si7 in-ui7 lin2 eng7 lin2 e5 chhiu2 sou2 choe3--e5 kek Goa2 e5 siu7-khi3;  8). ti7 sou2 khi3 kia3-kha e5 Ai-kip8 toe7, sio-hiuN ti7 pat8-ho7 e5 siong7-te3, ti3-kau3 lin2 tu2-tioh8 chau5-biat8, ti7 thiN-e7 ban7-kok tiong, chiaN5-choe3 thang chiu3-chou2, thang leng5-jiok8--e5.  9). Li2 e5 liat8-chou2 e5 phaiN2, Iu5-tai7 liat8-ong5 e5 phaiN2, in e5 hou7-hui e5 phaiN2, lin2 ka-ki7 e5 phaiN2, lin2 e5 bou2 e5 phaiN2, chiu7-si7 ti7 Iu5-tai7 toe7, Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 koe-chhi7 sou2 kiaN5--e5, lin2 boe7 ki3-tit mah?  10). In kau3-taN iau2 bo5 ka-ki7 khiam-pi, bo5 kiaN-hiaN5, bo5 chun-than3 Goa2 ti7 lin2 e5 bin7-cheng5, kap lin2 e5 liat8-chou2 e5 bin7-cheng5, sou2 siat Goa2 e5 hoat-tou7, Goa2 e5 lut8-le7.  11). Sou2-i2 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh ng3 lin2 piN3-bin7, kang3 chai-e7 ti3-kau3 chau5-biat8 Iu5-tai7 e5 cheng3-lang5.  12). Iu5-tai7 sou2 chhun e5 peh-siN3, ngi7-phiN7 khi3 Ai-kip8 toe7, beh ti7-hia kia3-kha--e5, Goa2 beh chhu2 lai5 biat8--in; in beh to2 ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7, in beh tui3 to-kiam3, tui3 ki-hng, lai5 biat8-bo5, tui3 soe3 kau3 toa7, long2 beh tui3 to-kiam3, tui3 ki-hng, lai5 si2; in beh chiaN5-choe3 thang chiu3-chou2, thang gong5-ngiah8, thang loe2-me7, thang leng5-jiok8--e5.  13). In-ui7 Goa2 beh eng7 to-kiam3, eng7 ki-hng, eng7 un-ek8, heng5-hoat8 khia7-khi2 Ai-kip8 toe7--e5; chhin-chhiuN7 Goa2 i2-keng heng5-hoat8 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 chit8-iuN7;  14). hou7 hiah-e5 khi3 Ai-kip8 toe7 sou2 chhun e5 Iu5-tai7 lang5, long2 boe7-tit thoat-li7, a2-si7 lau5-teh, thang to3-lai5 Iu5-tai7 toe7, chiu7-si7 in e5 sim chin him-bou7 to3-lai5 khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7; in-ui7 tit-tioh8 thoat-li7--e5 e5 i2-goa7, bo5 chit8-e5 thang to3-lai5.
	15). Hiah-e5 toa3 ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7 Pa-thek-lo5 e5 lang5, kiN3-na7 chai in e5 bou2 bat tui3 pat8 e5 siong7-te3 sio-hiuN--e5, kap ti7 piN--thau5 teh-khia7 e5 cheng3 hu7-jin5, chu7-chip8 kui toa7-tin7, in3 Ia5-li7-bi2 kong2,  16). Li2 hong7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5 tui3 goan2 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, goan2 m7 thiaN--li2.  17). Goan2 koat-toan3 beh chiaN5 goan2 e5 chhui3 sou2 kong2 it-chhe3 e5 oe7, ng3 Thian-hou7 sio-hiuN, koan3-tian7, chiau3 goan2 kap goan2 e5 liat8-chou2, goan2 e5 kun-ong5, goan2 e5 kui3-chok8, ti7 Iu5-tai7 chiah e5 siaN5, kap Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 koe-chhi7, peng5-sou3 sou2 kiaN5--e5 chit8-iuN7; in-ui7 hit-si5 goan2 e5 sit8-but8 chhiong-chiok, hiong2-siu7 peng5-an; peng7-bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 chai-e7.  18). Chong2-si7 tui3 goan2 theng5-chi2 bo5 sio-hiuN, bo5 koan3-tian7 ti7 Thian-hou7, goan2 hoan2-tng2 khiam3-kheh it-chhe3; koh tui3 to-kiam3, tui3 ki-hng lai5 biat8-bo5.  19). Goan2 tui3 Thian-hou7 sio-hiuN koan3-tian7 e5 si5, goan2 choe3-piaN2 lai5 hok8-sai7 i, tui3 i koan3-tian7, goan2 tiong7-hu kiam2 bo5 hun7 mah?  20). Ia5-li7-bi2 chiu7 in3 hiah e5 peh-siN3, chiu7-si7 tui3 hiah e5 ta-pou hu7-jin5 eng7 chit e5 oe7 in3--i e5 peh-siN3, kong2,  21). Lin2 kap lin2 e5 liat8-chou2, lin2 e5 kun-ong5, lin2 e5 kui3-chok8, kap kok-lai7 e5 peh-siN3, ti7 Iu5-tai7 chiah e5 siaN5, kap Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 koe-chhi7 sou2 sio e5 hiuN, Ia5-ho5-hoa kiam2 bo5 ki3-tit--in, sim-lai7 kiam2 bo5 siuN7 mah?  22). Ia5-ho5-hoa in-ui7 lin2 sou2 choe3 e5 phaiN2, sou2 kiaN5 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7, boe7 koh lun2--tit; sou2-i2 lin2 e5 toe7 pha-hng, chiaN5-choe3 thang gong5-ngiah8, thang chiu3-chou2, bo5 lang5 khia7-khi2, chhin-chhiuN7 kin-a2-jit8 chit-khoan2.  23). In-ui7 lin2 sio-hiuN, iah8 in-ui7 lin2 tek-choe7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, iah8 bo5 thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7, bo5 than3 I e5 lut8-hoat, I e5 tiau5-le7, I e5 kan-cheng3 e5 oe7, sou2-i2 lin2 tu2-tioh8 chit e5 chai-e7, chhin-chhiuN7 kin-a2-jit8 chit-khoan2.
	24). Ia5-li7-bi2 koh tui3 cheng3 peh-siN3 kap cheng3 hu7-jin5-lang5 kong2, Lin2 ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7 it-chhe3 e5 Iu5-tai7 lang5, tioh8 thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7.  25). Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 an2-ni kong2, Lin2 kap lin2 e5 bou2 bat eng7 chhui3 kong2, eng7 chhiu2 chiaN5--i, kong2, Goan2 sou2 he7 e5 goan7, koat-toan3 beh kiaN5--i, chiu7-si7 beh tui3 Thian-hou7 sio-hiuN, iah8 beh tui3 i koan3-tian7; taN choe3 li2 kian-kou3 li2 e5 goan7, lai5 kiaN5 li2 e5 goan7.  26). Sou2-i2 lin2 toa3 Ai-kip8 toe7 it-chhe3 e5 Iu5-tai7 lang5, tioh8 thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7; Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 ki2 Goa2 e5 toa7-mia5 lai5 chiu3-choa7, ti7 Ai-kip8 choan5-toe7, Goa2 e5 mia5 bo5 koh hou7 Iu5-tai7 chok8 chit8-lang5 e5 chhui3 sou2 chheng-hou, kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 eng2-oah8.  27). KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh ti3-i3 ti7 in, beh kang3 chai-e7, bo5 kang3 hok-khi3, ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7 it-chhe3 e5 Iu5-tai7 lang5 beh tui3 to-kiam3, tui3 ki-hng lai5 biat8-bo5, kau3 long2 liau2.  28). Thoat-li7 to-kiam3, beh tui3 Ai-kip8 toe7 to3-lai5 Iu5-tai7 toe7--e5, in e5 lang5-giah8 chin-chio2; hiah-e5 sou2 chhun e5 Iu5-tai7 lang5 khi3 Ai-kip8 toe7, beh ti7-hia kia3-kha-e5, beh chai chi7-chui7 e5 oe7 tit-tioh8 eng3-giam7, si7 Goa2-e5 a2-si7 in-e5.  29). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 ti7 chit e5 sou2-chai7 beh heng5-hoat8 lin2, beh u7 chit e5 tiau7-thau5, hou7 lin2 chai Goa2 sou2 kong2 kang3 chai-e7 hou7 lin2 hiah e5 oe7 tek-khak eng3-giam7.  30). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh chiong Ai-kip8 ong5 Hoat-lo2 Hap8-hut-lah8 kau ti7 i e5 tui3-tek8 e5 chhiu2, kap siau3-siuN7 i e5 siN3-mia7 e5 lang5 e5 chhiu2; chhin-chhiuN7 Goa2 u7 chiong Iu5-tai7 ong5 Se-ti2-ka kau ti7 i e5 tui3-tek8, chiu7-si7 siau3-siuN7 i e5 siN3-mia7 e5 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat e5 chhiu2.

[45]	Iu5-tai7 ong5 Iok-se-a e5 kiaN2 Iok-nga2-keng3 si3--ni5, Ni5-li7-a e5 kiaN2, Pa-liok8, chiong sian-ti Ia5-li7-bi2 sou2 thoan5 hiah e5 oe7 ki3 ti7 chheh--nih;  2). hit-si5 Ia5-li7-bi2 tui3 i kong2, Pa-liok8 ah, Ia5-ho5-hoa I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 lun7-kau3 li2 u7 an2-ni kong2:  3). Li2 bat kong2, Goa2 u7 chai-e7 ah; Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 goa2 thong3-khou2 e5 teng2-bin7 ke-thiN iu-chhiu5; goa2 thou2-khui3 kau3 ia3-sian7, boe7 tit-tioh8 peng5-an.  4). TaN li2 tioh8 an2-ni ka7 i kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 sou2 kian3-lip8--e5, Goa2 beh thiah-hui2, Goa2 sou2 chai-cheng3--e5, Goa2 beh puih8--khi2-lai5; choan5-toe7 long2 an2-ni.  5). Li2 ui7 ka-ki7 tou5-bou5 toa7 tai7-chi3 mah? boh8-tit tou5-bou5.  KhoaN3 ah, in-ui7 Goa2 beh hou7 chai-e7 kang3-loh8 ti7 kiN3 u7 hiat-khi3--e5.  Chong2-si7 li2 bo5-lun7 khi3 toh-loh8, Goa2 beh hou7 li2 khioh--tioh8 ka-ki7 e5 siN3-mia7; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.

[46]	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 sian-ti Ia5-li7-bi2, lun7-khi2 liat8-kok e5 su7.  2). Lun7 Ai-kip8: si7 lun7 Ai-kip8 ong5 Hoat-lo2-ni5-ko e5 kun-peng, chat-iaN5 ti7 Pek-lat8 ho5-piN e5 Ka-ki-bi2-si, tng Iu5-tai7 ong5 Iok-se-a e5 kiaN2 Iok-nga2-keng3 si3--ni5 hou7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat sou2 phah-pai7--e5.
	3). Lin2 tioh8 pi7-pan7 toa7-sio2 e5 tin5-pai5, khi3 kau-chian3.  4). Lin2 tioh8 tho3 be2, khia5 be2, ti3 khoe khia7--khi2-lai5; boa5 chhiuN, chheng7 chian3-kah.  5). Goa2 siaN2-su7 khoaN3-kiN3 an2-ni? in kiaN-hiaN5 the3-au7; in e5 iong2-su7 thai5-su, kin2-kin2 chau2, bo5 oat8-thau5; si3-chiu-ui5 u7 kiaN-hiaN5; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  6). Gau5-chau2-e5 chau2-boe7-li7, iong2-su7 boe7-oe7 thoat-li7; ti7 pak-hng, Pek-lat8 ho5-piN, in long2 tioh8-tak poah8-to2.  7). Chit-e5 chhin-chhiuN7 Ni5-lo5 ho5 tiong3-moa2, chhin-chhiuN7 kang-ho5 e5 chui2 gia5-eng2--e5, si7 chi7-chui7 ah?  8). Ai-kip8 chhin-chhiuN7 Ni5-lo5 ho5 tiong3-moa2, i e5 chui2 chhin-chhiuN7 kang-ho5 gia5-eng2; i e5 oe7 kong2, Goa2 beh chheng3-koaiN5, goa2 beh jia-kham3 pian3-toe7; goa2 beh hui2-hoai7 siaN5 kap ki5-tiong khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3.  9). Be2 tioh8 kin2 chiuN7--lai5; chhia tioh8 loan7-loan7 chau2; iong2-su7 tioh8 chhut--lai5; Kou2-sit8 kap Hut e5 lang5 long2 gia5 tin5-pai5; Lou7-tek e5 lang5 gau5 khui-keng.  10). In-ui7 hit-jit8 si7 Chu2, ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 jit8, po3-siu5 e5 jit8, thang tui3 I e5 tui3-tek8 po3-siu5; to-kiam3 beh thun-chiah8 kau3-pa2, lim huih kau3-chui3; in-ui7 Chu2, ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, ti7 pak-hng Pek-lat8 ho5-piN u7 hian3-che3 e5 su7.  11). Ai-kip8 e5 peh-siN3 ah, tioh8 chiuN7--khi3 Ki-liat8, lai5 chhu2 ju2-hiuN; li2 eng7 choe7-choe7 ioh8 si7 khang-khang; li2 boe7 tit-tioh8 i-ho2.  12). Liat8-pang thiaN-kiN3 li2 e5 leng5-jiok8; pian3-toe7 long2 si7 li2 ai-khau3 e5 siaN; in-ui7 iong2-su7 kap iong2-su7 saN-khap8, choe3 chit8-e7 poah8-to2.
	13). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 sian-ti Ia5-li7-bi2 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, lun7-kau3 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat beh kau3, lai5 kong-kek Ai-kip8 toe7.
	14). Lin2 tioh8 po3-iong5 ti7 Ai-kip8, soan-pou3 ti7 Bit8-toat8, soan-pou3 ti7 Lo5-hut kap Tap-pi2-lek8, kong2, Tioh8 pai5-tui7, ka-ki7 pi7-pan7, in-ui7 to-kiam3 ti7 li2 e5 si3-ui5 teh thun-biat8.  15). Li2 e5 toa7-lat8--e5 chaiN2-iuN7 poah8-to2? in khia7 boe7 chai7, in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa koaN2 in.  16). I hou7 choe7-choe7 lang5 poah8-to2; tai7-ke to2 saN-thah8; in chiu7 kong2, Khi2--lai5, lan2 to3--lai5 khi3 pun2-chok8, kau3 lan2 pun2 sou2-chai7, lai5 siam2-pi7 ap-che3 lan2 e5 to-kiam3.  17). In ti7-hia kio3 kong2, Ai-kip8 ong5 Hoat-lo2 put-ko3 si7 chit8 e5 siaN, i u7 phah-sng2 i e5 ki-hoe7.  18). Toa7 kun-ong5, I e5 mia5 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, kong2, Goa2 ki2 Goa2 e5 oah8-mia7 lai5 chiu3-choa7, i beh lai5 chhin-chhiuN7 soaN-tiong e5 Tha-pok8, chhin-chhiuN7 hai2-piN e5 Ka-bit8.  19). Khia7-khi2 ti7 Ai-kip8 e5 peh-siN3 ah, li2 tioh8 pi7-pan7 siu7-liah8 eng3-iong7 e5 mih8-kiaN7, in-ui7 Lo5-hut beh pha-hng sio-hui2, bo5 lang5 khia7-khi2.  20). Ai-kip8 si7 sui2 e5 gu5-cheng2-a2, tok8-tok8 tui3 pak-hng chhut e5 hui2-biat8 lai5 lah, lai5 lah.  21). Ki5-tiong kou3-chhiaN3 e5 peng, chhin-chhiuN7 tiau5-lai7 pui5 e5 gu5-a2, in oat8-tng2-sin choe3 chit8-e7 chau2, khia7-boe7-tiau5; in-ui7 in tu2-tioh8 hoan7-lan7 e5 jit8, siu7 heng5-hoat8 e5 si5 i2-keng kau3 lah.  22). I e5 siaN chhin-chhiuN7 choa5, teh kiaN5; tui3-tek8 beh kui-tin7 lai5, in beh kiah8 pou2-thau5 lai5 kong-kek--i, chhin-chhiuN7 chho3-chhiu7 e5 lang5 chit8-iuN7.  23). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, I e5 chhiu7-na5 sui-jian5 chin-bat8, in iah8 beh chho3 i; in-ui7 in pi2 chhau2-meh khah choe7, boe7-oe7 sng3--tit.  24). Ai-kip8 e5 peh-siN3 beh kian3-siau3, beh kau ti7 pak-hng e5 peh-siN3 e5 chhiu2.  25). Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3, kong2:  KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh heng5-hoat8 siok8 ti7 Lo5 e5 A-bun5, kap Hoat-lo2, kap Ai-kip8, kap i e5 sin5-beng5, kap i e5 kun-ong5; iah8 beh heng5-hoat8 Hoat-lo2, i2-kip8 oa2-kho3 i e5 lang5.  26). Goa2 beh chiong in kau ti7 siau3-siuN7 in e5 siN3-mia7 e5 lang5 e5 chhiu2, kap Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat e5 chhiu2, kap i e5 jin5-sin5 e5 chhiu2; i2-au7 Ai-kip8 tek-khak koh u7 lang5 khia7-khi2, kap cha2-cheng5 chit8-iuN7; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	27). Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 Nga2-kok ah, li2 boh8-tit kiaN; I2-sek-liat8 ah, boh8-tit kiaN-hiaN5; khoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh tui3 hng7-hng7 e5 sou2-chai7 chin2-kiu3 li2; tui3 siu7-liah8--khi3 e5 toe7 chin2-kiu3 li2 e5 hou7-e3; Nga2-kok beh to3--lai5, tit-tioh8 an-cheng7, peng5-an, bo5 lang5 hou7 i kiaN-hiaN5.  28). Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 Nga2-kok ah, boh8-tit kiaN-hiaN5, in-ui7 Goa2 kap li2 ti7-teh; iah8 beh chiong Goa2 sou2 koaN2 li2 kau3 hiah e5 kok it-chin7 chau5-biat8; chong2-si7 bo5 it-chin7 chau5-biat8 li2; beh chiau3 sou2 hap8-gi5--e5, chek-pi7 li2, toan3-toan3 boe7-oe7 bo5 heng5-hoat8 li2; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.

[47]	Hoat-lo2 kong-kek Ka-sat e5 tai7-seng, u7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lun7 Hui-li7-su7 lang5 e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 sian-ti Ia5-li7-bi2.
	2). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, u7 chui2 tui3 pak-hng chheng3--khi2-lai5, chiaN5-choe3 tiong3-moa2 e5 ho5, beh tiong3-moa2 chit e5 toe7, kap ki5-tiong sou2 u7-e5, kap siaN5 kap ki5-tiong sou2 khia7-khi2--e5; lang5 beh au5-kio3, keng2-lai7 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 beh thi5-khau3.  3). Ui7-tioh8 tui3-tek8 iong2 e5 be2, i e5 toe5 khok8-khok8-hau2 e5 siaN, ia7 ui7-tioh8 i hiah e5 chian3-chhia kin2-kin2 chau2, i e5 chhia-lun5 hu7-hu7-hau2, chiu7 chiah-e5 choe3 lau7-pe7--e5 chhiu2 nng2, bo5 oat8-thau5 khoaN3 i e5 kiaN2.  4). In-ui7 si5-jit8 kau3 lah, beh hui2-biat8 it-chhe3 e5 Hui-li7-su7 lang5, beh tui3 Chhui-lo5 Se-tun3 chian2-tu5 sou2 chhun pang-chan7 in--e5; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh hui2-biat8 Hui-li7-su7 lang5, Ka-hui-thok hai2-su7 sou2 chhun e5 peh-siN3.  5). Ka-sat i2-keng bo5 poaN3-ki thau5-mng5; A-sit8-ki-lun5 kui ti7 bo5; soaN-kok sou2 chhun--e5, li2 ka-ki7 koah-bah, beh kau3 joa7-ku2 ah?  6). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 to-kiam3 ah, li2 beh kau3 ti7-si5 chiah soah? tioh8 kiu jip8 li2 e5 to-siu3, an-cheng7 bo5 tin2-tang7.  7). Ia5-ho5-hoa i2-keng beng7-leng7 li2 kong-kek A-sit8-ki-lun5, kong-kek hai2-piN e5 toe7; I i2-keng phai3 li2 tiaN7-tioh8, li2 thai2-tho2 oe7 theng5-chi2 ah?

[48]	Lun7 Mou5-ap. Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 an2-ni kong2, Ni5-pho u7 chai-e7 ah, in-ui7 siu7 hui2-hoai7; Ki-liat8-teng5 tu2-tioh8 kian3-siau3, siu7-chhu2; Bi2-su-ka tu2-tioh8 kian3-siau3, siu7 pai7-hoai7.  2). Mou5-ap bo5 koh siu7 o-lo2, u7 lang5 ti7 Hi-sit8-pun2 siat ke3-bou5 beh hai7 i; kong2, Lai5 lah, lan2 ka7 i chian2-tu5, hou7 i bo5 koh chiaN5-choe3 kok.  Ma2-tek-bian5 ah, li2 iah8 tioh8 cheng7-cheng7, boh8 choe3 siaN; to-kiam3 beh tui-koaN2 li2.  3). Tui3 Ho5-lo5-liam7 u7 au5-kio3 e5 siaN, u7 chhiuN2-kiap kap toa7 e5 hui2-biat8.  4). Mou5-ap tu2-tioh8 hui2-biat8, i e5 gin2-a2 hau2 e5 siaN hou7 lang5 thiaN-kiN3.  5). In-ui7 lang5 peh-chiuN7 Lou2-hi e5 soaN-phiaN5, na2-kiaN5 na2-khau3; loh8 Ho5-lo5-liam7 e5 soaN-phiaN5, thiaN-kiN3 hui2-biat8 ai-khau3 e5 siaN.  6). Lin2 tioh8 to5-chau2, ka-ki7 kiu3 siN3-mia7; chhin-chhiuN7 khong3-ia2 e5 tou7-siong5.  7). Li2 in-ui7 oa2-kho3 ka-ki7 e5 sou2-choe3, kap ka-ki7 e5 chai5-po2, iah8 beh siu7-liah8.  Ki-boat kap siok8 i e5 che3-si kui3-chok8, iah8 beh choe3-chit8-e7 siu7 chhian-i5.  8). KiaN5 hui2-biat8--e5, beh kau3 tak8 e5 siaN5; bo5 chit8 e5 siaN5 oe7 bian2-tit; soaN-kok beh ti3-kau3 pai7-loh8, piN5-iuN5 beh siu7 hui2-hoai7, chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 kong2--e5.  9). Tioh8 eng7 sit8 hou7 Mou5-ap, hou7 i pe-chau2; i chiah e5 siaN5 beh ti3-kau3 pha-hng, bo5 lang5 khia7-khi2.  10). Chhin3-chhin3 chhai2-chhai2 choe3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 kang--e5, tioh8 siu7 chiu3-chou2; kim3-chi2 i e5 to bak-tioh8 huih--e5, tioh8 siu7 chiu3-chou2.  11). Mou5-ap tui3 siau3-lian5 i2-lai5, siong5-siong5 hiong2-siu7 peng5-an; chhin-chhiuN7 che7-chheng e5 chiu2, bo5 tui3 chit e5 khi3-ku7 piaN3 ti7 pat8 e5 khi3-ku7; iah8 be7 bat siu7-liah8; in-ui7 an2-ni i e5 goan5-bi7 iau2 ti7-teh, khi3-bi7 be7 pian3.  12). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, KhoaN3 ah, jit8-chi2 beh kau3, Goa2 beh chhe piaN3-chiu2--e5 khi3 i hia, ka7 i piaN3-chhut--lai5; piaN3-khang i e5 khi3-ku7, phah-phoa3 i e5 chiu2-ang3.  13). Mou5-ap beh ui7-tioh8 Ki-boat lai5 kian3-siau3, chhin-chhiuN7 I2-sek-liat8-ke ui7-tioh8 in sou2 oa2-kho3 e5 Pek-tek8-li7 lai5 kian3-siau3 chit8-iuN7.  14). Li2 chaiN2-iuN7 kong2, Goan2 si7 iong2-su7, si7 u7 lat8 thang kau-chian3 e5 lang5?  15). Mou5-ap piN3-choe3 pha-hng, tui3-tek8 chiuN7-khi3, jip8 i hiah e5 siaN5; sou2 keng2-soan2 e5 siau3-lian5 lang5 loh8-khi3 tu2-tioh8 thai5-si2; che si7 Kun-ong5, mia5 choe3 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, kong2--e5.  16). Mou5-ap e5 chai-e7 kun7 lah, i e5 hoan7-lan7 kin2-kin2 kau3.  17). KiN3-na7 ti7 i e5 chiu-ui5, bat i e5 mia5--e5, lin2 long2 tioh8 ui7 i pi-siong; kong2, Hit e5 iong2 e5 thui5, sui2 e5 koaiN2-a2, thai2 oe7 chih8 kau3 an2-ni?  18). Toa3 ti7 Ti2-pun2 e5 peh-siN3 ah, tioh8 tui3 li2 eng5-kng e5 ui7 loh8-lai5, che7 ti7 ta-so3 e5 toe7; in-ui7 hui2-biat8 Mou5-ap--e5 chiuN7-lai5 kong-kek li2, hui2-hoai7 li2 hiah e5 oe7-sou2.  19). Toa3 ti7 A-lo5-jiN2--e5 ah, tioh8 khia7 ti7 lou7-piN koan-khoaN3, mng7 to5-chau2 e5 ta-pou-lang5, kap thoat-li7 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, kong2, Si7 sim2-mih8 tai7-chi3 ah?  20). Mou5-ap in-ui7 hui2-hoai7 lai5 kian3-siau3, lin2 tioh8 thi5-khau3 au5-kio3; tioh8 ti7 A-lun3 po3-ko3, kong2, Mou5-ap piN3-choe3 pha-hng.  21). Heng5-hoat8 i2-keng kau3 ti7 piN5-iuN5 e5 toe7, ti7 Ho5-lun5, ti7 Nga2-chap8, ti7 Bi2-hoat-ap;  22). ti7 Ti2-pun2, ti7 Ni5-pho, ti7 Pek-te-pi2-lah8-thai3-im;  23). ti7 Ki-liat8-teng5, ti7 Pek-ka-boat8, ti7 Pek-bi2-un;  24). ti7 Ka-liok8, ti7 Pho-su-lah8, kap Mou5-ap toe7 hng7-kun7 sou2 u7 e5 siaN5.  25). Mou5-ap e5 kak chho3-tng7 lah, i e5 chhiu2-kut at-chih8 lah; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  26). Lin2 tioh8 hou7 Mou5-ap chiu2-chui3; in-ui7 i chu7-ko, poe7-gek8 Ia5-ho5-hoa; i beh ti7 i sou2 thou3 e5 tiong-kan ko7-lai5 ko7-khi3; koh beh hou7 lang5 thi2-chhio3.  27). I2-sek-liat8 kiam2 m7-bat hou7 li2 thi2-chhio3 mah? i kiam2 si7 ti7 chhat8 e5 tiong-kan hou7 lang5 chha5-chhut mah? in-ui7 li2 tak8-pai2 kong2-khi2 i e5 si5, chiu7 io5-thau5 poaN7-hi7.  28). Khia7-khi2 ti7 Mou5-ap--e5 ah, lin2 tioh8 li7-khui chiah e5 siaN5, khia7-khi2 ti7 chioh8-poaN5; chhin-chhiuN7 ka-chui choh-siu7 ti7 khang-khau2 e5 piN.  29). Goan2 u7 thiaN-kiN3 Mou5-ap e5 kiau-ngou7, i e5 kiau-ngou7 kau3-kek8; i e5 chu7-ko, i e5 kiau-ngou7, i e5 bu2-ban7, chun5-sim ka-ki7 liah8 choe3-toa7.  30). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 chai i e5 siu7-khi3, kap i khang-khang e5 khoa-khau2, sou2-kiaN5 si7 khang-khang.  31). In-ui7 an2-ni, goa2 beh ui7-tioh8 Mou5-ap thi5-khau3, goa2 beh ui7-tioh8 Mou5-ap choan5-toe7 au5-kio3; in beh ui7-tioh8 Kiat-jiN2-hap-liat8-siat e5 lang5 thou2-khui3.  32). Se-pi2-ma2 e5 phu5-to5-chhiu7 ah, goa2 ui7-tioh8 li2 thi5-khau3, pi2 Nga2-sia7 lang5 e5 thi5-khau3 khah siong-tiong7; li2 e5 ki thoaN3-ke3 hai2, tit8-tit8 chhun kau3 Nga2-sia7 e5 hai2; hit e5 kiaN5 hui2-biat8--e5 i2-keng lim5-kau3 li2 beh siu-seng5 e5 ke2-chi2, kap li2 e5 phu5-to5.  33). Pui5 e5 chhan5 kap Mou5-ap toe7, i e5 hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8 long2 bo5--khi3.  Goa2 hou7 chiu2-khut e5 chiu2 bo5--khi3; bo5 lang5 tah8 chiu2, chhut hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN, hit e5 siaN m7-si7 hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN.  34). In-ui7 Hi-sit8-pun2 ai-siong e5 siaN thang3-kau3 I2-li7-a-li7, tit8-tit8 kau3 Nga2-chap8, koh tui3 So2-jiN2 kau3 Ho5-lo5-liam7, tit8-kau3 I-ki-lah8 Si-li7-si-a, in-ui7 Leng5-lim5 e5 chui2 tek-khak kou-ta5.  35). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 beh ti7 Mou5-ap toe7, hou7 hit e5 hian3-che3 ti7 soaN-thau5-toaN5--e5 kap hit e5 sio-hiuN ti7 i hiah e5 sin5-beng5--e5, long2 soah.  36). In-ui7 an2-ni, goa2 e5 sim ui7-tioh8 Mou5-ap chhin-chhiuN7 phin2-siau teh tan5; goa2 e5 sim ui7-tioh8 Kiat-jiN2-hap-liat8-siat lang5 chhin-chhiuN7 phin2-siau teh tan5; in-ui7 in sou2 chek-chu7 e5 chai5-but8 long2 bo5--khi3.  37). Thau5-khak tak8-e5 kng-kho7-kho7, chhui3-chhiu tak8-e5 chian2 te2-te2, chhiu2-kut tak8-e5 koah-siong, io ha5 moa5-pou3.  38). Ti7 Mou5-ap tak8-keng e5 chhu3-teng2, kap i hiah e5 koe-chhi7, tak8 sou2-chai7 u7 thi5-khau3; in-ui7 Goa2 kong-phoa3 Mou5-ap, chhin-chhiuN7 kong3-phoa3 m7-teng3-i3 e5 khi3-ku7.  Che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  39). I hui2-hoai7 kau3 an2-ni! in thi5-khau3 kau3 an2-ni!  Mou5-ap kian3-siau3 oat8-to3-tng2 kau3 an2-ni! chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, Mou5-ap beh hou7 si3-ui5 e5 lang5 thi2-chhio3 gong5-ngiah8.  40). In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, i beh chhin-chhiuN7 eng-chiau2 pe--lai5, thi2-khui i e5 sit8 ti7 Mou5-ap.  41). Ka-liok8 hou7 lang5 chhu2--khi3, hiah e5 oe7-sou2 hou7 lang5 chiam3--khi3; kau3 hit-jit8, Mou5-ap chiah e5 iong2-su7 e5 sim chhin-chhiuN7 beh siN-kiaN2 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 sim.  42). Mou5-ap beh tu2-tioh8 hui2-biat8, bo5 koh chiaN5-choe3 kok; in-ui7 in chu7-ko, poe7-gek8 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  43). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Mou5-ap khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 ah, kiaN-hiaN5, ham7-khiN, oah8-tauh, long2 kau3 ti7 li2.  44). Chau2-pi7 kiaN-hiaN5-e5, beh poah8-loh8 ham7-khiN; tui3 ham7-khiN peh--khi2-lai5 e5, beh hou7 oah8-tauh tauh-tioh8; in-ui7 Goa2 beh hou7 heng5-hoat8 e5 ni5 lim5-kau3 Mou5-ap; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  45). Hiah e5 to5-chau2--e5 khui3-lat8 chin7, khia7 ti7 Hi-sit8-pun2 im3-ng2-e7; chong2-si7 he2 tui3 Hi-sit8-pun2 chhut, he2-iam7 tui3 Se-hong5 hoat, it-chin7 sio Mou5-ap e5 pian-kai3, kap chok-loan7 e5 lang5 thau5-khak e5 teng2-bin7.  46). Mou5-ap ah, li2 u7 chai-e7; Ki-boat e5 peh-siN3 biat8-bo5 lah, li2 e5 cheng3-kiaN2 hou7 lang5 liah8--khi3, li2 e5 cheng3 cha-bou2-kiaN2 choe3 siu7-liah8--e5.  47). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Chong2-si7 kau3 jit8-au7, Goa2 beh hou7 Mou5-ap siu7-liah8 e5 lang5 to3-tng2.  Lun7 Mou5-ap siu7 sim2-phoaN3 e5 oe7, kau3 chia ui5-chi2.

[49]	Lun7 A-bun5.  Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, I2-sek-liat8 bo5 kiaN2 mah? bo5 hou7-su5 mah? Ma2-lek8-kham chaiN2-iuN7 tit-tioh8 Ka-tek e5 toe7 choe3 giap8, i e5 peh-siN3 chaiN2-iuN7 khia7-khi2 i tiong-kan hiah e5 siaN5?  2). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, KhoaN3 ah, jit8-chi2 beh kau3, Goa2 beh hou7 kau-chian3 e5 siaN thiaN ti7 A-bun5 chok8 e5 Lah8-pa, i beh chiaN5-choe3 pha-hng e5 thou5-tui; i chiah e5 siaN5 beh hou7 he2 sio; cheng5 chiam3 I2-sek-liat8--e5, taN beh hou7 I2-sek-liat8 chiam3 to3-tng2; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  3). Hi-sit8-pun2 ah, li2 tioh8 ai-khau3, in-ui7 Gai7 e5 siaN5 piN3-choe3 pha-hng; Lah8-pa e5 peh-siN3 ah, tioh8 au5-kio3, eng7 moa5-pou3 ha5-io; tioh8 thi5-khau3, kiaN5-lai5 kiaN5-khi3 ti7 li5-pa-tiong; in-ui7 Ma2-lek8-kham kap i e5 che3-si kui3-chok8 beh choe3 chit8-e7 hou7 lang5 liah8-khi3.  4). Poe7-gek8 e5 peh-siN3 ah, lin2 siaN2-su7 in-ui7 hiah e5 soaN-kok, chiu7-si7 chui2 lun7-tek8 e5 soaN-kok, lai5 khoa-khau2 ah? li2 oa2-kho3 chai5-po2, kong2, Chi7-chui7 oe7 lai5 kau3 goan2 chia.  5). Chu2 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh hou7 kiaN-hiaN5 tui3 si3-ui5 lim5-kau3 lin2; lin2 beh siu7 koaN2-chhut, tak8-lang5 tit8-tit8 khi3; chau2 bo5 lou7--e5, bo5 lang5 thang chu7-chip8.  6). Chong2-si7 au7-lai5 Goa2 beh hou7 A-bun5 chok8 siu7-liah8 e5 lang5 to3-tng2; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	7). Lun7 I2-tong.  Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Ti7 The5-ban7 bo5 koh u7 ti3-hui7 mah? Chhang-mia5 e5 lang5 bo5 koh u7 ke3-ek8 mah? in e5 ti3-hui7 bo5--khi3 mah?  8). Ti2-tan3 e5 peh-siN3 ah, the3--khi3 ah, to5-chau2 ah, bih khi3 bat8 ah; in-ui7 Goa2 heng5-hoat8 I2-so3 e5 si5, beh hou7 i e5 chai-e7 kau3 ti7 i.  9). Ban2 phu5-to5--e5 na7 kau3 li2 hia ban2, kiam2 bo5 iau2 lau5 kui2-liap8-a2 mah? chhat8 na7 mi5--si5 lai5, kiam2 m7-si7 sng2-tng7 kau3 moa2-i3 na7-tiaN7?  10). Chong2-si7 Goa2 hou7 I2-so3 kng-liu-liu, lou7-hian7 i khng3-bat8 e5 sou2-chai7, ti3-kau3 bo5 te3 thang bih; i e5 hou7-e3, i e5 hiaN-ti7, i e5 chhu3-piN long2 sit-pai7; i iah8 kui ti7 bo5.  11). Tioh8 chiong li2 bo5-pe7 e5 kiaN2 pang3-he7-teh, Goa2 beh po2-choan5 in oah8; li2 chiah e5 koaN2-hu7, iah8 tioh8 oa2-kho3 goa2.  12). In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, pun2 m7 eng-kai lim hit e5 poe--e5, tek-khak beh lim--i, boh8-kioh li2, li2 kiam2 oe7 it-chin7 bian2 heng5-hoat8 mah? li2 tek-khak boe7 bian2-tit heng5-hoat8, li2 tek-khak tioh8 lim--i.  13). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 ki2 ka-ki7 lai5 chiu3-choa7, Pho-su-lah8 beh chiaN5-choe3 thang gong5-ngiah8, thang leng5-jiok8, thang chiu3-chou2, koh hong-hoe3; i long2-chong2 e5 siaN5 beh eng2-oan2 piN3-choe3 pha-hng.  14). Goa2 tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa hia thiaN-kiN3 siau-sit, iah8 u7 su3-chia2 hong7-chhe khi3 liat8-kok, kong2, Lin2 tioh8 chu7-chip8 lai5 kong-kek i, tioh8 khi2-lai5 kau-chian3.  15). In-ui7 Goa2 hou7 li2 ti7 liat8-kok-tiong choe3 bi5-soe3, hou7 lang5 khoaN3-khin.  16). Khia7-khi2 chioh8-tong7-lai7, pe2-siu2 soaN-teng2--e5 ah, li2 e5 ui-hong, li2 sim-lai7 e5 kiau-ngou7 ka-ki7 phian3; li2 sui-jian5 chhin-chhiuN7 eng-chiau2, choh li2 e5 siu7 ti7 koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7, Goa2 beh tui3 hia ka7 li2 chhu2-loh8-lai5; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  17). I2-tong beh chiaN5-choe3 thang gong5-ngiah8--e5, kiN3-na7 tui3 hia ke3--e5, tek-khak beh ki5-koai3, in-ui7 i sou2 tu2-tioh8 it-chhe3 e5 chai-e7, lai5 thi2-chhio3 i.  18). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Tek-khak bo5 lang5 khia7-khi2 ti7-hia, iah8 bo5 lang5 kia3-kha ti7-hia; si7 beh chhin-chhiuN7 Sou2-to-ma2, Go5-mou5-lah8, kap hu7-kun7 e5 siaN5 to2-hoai7 chit8-iuN7.  19). KhoaN3 ah, i beh chhin-chhiuN7 sai, tui3 Iok-tan3 ho5-piN e5 chhiu7-na5 khi2--lai5, kong-kek kian-kou3 khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7; bak8-nih-ku2 Goa2 beh hou7 in to5-chau2, li7-khui chit e5 sou2-chai7.  Chi7-chui7 siu7 keng2-soan2, Goa2 chiu7 phai3 i ti7-li2 chit e5 toe7; chi7-chui7 oe7 pi2--tit Goa2? chi7-chui7 oe7 ka7 Goa2 teng7 chit8 e5 ki5 ah? u7 sim2-mih8 bok8-chia2 oe7 khia7 ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5 ah?  20). Sou2-i2 lin2 tioh8 thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 ke3-ek8 kong-kek I2-tong e5 ke3-chhek; i2-kip8 I sou2 chu3-tiaN7 kong-kek The5-ban7 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 e5 chi2-i3; in tiaN7-tioh8 beh chiong hiah e5 iuN5-kun5 e5 soe3--e5 thoa--khi3; I iah8 beh hou7 in khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7 hong-hoe3.  21). In-ui7 in to2-hoai7 e5 siaN, toe7 chiu7 tin2-tang7; in au5-kio3 e5 siaN, thiaN kau3 Ang5-hai2.  22). KhoaN3 ah, i beh khi2--lai5, chhin-chhiuN7 eng-chiau2 pe--lai5, thi2-khui i e5 sit8 ti7 Pho-su-lah8; kau3 hit-jit8, I2-tong chiah e5 iong2-su7 e5 sim chhin-chhiuN7 beh siN-kiaN2 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 sim.
	23). Lun7 Tai7-ma2-sek.  Hap-ma2 kap A-jiN2-poat8 kian3-siau3, in-ui7 in thiaN-kiN3 phaiN2 siau-sit, chiu7 sit-taN2; hai2-bin7 u7 iu-chhiu5, boe7 peng5-cheng7.  24). Tai7-ma2-sek soe-jiok8, oat8-tng2-sin beh to5-chau2, ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah, chiong i liah8-tiau5-tiau5; thong3-khou2 iu-chhiu5 chiong i khiu2-tiau5-tiau5, chhin-chhiuN7 beh siN-kiaN2 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 chit8-iuN7.  25). Thang o-lo2 e5 siaN5, chiu7-si7 Goa2 sou2 hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN5, chaiN2-iuN7 siu7 pang3-sak kau3 an2-ni?  26). I e5 siau3-lian5 lang5 beh ti7 i e5 koe-chhi7 to2--loh8-khi3; tng hit-jit8 i it-chhe3 e5 peng-teng beh biat8-bo5; che si7 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  27). Goa2 iah8 beh hou7 he2 toh8 ti7 Tai7-ma2-sek e5 siaN5-chhiuN5, sio-biat8 Pian7-hap-tat8 e5 kiong-tian7.
	28). Lun7 Ki-tat8 kap Ha7-so2 chiah e5 kok, chiu7-si7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat sou2 phah--e5, Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2:  Li2 khi2-lai5, chiuN7--khi3 Ki-tat8, chau5-biat8 tang-hng e5 lang5.  29). In e5 pou3-piN5 kap iuN5-kun5, lang5 beh chhiuN2--khi3; chiong tiuN3-pak kap it-chhe3 e5 khi3-ku7, kap lok8-to5, chhiuN2 choe3 ka-ki7 e5; lang5 tui3 in hoah kong2, Si3-ui5 long2 u7 kiaN-hiaN5.  30). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Ha7-so2 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 ah, tioh8 to5-chau2, chau2-khi3-hng7, bih-khi3-bat8; in-ui7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat siat-ke3 beh hai7 lin2, tiaN7-tioh8 i3-su3 beh kong-kek lin2.  31). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Khi2--lai5, chiuN7--khi3 kong-kek an-jian5 khia7-khi2 bo5 khoa3-lu7 e5 chok8, in bo5 mng5-hou7, bo5 mng5-chhoaN3, si7 ka-ki7 khia7-khi2--e5.  32). In e5 lok8-to5 beh hou7 lang5 chhiuN2--khi3; in choe7-choe7 cheng-siN beh hou7 lang5 kiap--khi3; kiN3-na7 thi3 pin3-piN--e5, beh koaN2-soaN3 in ti7 si3-hng; hou7 chai-e7 tui3 si3-ui5 kau3 ti7 in; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  33). Ha7-so2 beh chiaN5-choe3 ia2-kau2 tiam3 e5 sou2-chai7, eng2-oan2 chhiN-chhin3, bo5 lang5 ti7-hia khia7-khi2, iah8 bo5 lang5 ti7-hia kia3-kha.
	34). Iu5-tai7 ong5 Se-ti2-ka khi2-thau5 che7-ui7 e5 si5, Ia5-ho5-hoa lun7 I2-lan5 e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 sian-ti Ia5-li7-bi2 kong2,  35). Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh at-chih8 I2-lan5 lang5 e5 keng, chiu7-si7 in siong7-teng2 e5 khui3-lat8.  36). Goa2 beh hou7 si3-bin7 e5 hong tui3 thiN e5 si3-bin7 chhe--lai5, lim5-kau3 I2-lan5 lang5, chiong in koaN2-soaN3 ti7 si3-hng; I2-lan5 siu7 koaN2-soaN3 e5 lang5 bo5 chit8-kok bo5 kau3.  37). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 beh hou7 I2-lan5 lang5 ti7 tui3-tek8 e5 bin7-cheng5 kap siau3-siuN7 in e5 siN3-mia7 e5 lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 lai5 kiaN-hiaN5; Goa2 ia7 beh hou7 chai-e7, chiu7-si7 Goa2 e5 toa7 siu7-khi3, lim5-kau3 in; koh beh hou7 to-kiam3 tui-jip in, kau3 it-chin7 biat8 in.  38). Goa2 beh siat-lip8 Goa2 e5 po2-cho7 ti7 I2-lan5, tui3-hia tu5--khi3 kun-ong5 kap kui3-chok8; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  39). Chong2-si7 kau3 jit8-au7, Goa2 beh hou7 I2-lan5 siu7-liah8 e5 lang5 to3--lai5; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.

[50]	Ia5-ho5-hoa thok sian-ti Ia5-li7-bi2 lun7 Pa-pi2-lun5, lun7 Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 e5 toe7, sou2 kong2 e5 oe7.
	2). Lin2 tioh8 thoan5-pou3 ti7 liat8-pang-tiong hou7 in thiaN-kiN3, tioh8 khia7 toa7-ki5; tioh8 hou7 in thiaN-kiN3, m7-thang un2-moa5; kong2, Pa-pi2-lun5 siu7 kong-phoa3, Pi2-lek8 kian3-siau3, Bi2-lo5-tat8 phah-phaiN2, i e5 put8 long2 kian3-siau3, i e5 ngou2-siong7 long2 phah-phaiN2.  3). In-ui7 u7 chit8-kok tui3 pak-hng khi2-lai5 kong-kek i, beh hou7 i e5 toe7 pha-hng, bo5 lang5 khia7-khi2; lang5 kap cheng-siN long2 chau2--khi3.  4). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Hit-jit8 hit-si5 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 beh lai5, in beh kap Iu5-tai7 lang5 saN-kap lai5, in beh kiaN5-lou7, na2-kiaN5 na2-hau2, lai5 chhe7 in e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  5). In mng7 Sek-an e5 su7, bin7 ng3-hia, kong2, Lai5--lah, lin2 tioh8 kiat eng2-oan2 bo5 boe7-ki3-tit e5 iok, lai5 kap Ia5-ho5-hoa lian5-hap8.
	6). Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 choe3 be5-lou7 e5 iuN5; in e5 bok8-chia2 hou7 in kiaN5 chha-lou7; hou7 in oat--khi3 soaN--nih; in tui3 toa7-soaN kiaN5 kau3 sio2-soaN, boe7-ki3-tit in an-hioh e5 sou2-chai7.  7). KiN3-na7 tu2-tioh8 in-e5 beh thun-chiah8 in; in chiah e5 tui3-tek8 kong2, Goan2 bo5 choe7, in-ui7 in tek-choe7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, chiu7-si7 kong-gi7 khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7, ia7 si7 in e5 liat8-chou2 sou2 ng3-bang7 e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  8). Lin2 tioh8 tui3 Pa-pi2-lun5 tiong to5-chau2, tui3 Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 e5 toe7 chhut--khi3; tioh8 chhin-chhiuN7 kang e5 soaN-iuN5 ti7 iuN5-kun5 e5 thau5-cheng5.  9). Goa2 beh kek-tong7 choe7-choe7 toa7-kok tui3 pak-hng saN-kap lai5 kong-kek Pa-pi2-lun5; in beh pai5-tin7 kong-kek i; i beh tui3-hia siu7 kong-phoa3; in e5 chiN3 beh chhin-chhiuN7 gau5 sia7 e5 iong2-su7 e5 chiN3, long2 bo5 khang-khang to3-tng2-lai5.  10). Ka-lek8-ti2 beh hou7 lang5 chhiuN2--khi3; kiN3-na7 chhiuN2-i--e5 long2 beh moa2-i3; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  11). ChhiuN2 Goa2 e5 giap8--e5 ah, in-ui7 lin2 hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8; in-ui7 lin2 thiau3-lai5 thiau3-khi3 chhin-chhiuN7 tah8 gou7-kak e5 gu5-bu2, ia7 teh hau2 chhin-chhiuN7 iong2 e5 be2;  12). lin2 e5 lau7-bu2 beh kian3-siau3 kau3-kek8, siN--li2-e5 tek-khak lau3-khui3; khoaN3 ah, i beh liat8 ti7 chiah e5 kok e5 lou7-be2, chiaN5-choe3 khong3-ia2, choe3 ta-so3 e5 toe7, choe3 soa-bou5.  13). In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 toa7 siu7-khi3, tek-khak bo5 lang5 khia7-khi2, beh choan5-jian5 pha-hng; kiN3-na7 keng-ke3 Pa-pi2-lun5--e5 beh gong5-ngiah8, ia7 in-ui7 i sou2 tu2-tioh8 chiah e5 chai-e7 lai5 thi2-chhio3 i.  14). Khui-keng e5 lang5 ah, lin2 tioh8 ti7 Pa-pi2-lun5 si3-ui5 pai5-tin7; tioh8 sia7-chiN3 kong-kek i, boh8-tit po2-sioh lin2 e5 chiN3; in-ui7 i u7 tek-choe7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  15). Lin2 tioh8 ti7 i e5 si3-ui5 hoah-hiam3; i i2-keng tau5-hang5; i e5 iaN5-che7 to2-hoai7 lah, siaN5-chhiuN5 thiah-hui2 lah; in-ui7 che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa po3-siu5 e5 su7, lin2 tioh8 ng3 i po3-siu5; i chaiN2-iuN7 khoan2-thai7 lang5, ia7 tioh8 an2-ni khoan2-thai7 i.  16). Lin2 tioh8 tui3 Pa-pi2-lun5 chian2-tu5 ia7-cheng2-e5 kap siu-koah e5 si5 kiah8 liam5-a2 e5; in-ui7 kiaN ap-che3 e5 to-kiam3 tak8-lang5 beh to3--khi3 pun2-chok8, tak8-lang5 beh chau2 kau3 pun2 sou2-chai7.
	17). I2-sek-liat8 si7 si3-soaN3 e5 iuN5, si7 hou7 sai koaN2-chau2--e5; tai7-seng si7 A-sut8 ong5 thun i, lou7-be2 chit e5 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5, Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat, at-chih8 i e5 kut-thau5.  18). Sou2-i2 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3, an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh heng5-hoat8 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 kap i e5 toe7, chhin-chhiuN7 Goa2 bat heng5-hoat8  A-sut8 ong5 chit8-iuN7.  19). Goa2 beh koh chhoa7 I2-sek-liat8 to3-lai5 i e5 chhau2-tiuN5, i beh ti7 Ka-bit8 kap Pa-san chiah8 chhau2; koh ti7 I2-hoat-lian5 soaN kap Ki-liat8 toe7, i e5 sim tit-tioh8 pa2-chiok.  20). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Hit-jit8 hit-si5 beh chha5 I2-sek-liat8 e5 choe7-koa3, ia7 long2-chong2 bo5; beh chhe7 Iu5-tai7 e5 choe7-ok, ia7 chhe7-bo5; in-ui7 goa2 sou2 lau5-teh e5 peh-siN3 Goa2 beh sia3-bian2 in.
	21). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Tioh8 chiuN7-khi3 kong-kek Bi2-lah8-tai7-ong e5 toe7 kap Pi2-kat khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3; tioh8 tui-jip it-chin7 thai5 in, chiau3 Goa2 it-chhe3 sou2 hoan-hu3 li2-e5 khi3 kiaN5.  22). Keng2-lai7 u7 kau-chian3 e5 siaN kap toa7 hui2-biat8.  23). Phah choan5-toe7 e5 toa7 ki thui5 chaiN2-iuN7 phah-chih8 hui2-hoai7 ah! Pa-pi2-lun5 ti7 liat8-kok tiong chaiN2-iuN7 pha-hng ah!  24). Pa-pi2-lun5 ah, Goa2 ui7 li2 siat oah8-tauh, li2 hou7 i tauh-tioh8 ia7 m7-chai; li2 hou7 lang5 chhe7-tioh8, liah8-tioh8, in-ui7 li2 kap Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3 tui3-tek8.  25). Ia5-ho5-hoa i2-keng khui I e5 kun-chong-kek8, kiah8-chhut I toa7 siu7-khi3 e5 khi3-hai5; in-ui7 Chu2, ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, u7 tai7-chi3 ti7 Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 e5 toe7.  26). Lin2 tioh8 tui3 kek8-hng7 e5 piN-kai3 lai5 kong-kek i; khui i e5 chhek-chhng; hiat i chiaN5 thou5-tui, it-chin7 biat8 i, bo5 lau5 poaN3-hang7.  27). Tioh8 thai5 i it-chhe3 e5 gu5-kang2; hou7 in loh8--khi3 siu7-thai5; in u7 chai-e7 ah! in-ui7 pan7 in e5 jit8, hit e5 ki5 i2-keng kau3.  28). U7 tui3 Pa-pi2-lun5 toe7 to5-chau2 chhut-lai5-e5 e5 siaN, ti7 Sek-an po3-ko3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 po3-siu5, chiu7-si7 I ui7-tioh8 I e5 tian7 lai5 po3-siu5.  29). Tioh8 chio-chip8 sia7-chiN3 e5 peng, chiu7-si7 it-chhe3 khui-keng--e5, lai5 kong-kek Pa-pi2-lun5; ti7 i e5 si3-ui5 chat-iaN5 lai5 phah i; m7-thang hou7 i chau2 chit8-e5; chiau3 i sou2 choe3--e5 po3-eng3 i; i chaiN2-iuN7 khoan2-thai7 lang5, tioh8 chiau3 an2-ni khoan2-thai7 i; in-ui7 i kiau-ngou7 poe7-gek8 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Seng3--e5.  30). In-ui7 an2-ni i e5 siau3-lian5 lang5 beh ti7 i e5 koe-chhi7 to2--loh8-khi3, tng hit-jit8 i it-chhe3 e5 peng-teng beh biat8-bo5; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  31). Chu2, ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, KhoaN3 ah, kiau-ngou7--e5 ah, goa2 choe3 li2 e5 tui3-tek8; in-ui7 Goa2 pan7 li2 e5 jit8, hit e5 ki5 i2-keng kau3.  32). Kiau-ngou7--e5 tioh8-tak poah8-to2, bo5 lang5 hu5 i khi2--lai5; Goa2 beh hou7 he2 ti7 i hiah e5 siaN5 toh8--khi3-lai5, chiong i si3-ui5 sou2-u7-e5 it-chin7 sio-lio-khi3.
	33). Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kap Iu5-tai7 lang5 piN5-piN5 siu7 ap-che3; hoan7-na7 liah8-in--e5, long2 ka7 i kou3-tiau5-tiau5, m7-kheng2 pang3 i khi3.  34). Kiu3-siok8 in--e5 u7 toa7 khui3-lat8; I e5 mia5 si7 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I beh sin in e5 oan, hou7 choan5-toe7 tit-tioh8 peng5-an, iah8 hou7 Pa-pi2-lun5 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah.  35). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, U7 to-kiam3 lim5-kau3 Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5, kap Pa-pi2-lun5 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3, kap in e5 kui3-chok8, kap in e5 phok-su7.  36). U7 to-kiam3 lim5-kau3 khoa-khau2 e5 lang5, in chiu7 chiaN5-choe3 gong7; u7 to-kiam3 lim5-kau3 i e5 iong2-su7, in chiu7 kiaN-hiaN5.  37). U7 to-kiam3 lim5-kau3 i e5 be2, i e5 chhia, kap ki5-tiong e5 chap8-sek lang5; in beh chhin-chhiuN7 hu7-jin5-lang5 chit8-iuN7; u7 to-kiam3 lim5-kau3 i e5 po2-mih8, chiu7 siu7 chhiuN2-toat8.  38). U7 khong3-han7 lim5-kau3 i long2-chong2 e5 chui2, chiu7 beh ta-la--khi3; in-ui7 che si7 tiau-khek ngou2-siong7 e5 toe7, lang5 in-ui7 sin5-put8 lai5 tian-kong5.  39). Sou2-i2 khong3-ia2 e5 chau2-siu3 kap chhai5-long5 beh tiam3 ti7-hia; to-kiam3 iah8 beh tiam3 ti7 hit tiong-kan; eng2-eng2 bo5 jin5-ian, tai7-tai7 bo5 lang5 khia7.  40). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Tek-khak bo5 lang5 khia7-khi2 ti7-hia, iah8 bo5 lang5 kia3-kha ti7 in tiong-kan; beh chhin-chhiuN7 Goa2 Siong7-te3 chhia-to2 Sou2-to-ma2, Go5-mou5-lah8, kap hu7-kun7 e5 siaN5 chit8-iuN7.  41). KhoaN3 ah, u7 peh-siN3 tui3 pak-hng lai5; iah8 u7 toa7-kok kap choe7-choe7 kun-ong5 siu7 kek-tong7, tui3 toe7-kek8 lai5.  42). In kiah8 keng kap chhiuN, chan5-jim2 bo5 lin5-bin2; in e5 siaN chhin-chhiuN7 hai2-eng2 hoa7-hoa7-hau2; in khia5-be2 pai5-tui7, chhin-chhiuN7 chiuN7-tin7 e5 lang5; Pa-pi2-lun5 e5 siaN5 ah, in beh kong-kek li2.  43). Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 thiaN-kiN3 in e5 hong-siaN, chhiu2 chiu7 nng2--loh8-khi3; thong3-khou2 ka7 i khiN5-tiau5, thang3-thiaN3 chhin-chhiuN7 beh siN-kiaN2 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5.  44). KhoaN3 ah, i beh chhin-chhiuN7 sai tui3 Iok-tan3 ho5-piN e5 chhiu7-na5 khi2--lai5, kong-kek kian-kou3 khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7; bak8-nit-ku2, Goa2 beh hou7 in to5-chau2, li7-khui chit e5 sou2-chai7; chi7-chui7 siu7 keng2-soan2, Goa2 chiu7 phai3 i ti7-li2 chit e5 toe7; chi7-chui7 oe7 pi2--tit Goa2? chi7-chui7 oe7 ka7 Goa2 teng7 chit8 e5 ki5 ah? u7 sim2-mih8 bok8-chia2 oe7 khia7 ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5 ah?  45). Sou2-i2 lin2 tioh8 thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 ke3-ek8 kong-kek Pa-pi2-lun5 e5 ke3-chhek; i2-kip8 I sou2 chu3-tiaN7 kong-kek Ka-lek8-ti2 e5 chi2-i3.  In tiaN7-tioh8 beh chiong hiah e5 iuN5-kun5 e5 soe3--e5 thoa--khi3.  I ia7 beh hou7 in khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7 hong-hoe3.  46). In-ui7 Pa-pi2-lun5 to2-hoai7 e5 siaN, toe7 chiu7 tin2-tang7; in au5-kio3 e5 siaN thiaN ti7 liat8-pang tiong.

[51]	Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh khi2 hui2-biat8 e5 hong, kong-kek Pa-pi2-lun5, kap tiam3 ti7 Lip8-ka-bi2 e5 lang5.  2). Goa2 beh chhe goa7-pang lang5 lai5 kau3 Pa-pi2-lun5, lai5 poa3--in; hou7 in e5 toe7 khang-hu; ti7 i tu2-tioh8 hoan7-lan7 e5 jit8, in beh chiu-ui5 kong-kek i.  3). Khui-keng--e5 tioh8 ng3 khui-keng--e5 lai5 khui-keng, ng3 chheng7-kah theng2-sin--e5 lai5 khui-keng; boh8-tit sioh i e5 siau3-lian5 lang5, tioh8 it-chin7 biat8 i e5 choan5-kun.  4). Siu7-thai5--e5 beh to2 ti7 Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 e5 toe7; siu7-chhi3--e5 beh to2 ti7 i e5 koe-lou7.  5). Sui-bong2 I2-sek-liat8 kap Iu5-tai7, in e5 toe7-hng moa2-moa2 tek-choe7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 Seng3--e5, iau2-ku2 in bo5 hou7 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa i e5 Siong7-te3 khi3-sak in.  6). Lin2 tioh8 tui3 Pa-pi2-lun5 tiong chau2-chhut, tak8-lang5 kiu3 ka-ki7 e5 siN3-mia7; boh8-tit ti7 in e5 choe7-tiong lai5 biat8-bo5; in-ui7 che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa po3-siu5 e5 ki5, I beh hou7 in tu2-tioh8 eng-kai siu7 e5 po3-eng3.  7). Pa-pi2-lun5 peng5-sou3 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhiu2-lai7 e5 kim poe, hou7 choan5-toe7 e5 lang5 chui3; liat8-pang bat lim i e5 chiu2, sou2-i2 liat8-pang hoat-kong5.  8). Pa-pi2-lun5 hut-jian5 chhia-to2, hui2-hoai7; tioh8 ui7 i thi5-khau3, theh8 ju2-hiuN lai5 chi2 i e5 thang3-thiaN3, kiam2-chhai2 iau2 oe7-i-tit.  9). Lan2 siuN7 beh i-ti7 Pa-pi2-lun5, na7-si7 i bo5 tit-tioh8; lan2 tioh8 li7-khui i, tak8-lang5 to3-lai5 khi3 pun2-kok; in-ui7 i e5 choe7-an3 tu2-thiN, thau3 kau3 kiong-chhong.  10). Ia5-ho5-hoa i2-keng hian2-beng5 lan2 e5 kong-gi7; lai5 ah, lan2 thang ti7 Sek-an po3-ko3 lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 sou2-choe3.  11). Lin2 tioh8 boa5-kng lin2 e5 chiN3, gia5-tiau5 lin2 e5 tin5-pai5, Ia5-ho5-hoa tiaN7-tioh8 i3-su3 kong-kek Pa-pi2-lun5, lai5 hui2-biat8--i; sou2-i2 kek-tong7 Ma2-tai7 kun-ong5 e5 sim; in-ui7 che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa po3-siu5, chiu7-si7 I ui7-tioh8 I e5 tian7 lai5 po3-siu5.  12). Tioh8 khia7 toa7-ki5 kong-kek Pa-pi2-lun5 e5 siaN5-chhiuN5; tioh8 kian-kou3 liau5-bang7 e5 tai5, phai3 siu2-bang7-e5, siat bai5-hok8; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 kong2 lun7 Pa-pi2-lun5 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3, I u7 ke3-ek8 i, iah8 u7 chiaN5--i.  13). Khia7-khi2 ti7 choe7-choe7 chui2 e5 teng2-bin7, toa7 hoat-chai5--e5 ah, li2 e5 kiat-kiok8 kau3 lah, tham-sim e5 liong7 moa2 lah.  14). Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa ki2 ka-ki7 chiu3-choa7 kong2, Goa2 beh hou7 lang5 chhiong-moa2 lin2 tiong-kan, chhin-chhiuN7 chhau2-meh chit8-iuN7, in beh hoah-hiam3 kong-kek li2.
	15). Ia5-ho5-hoa eng7 leng5-lek8 chhong3-cho7 toe7, eng7 ti3-hui7 kian3-lip8 se3-kai3; eng7 chhang-mia5 tian2-khui chiah e5 thiN.  16). I chit8-e7 chhut-siaN, khong-tiong chiu7 u7 choe7-choe7 chui2 kek-tong7; I hou7 hun5-bu7 tui3 toe7-kek8 chheng3--khi2-lai5; I ui7-tioh8 hou7, chhong3-cho7 sih-na3; I hou7 hong tui3 I e5 hu2-khou3 chhut-lai5.  17). Tak8-lang5 long2 gu5-chhun2 bo5 ti3-sek; tak8 e5 gun5-chhiuN7 long2 ui7-tioh8 i tiau-khek e5 ngou2-siong7 lai5 kian3-siau3; in-ui7 i sou2 chu3 e5 ngou2-siong7 si7 ke2--e5, ia7 bo5 oah8-khi3 ti7 i e5 lai7-bin7.  18). Long2 si7 khang-khang--e5; si7 be5-hek8 lang5 e5 sou2-choe3; kau3 pan7-li2 in e5 si5, tek-khak siu7 tu5-biat8.  19). Nga2-kok e5 hun7-giah8 bo5 chhin-chhiuN7 chiah-e5; in-ui7 I si7 chhong3-cho7 ban7-mih8 e5 Chu2; I2-sek-liat8 ia7 si7 I san2-giap8 e5 chi-phai3; ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 I e5 mia5.
	20). Li2 si7 Goa2 e5 pou2-thau5, kau-chian3 e5 ke-si; Goa2 beh eng7 li2 phah-chhui3 liat8-pang, eng7 li2 hui2-biat8 liat8-kok;  21). eng7 li2 phah-chhui3 be2 kap khia5-be2-e5;  22). eng7 li2 phah-chhui3 chian3-chhia, kap che7 ti7 hi2 teng2-bin7--e5; eng7 li2 phah-chhui3 ta-pou-lang5 kap hu7-jin5-lang5; eng7 li2 phah-chhui3 lau7-lang5 kap gin2-a2;  23). eng7 li2 phah-chhui3 siau3-lian5 lang5 kap chai7-sek-lu2; eng7 li2 phah-chhui3 bok8-chia2 kap i e5 iuN5-kun5; eng7 li2 phah-chhui3 choh-chhan5 lang5, kap i e5 chit8-tui3 gu5; eng7 li2 phah-chhui3 chong2-tok kap koaN-oan5.  24). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Cha2 Pa-pi2-lun5 kap Ka-lek8-ti2 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3, ti7 Sek-an sou2 kiaN5 it-chhe3 e5 phaiN2, Goa2 beh po3-eng3 in, hou7 lin2 chhin-bak8 khoaN3-kiN3.
	25). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Li2 chit e5 kiaN5 hui2-biat8 e5 soaN ah, khoaN3 ah, Goa2 tui3-tek8 li2; li2 hui2-biat8 choan5-toe7, Goa2 beh chhun Goa2 e5 chhiu2 ti7 li2 e5 teng2-bin7, tui3 soaN-giam5 chhia li2 loh8--khi3; hou7 li2 chiaN5-choe3 sio-hui2 e5 soaN.  26). Lang5 tek-khak bo5 tui3 li2 hia chhu2 chit8 te3 chioh8 choe3 chhu3-kak, iah8 bo5 chit8 te3 chioh8 choe3 toe7-ki; li2 beh eng2-oan2 pha-hng; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  27). Tioh8 ti7 keng2-lai7 khia7 toa7-ki5, ti7 tak8-kok-tiong pun5 sau3-kak; tiau-ti5 pi7-pan7 liat8-kok lai5 kong-kek i; chio-chip8 A-lah8-lat8, Bi2-ni5, A-sit8-ki-na2 chiah e5 kok lai5 kong-kek i; koh phai3 kun-tiuN2 lai5 kong-kek i; hou7 be2-peng chiuN7-lai5 chhin-chhiuN7 chhou-mng5 e5 chhau2-meh.  28). Tiau-ti5 pi7-pan7 liat8-kok kap Ma2-tai7 e5 liat8-ong5, i e5 chong2-tok, i e5 koaN-oan5, kap i sou2 koan2 choan5-toe7 e5 lang5, lai5 kong-kek i.  29). Toe7 tin2-tang7 koh chhiN-chham2; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong-kek Pa-pi2-lun5 e5 chi2-i3 i2-keng tiaN7-tioh8; beh hou7 Pa-pi2-lun5 e5 toe7 pha-hng, bo5 lang5 khia7-khi2.  30). Pa-pi2-lun5 e5 iong2-su7 m7-ai3 kau-chian3, toa3 ti7 iaN5-poaN5-lai7; i e5 lat8 i2-keng bo5, chiaN5-choe3 chhin-chhiuN7 hu7-jin5-lang5, in e5 chhu3-theh8 siu7-sio, in e5 mng5-kong5 phah-chih8.  31). Chau2-bun5-su--e5 chau2-khi3 tu2-tioh8 chau2 bun5-su--e5; po3 siau-sit--e5 tu2-tioh8 po3 siau-sit--e5; po3-ko3 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 chai, i e5 siaN5 si3-bin7 hou7 lang5 chhu2-khi3;  32). lou7 thau5 hou7 lang5 chiam3-khi3, lou5-tek siu7 he2 sio, kau-chian3 e5 lang5 iah8 kiaN-hiaN5.
	33). Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3, an2-ni kong2: Pa-pi2-lun5 chhin-chhiuN7 chhek-tiaN5, i2-keng tah8 kau3 piN5-piN5; koh bo5 joa7-ku2, siu-seng5 e5 si5 chiu7 kau3.  34). Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat thun-chiah8 goa2, teh-chhui3 goa2; hou7 goa2 chiaN5-choe3 khang e5 khi3-ku7; i chhin-chhiuN7 toa7-hi5 thun goa2; eng7 goa2 e5 po2-mih8 chhiong-moa2 i e5 pak-tou2, koh chiong goa2 thou3-chhut.  35). Sek-an khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 beh kong2, Pa-pi2-lun5 eng7 po7-giok8 khoan2-thai7 goa2, kap goa2 e5 sin-the2; goan7 chit e5 choe7 kui ti7 i.  Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 lang5 beh kong2, Goan7 lau5 goan2 e5 huih e5 choe7 kui ti7 Ka-lek8-ti2 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3.  36). Sou2-i2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh thoe3 li2 sin-oan, iah8 beh thoe3 li2 po3-siu5; Goa2 beh hou7 i e5 hai2 ta--khi3, hou7 i e5 chui2-choaN5 bo5 chui2.  37). Pa-pi2-lun5 beh chiaN5-choe3 thou5-tui, choe3 ia2-kau2 toa3 e5 sou2-chai7; choe3 thang gong5-ngiah8, thang thi2-chhio3--e5, iah8 bo5 lang5 khia7-khi3.  38). In beh chhin-chhiuN7 iong2 e5 sai hm7-hm7-hau2, chhin-chhiuN7 soe3-chiah sai hau2-kio3.  39). Tng in jiat8 e5 si5, Goa2 beh ui7 in pan7 chiu2-toh, hou7 i chiu2-chui3, hou7 i khoai3-lok8, tng5 khun3, eng2 bo5 cheng-sin5; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  40). Goa2 beh toa3 in loh8--khi3, chhin-chhiuN7 iuN5-a2, chhin-chhiuN7 kang e5 mi5-iuN5, kang e5 soaN-iuN5, kau3 siu7-thai5 e5 toe7.  41). Si7-sa-khek chaiN2-iuN7 siu7 kong-phoa3! thiN-e7 sou2 o-lo2--e5, chaiN2-iuN7 siu7 pa3-chiam3! Pa-pi2-lun5 ti7 liat8-kok-tiong, chaiN2-iuN7 piN3-choe3 pha-hng!  42). Hai2-chui2 tiong3--khi2-lai5, im-ke3 Pa-pi2-lun5; i hou7 choe7-choe7 eng2 kham3-bat8.  43). I e5 siaN5 piN3-choe3 pha-hng, ta-so3 e5 toe7, soa-bou5, bo5 lang5 khia7-khi2, bo5 lang5 keng-ke3 e5 sou2-chai7.  44).
