Goa2 beh heng5-hoat8 Pi2-lek8 ti7 Pa-pi2-lun5, Goa2 beh ou2-chhut i e5 chhui3 sou2 thun e5; ban7 peh-siN3 bo5 koh kui-oa2 i; Pa-pi2-lun5 e5 siaN5-chhiuN5 iah8 to2-hoai7.
	45). Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 ah, lin2 tioh8 tui3 i e5 tiong-kan chhut-khi3; tak8-lang5 kiu3 ka-ki7, siam2-pi7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 toa7 siu7-khi3.  46). Lin2 e5 sim m7 thang sit-taN2, iah8 m7-thang in-ui7 keng2-lai7 sou2 thiaN-kiN3 e5 hong-siaN lai5 kiaN-hiaN5; in-ui7 kin-ni5 u7 hong-siaN thoan5-lai5, mi5--si5 iah8 u7 hong-siaN; keng2-lai7 u7 kiong5-po7 e5 su7, koaN-tiuN2 kong-kek koaN-tiuN2.  47). KhoaN3 ah, jit8-chi2 beh kau3, Goa2 beh pan7 Pa-pi2-lun5 tiau-khek e5 ngou2-siong7, hou7 in choan5-toe7 kian3-siau3; i hiah e5 siu7-thai5 e5 lang5 beh to2 ti7 in tiong-kan.  48). Hit-si5 thiN-toe7 kap ki5-tiong sou2 u7--e5, beh in-ui7 Pa-pi2-lun5 sit-pai7 lai5 hoaN-hi2; in-ui7 kiaN5 hui2-biat8--e5 beh tui3 pak-hng lai5 kau3 i hia; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  49). Pa-pi2-lun5 an3-chaiN2-iuN7 hou7 I2-sek-liat8 siu7-thai5 e5 lang5 to2--loh8-khi3, chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, i choan5-toe7 siu7-thai5 e5 lang5 iah8 beh ti7 Pa-pi2-lun5 to2--loh8-khi3.  50). Siam2-pi7 to-kiam3--e5 tioh8 kin2 chau2, m7-thang khia7--teh; tioh8 ti7 hng7-hng7 e5 sou2-chai7 ki3-liam7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, sim-lai7 tui-siuN7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2.  51). Goan2 in-ui7 thiaN loe2-me7 lau3-khui3, moa2-bin7 kian3-siau3; in-ui7 iN7-pang lang5 jip8 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3 hiah e5 seng3 e5 sou2-chai7.  52). Sou2-i2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, KhoaN3 ah, jit8-chi2 beh kau3, Goa2 pan7 Pa-pi2-lun5 tiau-khek e5 ngou2-siong7; thong-kok siu7-siong e5 lang5 beh hiN-hiN-chhan.  53). Pa-pi2-lun5 sui-jian5 chiuN7 kau3 thiN, sui-jian5 hou7 i kian-kou3 koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7 koh-khah kian-kou3; iau2-ku2 u7 kiaN5 hui2-biat8--e5 beh tui3 Goa2 chia kau3 i hia; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  54). Tui3 Pa-pi2-lun5 u7 ai-khau3 e5 siaN, tui3 Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 e5 toe7 u7 toa7 hui2-biat8 e5 siaN.  55). In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa hui2-biat8 Pa-pi2-lun5, hou7 in tiong-kan e5 toa7-siaN soah--khi3, in e5 eng2 hoa7-hoa7-hau2, chhin-chhiuN7 choe7-choe7 e5 chui2; i hiang2 e5 siaN iah8 hoat-chhut.  56). In-ui7 hui2-biat8--e5 lai5 kong-kek Pa-pi2-lun5; i e5 iong2-su7 siu7-liah8, in e5 keng tu2-tioh8 at-chih8; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 kiaN5 po3-eng3 e5 Siong7-te3, I koat-toan3 beh po3-siu5.  57). Kun-ong5, mia5 choe3 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa--e5, kong2, Goa2 beh hou7 i e5 kui3-chok8, phok-su7, chong2-tok, koaN-oan5, i2-kip8 iong2-su7, long2 chiu2-chui3, eng2-eng2 khun3, bo5 cheng-sin5.  58). Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2: Pa-pi2-lun5 khoah-toa7 e5 siaN5-chhiuN5 beh it-chin7 to2-hoai7; i koaiN5-toa7 e5 siaN5-mng5 beh hou7 he2 sio-lio--khi3; cheng3 peh-siN3 sou2 tioh8-boa5--e5 beh kui ti7 khang-khang; liat8-kok sou2 tioh8-boa5--e5 kui ti7 he2; in long2 beh ia3-sian7.
	59). Iu5-tai7 ong5 Se-ti2-ka che7-ui7 e5 te7-si3-ni5 chiuN7-khi3 Pa-pi2-lun5 e5 si5, Ma2-se-nga2 e5 sun, Ni5-li7-a e5 kiaN2 Se-lai5-nga2, kap ong5 saN-kap khi3.  60). (Se-lai5-nga2 si7 ong5 e5 loe7-si7) sian-ti Ia5-li7-bi2 u7 oe7 hoan-hu3 i.  Ia5-li7-bi2 chiong it-chhe3 beh lim5-kau3 Pa-pi2-lun5 e5 chai-e7, chiu7-si7 lun7-kau3 Pa-pi2-lun5 sou2 sia2 it-chhe3 e5 oe7, lai5 ki3-chiuN7-chheh.  61). Ia5-li7-bi2 tui3 Se-lai5-nga2 kong2, Li2 kau3 Pa-pi2-lun5 e5 si5, iau2-kin2 tioh8 thak8 chit e5 chheh--nih e5 oe7.  62). Koh tioh8 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 lun7-kau3 chit sou2-chai7 bat kong2 beh biat8--i, sim7-chi3 bo5 lang5 khia7-khi2, lian5 cheng-siN iah8 bo5, tek-khak eng2-oan2 pha-hng.  63). Li2 chit e5 chheh thak8-liau2, chiu7 tioh8 pak8 ti7 chit8 te3 chioh8-thau5, hiat-loh8 ti7 Pek-lat ho5 tiong,  64). kong2, Pa-pi2-lun5 ui7-tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beh kang3 hou7 i e5 chai-e7 tek-khak chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni tim5--loh8-khi3, boe7 koh khi2-lai5; in long2 beh ia3-sian7.
	Ia5-li7-bi2 e5 oe7, kau3 chia ui5-chi2.
[52]	Se-ti2-ka che7-ui7 e5 si5, ji7-chap8-it he3; ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 choe3 ong5 chap8-it ni5.  I e5 lau7-bu2 mia5 Hap-bou7-tha; si7 Lip8-na2 lang5 Ia5-li7-bi2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2.  2). I kiaN5 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 khoaN3-choe3 phaiN2 e5 su7; chiau3 Iok-nga2-keng3 it-chhe3 sou2 kiaN5--e5.  3). Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 kap Iu5-tai7 tu2-tioh8 chiah e5 su7, si7 in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa hoat-chhut siu7-khi3; beh tui3 I e5 bin7-cheng5 koaN2-chhut in; hit-si5 Se-ti2-ka poe7-poan7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5.  4). Tng Se-ti2-ka che7-ui7 te7-kau2 ni5, Chap8-geh8 chhoe-chap8, Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat chhoa7 i choan5-kun lai5 kong-kek Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, ti7 siaN5 e5 tui3-bin7 chat-iaN5, koh ti7 si3-ui5 choh thou5-tui kong-kek siaN5.  5). Tui3 an2-ni siaN5 siu7 ui5-khun3, tit8-kau3 Se-ti2-ka chap8-it ni5.  6). Si3-geh8 chhoe-kau2 jit8, siaN5-lai7 ki-hng chin siong-tiong7, ti3-kau3 hit sou2-chai7 e5 peh-siN3 long2 bo5 niu5.  7). SiaN5 siu7 kong-phoa3, it-chhe3 e5 peng-teng thau3-mi5 tui3 oa2-kun7 ong5 e5 hng5, nng7 e5 siaN5-chhiuN5 tiong e5 mng5, hit tiau5 lou7 chau2 chhut siaN5.  Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 tu2-tu2 ti7 si3-ui5 kong-kek siaN5, in chiu7 tui3 A-lah8-pa e5 lou7 to5-chau2.  8). Ka-lek8-ti2 e5 kun-peng tui-jip ong5, ti7 Ia5-li7-ko e5 piN5-iuN5 tui--tioh8 Se-ti2-ka; i e5 choan5-kun long2 li7-khui i si3-soaN3.  9). In liah8-tioh8 ong5, toa3 kau3 Hap-ma2 toe7 e5 Li7-pi2-lah8, Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 hia; Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 chiu7 sim2-phoaN3 i.  10). Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 ti7 Se-ti2-ka e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5, thai5-si2 i hiah e5 kiaN2, koh ti7 Li7-pi2-lah8 thai5 Iu5-tai7 it-chhe3 e5 kui3-chok8.  11). Koh iah Se-ti2-ka nng7-lui2 bak8-chiu, Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 eng7 thih-lian7 lian7--i, toa3 kau3 Pa-pi2-lun5, koaiN i ti7 kaN--nih, tit8-kau3 i si2 e5 jit8.
	12). Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat ong5 chap8-kau2 ni5, gou7-geh8 chhoe-chap8 jit8, kun-sui5 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 e5 si7-oe7-tiuN2 Ni5-pou3-sat-lah8-tan3 jip8 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2.  13). Eng7 he2 sio Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 tian7, kap ong5-kiong; koh eng7 he2 sio Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 it-chhe3 e5 chhu3, chiu7-si7 hu3-kui3-ke e5 chhu3.  14). Kun-te3 si7-oe7-tiuN2 Ka-lek8-ti2 e5 choan5-kun chiu7 thiah-hui2 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 si3-ui5 e5 siaN5-chhiuN5.  15). Hit-si5 si7-oe7-tiuN2 Ni5-pou3-sat-lah8-tan3 chiong bin5-kan song3-hiong--e5, kap lau5 ti7 siaN5-lai7 sou2 chhun e5 peh-siN3, kap hiah e5 tau5-hang5 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5--e5, i2-kip8 cheng3-lang5-tiong sou2 chhun--e5, long2 liah8-khi3.  16). Tok8-tok8 si7-oe7-tiuN2 Ni5-pou3-sat-lah8-tan3 lau5 hit e5 toe7-hng te7-it song3-hiong--e5, hou7 in ti7-li2 phu5-to5-hng5, kap cheng3-choh.  17). Ia5-ho5-hoa tian7-lai7 e5 tang5-thiau7, kap Ia5-ho5-hoa tian7-lai7 e5 phun5-cho7, i2-kip8 tang5-hai2, Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 long2 phah-phoa3, chiong hiah e5 tang5 un7 kau3 Pa-pi2-lun5.  18). Koh toa3-khi3 tiaN2, thuh-a2, chian2-to, poaN5, oaN2, kap sou2 eng7 it-chhe3 e5 tang5-khi3.  19). Poe, he2-lou5, poaN5, tiaN2, teng-tai5, oaN2, au, it-chhe3 kim-khi3 e5 kim, gun5-khi3 e5 gun5, si7-oe7-tiuN2 long2 toa3-khi3.  20). Koh toa3 Sou2-lo5-bun5 ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 tian7 sou2 chhong3 nng7 ki thiau7, chit8 e5 tang5-hai2 kap cho7-e7 chap8-ji7 chiah tang5-gu5, chiah e5 khi3-ku7 e5 tang5 boe7-oe7 chhin3 i e5 khin-tang7.  21). Chit8-ki thiau7 koaiN5 chap8-poeh tiu2, iN5-khoan5 chap8-ji7 tiu2, kau7 si3-chaiN2, tiong-ng khang-khak.  22). Thiau7 e5 teng2-bin7 u7 tang5 e5 thiau7-tau2, koaiN5 gou7 tiu2; thiau7-tau2 e5 chiu-ui5 u7 bang7-a2 kap siah8-liu5, long2 si7 tang5 choe3--e5; te7-ji7 ki thiau7 siang5 chit8-khoan2, iah8 u7 siah8-liu5.  23). Si3-bin7 u7 kau2-chap8-lak8 liap8 e5 siah8-liu5; ti7 bang7-a2 e5 chiu-ui5 kiong7 u7 chit8-pah liap8 siah8-liu5.  24). Si7-oe7-tiuN2 liah8 che3-si-thau5 Se-lai5-nga2, kap te7-ji7-kip e5 che3-si Se-hoan-a, kap saN e5 kou3-mng5--e5;  25). koh tui3 siaN5-lai7 liah8 chit8 e5 koan2-peng e5 koaN, kap ti7 siaN5-lai7 sou2 tu2-tioh8 siong5-siong5 kiN3 ong5 e5 bin7--e5 chhit-lang5, kap kun-tiuN2 e5 su-ki3, tiam2-sng3 peh-siN3--e5, i2-kip8 siaN5-tiong sou2 tu2-tioh8 e5 kok-bin5 lak8-chap8 lang5.  26). Si7-oe7-tiuN2 Ni5-pou3-sat-lah8-tan3 chiong chiah e5 lang5 toa3 kau3 Li7-pi2-lah8, Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 hia.  27). Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 phah--in, ti7 Hap-ma2 toe7 e5 Li7-pi2-lah8 thai5-si2 in; an2-ni Iu5-tai7 peh-siN3 siu7-liah8, li7-khui pun2-toe7.  28). Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat sou2 liah8 e5 jin5-sou3, ki3 ti7 e7-toe2; ti7 te7 chhit ni5, liah8 Iu5-tai7 lang5 saN-chheng lian5-ji7-chap8-saN lang5.  29). Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat chap8-poeh ni5, tui3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 liah8-khi3 poeh-pah saN-chap8-ji7 lang5.  30). Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat ji7-chap8-saN-ni5, si7-oe7-tiuN2 Ni5-pou3-sat-lah8-tan3 liah8--khi3 Iu5-tai7 lang5 chhit-pah si3-chap8-gou7 mia5; kiong7 u7 si3-chheng lak8-pah lang5.
	31). Iu5-tai7 ong5 Iok-nga2-kun siu7-liah8 liau2-au7, te7 saN-chap8-chhit--ni5, Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 I2-bi7-bi2-lo5-tat8 goan5--ni5, chap8-ji7-geh8 ji7-gou7 jit8, ku2-khi2 Iu5-tai7 ong5 Iok-nga2-kun, pang3 i chhut-kaN.  32). Iah8 eng7 ho2-oe7 an-ui3 i, hou7 i e5 ui7 khah-koaiN5 ki5-u5 chiah e5 ong5 e5 ui7, chiu7-si7 kap i tang5 ti7 Pa-pi2-lun5--e5.  33). Thng3--khi3 i kaN-lai7 sou2 chheng7 e5 saN, chit8-si3-lang5 kap Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 saN-kap chiah8.  34). Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 siuN2-su3 i sou2 khiam3-eng7 e5 sit8-but8, jit8-jit8 hou7 i chit8-hun7; kui-si3-lang5 si7 an2-ni, tit8-kau3 i si2 e5 jit8.
